Файл: main.py
Комментарий: Точка входа локального приложения.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: """
    2: Сравнение файлов
    3: 
    4: Главный файл запуска проекта для PyCharm.
    5: 
    6: Весь основной код приложения находится в папке:
    7:     src/file_compare_app/
    8: 
    9: Зачем так сделано:
   10:     - main.py остается простой точкой запуска;
   11:     - логика сравнения, интерфейс, отчеты и анализаторы лежат отдельно;
   12:     - проект проще тестировать и собирать в .exe.
   13: 
   14: Чтобы запустить приложение:
   15:     1. Откройте этот файл в PyCharm.
   16:     2. Нажмите зеленую кнопку Run.
   17: """
   18: 
   19: from __future__ import annotations
   20: 
   21: import sys
   22: from pathlib import Path
   23: 
   24: 
   25: PROJECT_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
   26: SOURCE_ROOT = PROJECT_ROOT / "src"
   27: 
   28: if str(SOURCE_ROOT) not in sys.path:
   29:     sys.path.insert(0, str(SOURCE_ROOT))
   30: 
   31: from file_compare_app.__main__ import main
   32: 
   33: 
   34: if __name__ == "__main__":
   35:     raise SystemExit(main())

Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\base.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
    2: from pathlib import Path
    3: 
    4: from file_compare_app.core.models import ComparisonResult
    5: 
    6: 
    7: class AnalyzerDependencyError(RuntimeError):
    8:     pass
    9: 
   10: 
   11: class Analyzer(ABC):
   12:     @abstractmethod
   13:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   14:         raise NotImplementedError

====================================================================================================
Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\binary.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer
    4: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
    5: 
    6: 
    7: class BinaryAnalyzer(Analyzer):
    8:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
    9:         left = left_path.read_bytes()
   10:         right = right_path.read_bytes()
   11:         changes: list[Change] = []
   12:         max_len = max(len(left), len(right))
   13:         change_index = 1
   14:         offset = 0
   15: 
   16:         while offset < max_len and change_index <= 200:
   17:             left_byte = left[offset : offset + 1]
   18:             right_byte = right[offset : offset + 1]
   19:             if left_byte == right_byte:
   20:                 offset += 1
   21:                 continue
   22: 
   23:             start = offset
   24:             before = bytearray()
   25:             after = bytearray()
   26:             while offset < max_len and left[offset : offset + 1] != right[offset : offset + 1]:
   27:                 before.extend(left[offset : offset + 1])
   28:                 after.extend(right[offset : offset + 1])
   29:                 offset += 1
   30: 
   31:             length = max(len(before), len(after))
   32:             changes.append(
   33:                 Change(
   34:                     change_id=f"binary-{change_index}",
   35:                     change_type="binary",
   36:                     severity="normal",
   37:                     source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), byte_offset=start, byte_length=length),
   38:                     target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), byte_offset=start, byte_length=length),
   39:                     before=bytes(before).hex(),
   40:                     after=bytes(after).hex(),
   41:                     format="hex",
   42:                     confidence=1.0,
   43:                     notes="byte range differs",
   44:                 )
   45:             )
   46:             change_index += 1
   47: 
   48:         return ComparisonResult(
   49:             left_path=str(left_path),
   50:             right_path=str(right_path),
   51:             file_kind="binary",
   52:             changes=changes,
   53:             metadata={"left_size": str(len(left)), "right_size": str(len(right))},
   54:         )

====================================================================================================
Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\docx.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer, AnalyzerDependencyError
    4: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
    5: from file_compare_app.core.text_diff import line_changes
    6: 
    7: 
    8: class DocxAnalyzer(Analyzer):
    9:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   10:         left_lines = _extract_docx_lines(left_path)
   11:         right_lines = _extract_docx_lines(right_path)
   12:         changes: list[Change] = []
   13:         for index, (kind, left_index, right_index, before, after) in enumerate(line_changes(left_lines, right_lines), start=1):
   14:             changes.append(
   15:                 Change(
   16:                     change_id=f"docx-{index}",
   17:                     change_type=kind,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
   18:                     severity="normal",
   19:                     source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), line=left_index + 1) if left_index is not None else None,
   20:                     target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), line=right_index + 1) if right_index is not None else None,
   21:                     before=before,
   22:                     after=after,
   23:                     format="docx",
   24:                     confidence=1.0,
   25:                     notes="paragraph/table text",
   26:                 )
   27:             )
   28:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), "docx", changes)
   29: 
   30: 
   31: def _extract_docx_lines(path: Path) -> list[str]:
   32:     try:
   33:         from docx import Document
   34:     except ModuleNotFoundError as exc:
   35:         raise AnalyzerDependencyError("Для сравнения DOCX установите python-docx.") from exc
   36: 
   37:     document = Document(path)
   38:     lines = [paragraph.text for paragraph in document.paragraphs if paragraph.text.strip()]
   39:     for table in document.tables:
   40:         for row in table.rows:
   41:             cells = [cell.text.strip() for cell in row.cells]
   42:             if any(cells):
   43:                 lines.append(" | ".join(cells))
   44:     return lines

Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\image.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer, AnalyzerDependencyError
    4: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
    5: 
    6: 
    7: class ImageAnalyzer(Analyzer):
    8:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
    9:         try:
   10:             from PIL import Image, ImageChops
   11:         except ModuleNotFoundError as exc:
   12:             raise AnalyzerDependencyError("Для сравнения изображений установите Pillow.") from exc
   13: 
   14:         left = Image.open(left_path).convert("RGB")
   15:         right = Image.open(right_path).convert("RGB")
   16:         diff = ImageChops.difference(left, right)
   17:         bbox = diff.getbbox()
   18:         changes: list[Change] = []
   19:         if bbox is not None:
   20:             x1, y1, x2, y2 = bbox
   21:             changes.append(
   22:                 Change(
   23:                     change_id="image-1",
   24:                     change_type="modified",
   25:                     severity="normal",
   26:                     source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), x=x1, y=y1, width=x2 - x1, height=y2 - y1),
   27:                     target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), x=x1, y=y1, width=x2 - x1, height=y2 - y1),
   28:                     before="image region differs",
   29:                     after="image region differs",
   30:                     format="image",
   31:                     confidence=1.0,
   32:                     notes="pixel difference",
   33:                 )
   34:             )
   35:         ocr_changes = _ocr_text_change(left_path, right_path)
   36:         changes.extend(ocr_changes)
   37:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), "image", changes)
   38: 
   39: 
   40: def _ocr_text_change(left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> list[Change]:
   41:     try:
   42:         import pytesseract
   43:         from PIL import Image
   44:     except ModuleNotFoundError:
   45:         return []
   46: 
   47:     try:
   48:         left_text = pytesseract.image_to_string(Image.open(left_path), lang="rus+eng").strip()
   49:         right_text = pytesseract.image_to_string(Image.open(right_path), lang="rus+eng").strip()
   50:     except Exception:
   51:         return []
   52:     if left_text == right_text:
   53:         return []
   54:     return [
   55:         Change(
   56:             change_id="image-ocr-1",
   57:             change_type="modified",
   58:             severity="warning",
   59:             source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path)),
   60:             target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path)),
   61:             before=left_text,
   62:             after=right_text,
   63:             format="ocr",
   64:             confidence=0.8,
   65:             notes="OCR text differs",
   66:         )
   67:     ]

====================================================================================================
Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\klp.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: import re
    4: import zlib
    5: from pathlib import Path
    6: 
    7: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer
    8: from file_compare_app.core.config_profiles import is_risky_change, normalize_lines_for_path, risk_note
    9: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
   10: 
   11: 
   12: KLP_MAGIC = b"kscpolfmn"
   13: KLPARBIN_MARKER = b"<!--KLPARBIN -->"
   14: TEXT_RE = re.compile(r"[A-Za-zА-Яа-я0-9_./+ :;=,()\\\-\[\]{}]{4,}")
   15: 
   16: 
   17: class KasperskyKlpAnalyzer(Analyzer):
   18:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   19:         left_lines = [line.text for line in normalize_lines_for_path(left_path, extract_klp_profile_lines(left_path))]
   20:         right_lines = [line.text for line in normalize_lines_for_path(right_path, extract_klp_profile_lines(right_path))]
   21:         changes = _profile_changes(
   22:             _parse_profile_lines(left_lines),
   23:             _parse_profile_lines(right_lines),
   24:             left_path,
   25:             right_path,
   26:         )
   27:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), "klp", changes)
   28: 
   29: 
   30: def extract_klp_profile_lines(path: Path) -> list[str]:
   31:     data = path.read_bytes()
   32:     zlib_positions = _find_all(data, b"ZLIB")
   33:     if KLP_MAGIC not in data[:32] and KLPARBIN_MARKER not in data and not zlib_positions:
   34:         return _extract_text_klp_lines(path, data)
   35:     strings = set(_extract_readable_strings(data))
   36:     for payload in _extract_raw_deflate_payloads(data, zlib_positions):
   37:         strings.update(_extract_readable_strings(payload))
   38: 
   39:     clean_values = sorted(_clean_string(value) for value in strings if _clean_string(value))
   40:     sections = sorted(value for value in clean_values if _looks_like_section(value))
   41:     marker_position = data.find(KLPARBIN_MARKER)
   42: 
   43:     lines = [
   44:         "format: Kaspersky KLP policy",
   45:         f"magic: {_detect_magic(data)}",
   46:         f"size_bytes: {len(data)}",
   47:         f"klparbin_marker: {'yes' if marker_position >= 0 else 'no'}",
   48:         f"zlib_blocks: {len(zlib_positions)}",
   49:     ]
   50:     if marker_position >= 0:
   51:         lines.append(f"klparbin_offset: {marker_position}")
   52: 
   53:     lines.append("[sections]")
   54:     lines.extend(f"section: {section}" for section in sections)
   55:     lines.append("[values]")
   56:     lines.extend(f"value: {value}" for value in clean_values)
   57:     return lines
   58: 
   59: 
   60: def _extract_text_klp_lines(path: Path, data: bytes) -> list[str]:
   61:     for encoding in ("utf-8-sig", "utf-8", "cp1251", "latin-1"):
   62:         try:
   63:             text = data.decode(encoding)
   64:             break
   65:         except UnicodeDecodeError:
   66:             continue
   67:     else:
   68:         text = data.decode(errors="replace")
   69:     lines = [
   70:         "format: Kaspersky KLP policy text",
   71:         "magic: text",
   72:         f"size_bytes: {len(data)}",
   73:         "[values]",
   74:     ]
   75:     lines.extend(line.strip() for line in text.splitlines() if line.strip())
   76:     if len(lines) == 4:
   77:         lines.append(f"value: {path.name}")
   78:     return lines
   79: 
   80: 
   81: def _detect_magic(data: bytes) -> str:
   82:     if KLP_MAGIC in data[:32]:
   83:         return KLP_MAGIC.decode("ascii")
   84:     return "unknown"
   85: 
   86: 
   87: def _find_all(data: bytes, needle: bytes) -> list[int]:
   88:     positions: list[int] = []
   89:     start = 0
   90:     while True:
   91:         position = data.find(needle, start)
   92:         if position < 0:
   93:             return positions
   94:         positions.append(position)
   95:         start = position + len(needle)
   96: 
   97: 
   98: def _extract_raw_deflate_payloads(data: bytes, zlib_positions: list[int]) -> list[bytes]:
   99:     payloads: list[bytes] = []
  100:     for position in zlib_positions:
  101:         compressed = data[position + 4 :]
  102:         try:
  103:             decompressor = zlib.decompressobj(-zlib.MAX_WBITS)
  104:             payload = decompressor.decompress(compressed, 2_000_000)
  105:         except zlib.error:
  106:             continue
  107:         if payload:
  108:             payloads.append(payload)
  109:     return payloads
  110: 
  111: 
  112: def _extract_readable_strings(data: bytes) -> list[str]:
  113:     strings: set[str] = set()
  114:     for offset in (0, 1):
  115:         text = data[offset:].decode("utf-16le", errors="ignore")
  116:         strings.update(_split_and_match(text))
  117:     text = data.decode("ascii", errors="ignore")
  118:     strings.update(value for value in _split_and_match(text) if value.startswith(("KL", "KLP")))
  119:     return sorted(value for value in strings if _is_profile_value(value))
  120: 
  121: 
  122: def _split_and_match(text: str) -> set[str]:
  123:     found: set[str] = set()
  124:     for part in re.split(r"[\x00\r\n\t]+", text):
  125:         found.update(TEXT_RE.findall(part))
  126:     return found
  127: 
  128: 
  129: def _is_profile_value(value: str) -> bool:
  130:     value = _clean_string(value)
  131:     if len(value) < 3 or len(value) > 120:
  132:         return False
  133:     lowered = value.lower()
  134:     if lowered == "hash":
  135:         return True
  136:     if value.startswith("."):
  137:         return True
  138:     if "section" in lowered:
  139:         return True
  140:     if re.fullmatch(r"\d+(?:\.\d+)+", value):
  141:         return True
  142:     if re.fullmatch(r"[A-Za-z0-9_./+\-=]{4,}", value):
  143:         return True
  144:     if re.fullmatch(r"[A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_./+\-= ]{3,}", value):
  145:         return True
  146:     return False
  147: 
  148: 
  149: def _clean_string(value: str) -> str:
  150:     return " ".join(value.replace("\x00", " ").split())
  151: 
  152: 
  153: def _looks_like_section(value: str) -> bool:
  154:     lowered = value.lower()
  155:     if lowered in {"hash", "zlib", "format"}:
  156:         return False
  157:     if re.fullmatch(r"[A-Za-z0-9+/]{12,}={0,2}", value):
  158:         return False
  159:     if re.fullmatch(r"\d+(?:\.\d+)+", value):
  160:         return False
  161:     if len(value) > 90:
  162:         return False
  163:     return any(character.isalpha() for character in value) and (
  164:         value.startswith(".") or value[:1].isupper() or "section" in lowered
  165:     )
  166: 
  167: 
  168: def _parse_profile_lines(lines: list[str]) -> dict[str, object]:
  169:     metadata: dict[str, str] = {}
  170:     sections: set[str] = set()
  171:     values: set[str] = set()
  172:     mode = "metadata"
  173:     for line in lines:
  174:         if line == "[sections]":
  175:             mode = "sections"
  176:             continue
  177:         if line == "[values]":
  178:             mode = "values"
  179:             continue
  180:         if mode == "sections" and line.startswith("section: "):
  181:             sections.add(line.removeprefix("section: "))
  182:             continue
  183:         if mode == "values":
  184:             values.add(line.removeprefix("value: ") if line.startswith("value: ") else line)
  185:             continue
  186:         if ": " in line:
  187:             key, value = line.split(": ", 1)
  188:             metadata[key] = value
  189:     return {"metadata": metadata, "sections": sections, "values": values}
  190: 
  191: 
  192: def _profile_changes(
  193:     left_profile: dict[str, object],
  194:     right_profile: dict[str, object],
  195:     left_path: Path,
  196:     right_path: Path,
  197: ) -> list[Change]:
  198:     changes: list[Change] = []
  199:     _append_set_change(
  200:         changes,
  201:         left_profile["sections"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  202:         right_profile["sections"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  203:         left_path,
  204:         right_path,
  205:         "Секции",
  206:         "KLP sections",
  207:     )
  208:     _append_set_change(
  209:         changes,
  210:         left_profile["values"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  211:         right_profile["values"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  212:         left_path,
  213:         right_path,
  214:         "Значения",
  215:         "KLP values",
  216:     )
  217:     _append_metadata_change(
  218:         changes,
  219:         left_profile["metadata"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  220:         right_profile["metadata"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  221:         left_path,
  222:         right_path,
  223:     )
  224:     return changes
  225: 
  226: 
  227: def _append_set_change(
  228:     changes: list[Change],
  229:     left_values: set[str],
  230:     right_values: set[str],
  231:     left_path: Path,
  232:     right_path: Path,
  233:     title: str,
  234:     notes: str,
  235: ) -> None:
  236:     removed = sorted(left_values - right_values)
  237:     added = sorted(right_values - left_values)
  238:     if not removed and not added:
  239:         return
  240:     change_type = "modified" if removed and added else "removed" if removed else "added"
  241:     before_text = f"{title} удалены ({len(removed)}): {_sample_values(removed)}" if removed else ""
  242:     after_text = f"{title} добавлены ({len(added)}): {_sample_values(added)}" if added else ""
  243:     risky = is_risky_change(before_text, after_text, notes)
  244:     changes.append(
  245:         Change(
  246:             change_id=f"klp-{len(changes) + 1}",
  247:             change_type=change_type,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  248:             severity="risk" if risky else "normal",
  249:             source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), line=1) if removed else None,
  250:             target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), line=1) if added else None,
  251:             before=before_text,
  252:             after=after_text,
  253:             format="klp",
  254:             confidence=0.92,
  255:             notes=f"{notes}; {risk_note(before_text, after_text, notes)}" if risky else notes,
  256:         )
  257:     )
  258: 
  259: 
  260: def _append_metadata_change(
  261:     changes: list[Change],
  262:     left_metadata: dict[str, str],
  263:     right_metadata: dict[str, str],
  264:     left_path: Path,
  265:     right_path: Path,
  266: ) -> None:
  267:     changed_keys = sorted(key for key in set(left_metadata) | set(right_metadata) if left_metadata.get(key) != right_metadata.get(key))
  268:     if not changed_keys:
  269:         return
  270:     changes.append(
  271:         Change(
  272:             change_id=f"klp-{len(changes) + 1}",
  273:             change_type="modified",
  274:             severity="low",
  275:             source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), line=1),
  276:             target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), line=1),
  277:             before="; ".join(f"{key}: {left_metadata.get(key, '-')}" for key in changed_keys),
  278:             after="; ".join(f"{key}: {right_metadata.get(key, '-')}" for key in changed_keys),
  279:             format="klp",
  280:             confidence=0.9,
  281:             notes="KLP technical metadata",
  282:         )
  283:     )
  284: 
  285: 
  286: def _sample_values(values: list[str], limit: int = 3, max_length: int = 96) -> str:
  287:     if not values:
  288:         return "-"
  289:     sample = values[:limit]
  290:     suffix = f"; еще {len(values) - limit}" if len(values) > limit else ""
  291:     text = "; ".join(sample) + suffix
  292:     if len(text) <= max_length:
  293:         return text
  294:     return text[: max_length - 1].rstrip() + "…"

Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\pdf.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer, AnalyzerDependencyError
    4: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
    5: from file_compare_app.core.text_diff import line_changes
    6: 
    7: 
    8: class PdfAnalyzer(Analyzer):
    9:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   10:         left_lines = _extract_pdf_lines(left_path)
   11:         right_lines = _extract_pdf_lines(right_path)
   12:         changes: list[Change] = []
   13:         for index, (kind, left_index, right_index, before, after) in enumerate(line_changes(left_lines, right_lines), start=1):
   14:             changes.append(
   15:                 Change(
   16:                     change_id=f"pdf-{index}",
   17:                     change_type=kind,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
   18:                     severity="normal",
   19:                     source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), line=left_index + 1) if left_index is not None else None,
   20:                     target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), line=right_index + 1) if right_index is not None else None,
   21:                     before=before,
   22:                     after=after,
   23:                     format="pdf",
   24:                     confidence=0.9,
   25:                     notes="text layer or OCR",
   26:                 )
   27:             )
   28:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), "pdf", changes)
   29: 
   30: 
   31: def _extract_pdf_lines(path: Path) -> list[str]:
   32:     try:
   33:         import fitz
   34:     except ModuleNotFoundError as exc:
   35:         raise AnalyzerDependencyError("Для сравнения PDF установите PyMuPDF.") from exc
   36: 
   37:     document = fitz.open(path)
   38:     lines: list[str] = []
   39:     for page_number, page in enumerate(document, start=1):
   40:         text = page.get_text("text").strip()
   41:         if not text:
   42:             text = _ocr_page(page)
   43:         for raw_line in text.splitlines():
   44:             line = raw_line.strip()
   45:             if line:
   46:                 lines.append(f"page {page_number}: {line}")
   47:     return lines
   48: 
   49: 
   50: def _ocr_page(page: object) -> str:
   51:     try:
   52:         import fitz
   53:         import pytesseract
   54:         from PIL import Image
   55:     except ModuleNotFoundError as exc:
   56:         raise AnalyzerDependencyError("Для OCR установите pytesseract, Pillow и Tesseract OCR rus+eng.") from exc
   57: 
   58:     pix = page.get_pixmap(matrix=fitz.Matrix(2, 2), alpha=False)
   59:     image = Image.frombytes("RGB", [pix.width, pix.height], pix.samples)
   60:     return pytesseract.image_to_string(image, lang="rus+eng")

Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\text_config.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: import configparser
    4: import json
    5: import tomllib
    6: import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
    7: from pathlib import Path
    8: from typing import Any
    9: 
   10: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer
   11: from file_compare_app.core.config_profiles import is_risky_change, normalize_lines_for_path, risk_note
   12: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
   13: from file_compare_app.core.text_diff import line_changes
   14: 
   15: 
   16: CONFIG_SUFFIXES = {".json", ".yaml", ".yml", ".toml", ".ini", ".cfg", ".conf", ".env", ".properties", ".xml"}
   17: 
   18: 
   19: class TextConfigAnalyzer(Analyzer):
   20:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   21:         suffix = left_path.suffix.lower()
   22:         if suffix == ".json" and right_path.suffix.lower() == ".json":
   23:             return self._compare_mapping(left_path, right_path, _load_json(left_path), _load_json(right_path), "json")
   24:         if suffix == ".toml" and right_path.suffix.lower() == ".toml":
   25:             return self._compare_mapping(left_path, right_path, _load_toml(left_path), _load_toml(right_path), "toml")
   26:         if suffix in {".yaml", ".yml"} and right_path.suffix.lower() in {".yaml", ".yml"}:
   27:             left_data = _load_yaml(left_path)
   28:             right_data = _load_yaml(right_path)
   29:             if left_data is not None and right_data is not None:
   30:                 return self._compare_mapping(left_path, right_path, left_data, right_data, "yaml")
   31:         if suffix in {".ini", ".cfg"} and right_path.suffix.lower() in {".ini", ".cfg"}:
   32:             left_ini = _try_load_ini(left_path)
   33:             right_ini = _try_load_ini(right_path)
   34:             if left_ini is not None and right_ini is not None:
   35:                 return self._compare_mapping(left_path, right_path, left_ini, right_ini, "ini")
   36:             return self._compare_lines(left_path, right_path)
   37:         if suffix in {".env", ".properties"} and right_path.suffix.lower() in {".env", ".properties"}:
   38:             return self._compare_mapping(left_path, right_path, _load_key_value(left_path), _load_key_value(right_path), suffix.lstrip("."))
   39:         if suffix == ".xml" and right_path.suffix.lower() == ".xml":
   40:             return self._compare_mapping(left_path, right_path, _load_xml(left_path), _load_xml(right_path), "xml")
   41:         return self._compare_lines(left_path, right_path)
   42: 
   43:     def _compare_lines(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   44:         left_profile_lines = normalize_lines_for_path(left_path, _read_text(left_path).splitlines())
   45:         right_profile_lines = normalize_lines_for_path(right_path, _read_text(right_path).splitlines())
   46:         left_lines = [line.text for line in left_profile_lines]
   47:         right_lines = [line.text for line in right_profile_lines]
   48:         changes: list[Change] = []
   49:         for index, (kind, left_index, right_index, before, after) in enumerate(line_changes(left_lines, right_lines), start=1):
   50:             left_line_number = left_profile_lines[left_index].line_number if left_index is not None else None
   51:             right_line_number = right_profile_lines[right_index].line_number if right_index is not None else None
   52:             risky = is_risky_change(before, after)
   53:             notes = "line diff"
   54:             if risky:
   55:                 notes = f"{notes}; {risk_note(before, after)}"
   56:             changes.append(
   57:                 Change(
   58:                     change_id=f"text-{index}",
   59:                     change_type=kind,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
   60:                     severity="risk" if risky else "normal",
   61:                     source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), line=left_line_number) if left_line_number is not None else None,
   62:                     target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), line=right_line_number) if right_line_number is not None else None,
   63:                     before=before,
   64:                     after=after,
   65:                     format="text",
   66:                     confidence=1.0,
   67:                     notes=notes,
   68:                 )
   69:             )
   70:         file_kind = "config" if left_path.suffix.lower() in CONFIG_SUFFIXES or left_path.name.lower() in {"dockerfile", ".gitignore"} else "text"
   71:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), file_kind, changes)
   72: 
   73:     def _compare_mapping(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path, left_data: Any, right_data: Any, format_name: str) -> ComparisonResult:
   74:         changes: list[Change] = []
   75:         for index, (key_path, before, after, change_type) in enumerate(_diff_values(left_data, right_data), start=1):
   76:             before_text = "" if before is None else str(before)
   77:             after_text = "" if after is None else str(after)
   78:             risky = is_risky_change(before_text, after_text, key_path)
   79:             changes.append(
   80:                 Change(
   81:                     change_id=f"{format_name}-{index}",
   82:                     change_type=change_type,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
   83:                     severity="risk" if risky else "normal",
   84:                     source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path)),
   85:                     target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path)),
   86:                     before=before_text,
   87:                     after=after_text,
   88:                     format=format_name,
   89:                     confidence=1.0,
   90:                     notes=f"{key_path}; {risk_note(before_text, after_text, key_path)}" if risky else key_path,
   91:                 )
   92:             )
   93:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), "config", changes)
   94: 
   95: 
   96: def _read_text(path: Path) -> str:
   97:     for encoding in ("utf-8-sig", "utf-8", "cp1251", "latin-1"):
   98:         try:
   99:             return path.read_text(encoding=encoding)
  100:         except UnicodeDecodeError:
  101:             continue
  102:     return path.read_text(errors="replace")
  103: 
  104: 
  105: def _load_json(path: Path) -> Any:
  106:     return json.loads(_read_text(path))
  107: 
  108: 
  109: def _load_toml(path: Path) -> Any:
  110:     return tomllib.loads(_read_text(path))
  111: 
  112: 
  113: def _load_yaml(path: Path) -> Any | None:
  114:     try:
  115:         import yaml
  116:     except ModuleNotFoundError:
  117:         return None
  118:     return yaml.safe_load(_read_text(path))
  119: 
  120: 
  121: def _load_ini(path: Path) -> dict[str, dict[str, str]]:
  122:     parser = configparser.ConfigParser()
  123:     parser.read_string(_read_text(path))
  124:     return {section: dict(parser.items(section)) for section in parser.sections()}
  125: 
  126: 
  127: def _try_load_ini(path: Path) -> dict[str, dict[str, str]] | None:
  128:     try:
  129:         return _load_ini(path)
  130:     except configparser.Error:
  131:         return None
  132: 
  133: 
  134: def _load_key_value(path: Path) -> dict[str, str]:
  135:     values: dict[str, str] = {}
  136:     for line in _read_text(path).splitlines():
  137:         stripped = line.strip()
  138:         if not stripped or stripped.startswith("#") or "=" not in stripped:
  139:             continue
  140:         key, value = stripped.split("=", 1)
  141:         values[key.strip()] = value.strip()
  142:     return values
  143: 
  144: 
  145: def _load_xml(path: Path) -> dict[str, str]:
  146:     root = ET.fromstring(_read_text(path))
  147:     values: dict[str, str] = {}
  148: 
  149:     def walk(node: ET.Element, prefix: str) -> None:
  150:         current = f"{prefix}.{node.tag}" if prefix else node.tag
  151:         text = (node.text or "").strip()
  152:         if text:
  153:             values[current] = text
  154:         for key, value in sorted(node.attrib.items()):
  155:             values[f"{current}.@{key}"] = value
  156:         for child in node:
  157:             walk(child, current)
  158: 
  159:     walk(root, "")
  160:     return values
  161: 
  162: 
  163: def _diff_values(left: Any, right: Any, prefix: str = "") -> list[tuple[str, Any, Any, str]]:
  164:     if isinstance(left, dict) and isinstance(right, dict):
  165:         changes: list[tuple[str, Any, Any, str]] = []
  166:         for key in sorted(set(left) | set(right), key=str):
  167:             key_path = f"{prefix}.{key}" if prefix else str(key)
  168:             if key not in left:
  169:                 changes.append((key_path, None, right[key], "added"))
  170:             elif key not in right:
  171:                 changes.append((key_path, left[key], None, "removed"))
  172:             else:
  173:                 changes.extend(_diff_values(left[key], right[key], key_path))
  174:         return changes
  175:     if left != right:
  176:         return [(prefix, left, right, "modified")]
  177:     return []

Файл: src\file_compare_app\analyzers\xlsx.py
Комментарий: Анализаторы типов файлов и логика поиска изменений.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer, AnalyzerDependencyError
    4: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
    5: 
    6: 
    7: class XlsxAnalyzer(Analyzer):
    8:     def compare(self, left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
    9:         try:
   10:             from openpyxl import load_workbook
   11:         except ModuleNotFoundError as exc:
   12:             raise AnalyzerDependencyError("Для сравнения Excel установите openpyxl.") from exc
   13: 
   14:         left_wb = load_workbook(left_path, data_only=False)
   15:         right_wb = load_workbook(right_path, data_only=False)
   16:         changes: list[Change] = []
   17:         index = 1
   18:         for sheet_name in sorted(set(left_wb.sheetnames) | set(right_wb.sheetnames)):
   19:             if sheet_name not in left_wb.sheetnames:
   20:                 changes.append(_sheet_change(index, left_path, right_path, sheet_name, "", "sheet added", "added"))
   21:                 index += 1
   22:                 continue
   23:             if sheet_name not in right_wb.sheetnames:
   24:                 changes.append(_sheet_change(index, left_path, right_path, sheet_name, "sheet removed", "", "removed"))
   25:                 index += 1
   26:                 continue
   27:             left_ws = left_wb[sheet_name]
   28:             right_ws = right_wb[sheet_name]
   29:             max_row = max(left_ws.max_row, right_ws.max_row)
   30:             max_col = max(left_ws.max_column, right_ws.max_column)
   31:             for row in range(1, max_row + 1):
   32:                 for col in range(1, max_col + 1):
   33:                     left_cell = left_ws.cell(row=row, column=col)
   34:                     right_cell = right_ws.cell(row=row, column=col)
   35:                     if left_cell.value == right_cell.value:
   36:                         continue
   37:                     changes.append(
   38:                         Change(
   39:                             change_id=f"xlsx-{index}",
   40:                             change_type="modified",
   41:                             severity="normal",
   42:                             source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), sheet=sheet_name, cell=left_cell.coordinate),
   43:                             target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), sheet=sheet_name, cell=right_cell.coordinate),
   44:                             before="" if left_cell.value is None else str(left_cell.value),
   45:                             after="" if right_cell.value is None else str(right_cell.value),
   46:                             format="xlsx",
   47:                             confidence=1.0,
   48:                             notes=f"{sheet_name}!{right_cell.coordinate}",
   49:                         )
   50:                     )
   51:                     index += 1
   52:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), "xlsx", changes)
   53: 
   54: 
   55: def _sheet_change(index: int, left_path: Path, right_path: Path, sheet: str, before: str, after: str, change_type: str) -> Change:
   56:     return Change(
   57:         change_id=f"xlsx-{index}",
   58:         change_type=change_type,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
   59:         severity="normal",
   60:         source_location=ChangeLocation(str(left_path), sheet=sheet),
   61:         target_location=ChangeLocation(str(right_path), sheet=sheet),
   62:         before=before,
   63:         after=after,
   64:         format="xlsx",
   65:         confidence=1.0,
   66:         notes=sheet,
   67:     )

====================================================================================================
Файл: src\file_compare_app\core\config_profiles.py
Комментарий: Общие модели, профили нормализации, маршрутизация сравнения.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: import re
    4: from dataclasses import dataclass
    5: from pathlib import Path
    6: 
    7: 
    8: @dataclass(frozen=True)
    9: class NormalizedLine:
   10:     text: str
   11:     original: str
   12:     line_number: int
   13: 
   14: 
   15: SERVICE_LINE_PATTERNS = [
   16:     re.compile(r"^\s*cryptochecksum\s*:", re.IGNORECASE),
   17:     re.compile(r"^\s*:?\s*saved\s*$", re.IGNORECASE),
   18:     re.compile(r"^\s*:?\s*written by .+ at .+", re.IGNORECASE),
   19:     re.compile(r"^\s*(generated|created|exported)\s+(at|on|by)\b", re.IGNORECASE),
   20:     re.compile(r"^\s*(last[-_ ]?modified|timestamp|date|time)\s*[:=]", re.IGNORECASE),
   21:     re.compile(r"^\s*(size_bytes|klparbin_offset|zlib_blocks|magic|format)\s*:", re.IGNORECASE),
   22:     re.compile(r"^\s*#\s*(generated|saved|written)\b", re.IGNORECASE),
   23: ]
   24: 
   25: RISK_PATTERNS = [
   26:     re.compile(r"\baccess-list\b|\bacl\b|\bfirewall\b", re.IGNORECASE),
   27:     re.compile(r"\bpermit\b|\bdeny\b|\boutside_in\b|\binside_in\b", re.IGNORECASE),
   28:     re.compile(r"\binterface\b|\broute\b|\bgateway\b|\bnat\b", re.IGNORECASE),
   29:     re.compile(r"\bpassword\b|\bpasswd\b|\bsecret\b|\bencrypt", re.IGNORECASE),
   30:     re.compile(r"\bdisable(?:d)?\b|\boff\b|\bprotection\b|\bkaspersky\b|\bklprss\b", re.IGNORECASE),
   31: ]
   32: 
   33: 
   34: def normalize_lines_for_path(path: Path, lines: list[str]) -> list[NormalizedLine]:
   35:     return [
   36:         normalized
   37:         for line_number, line in enumerate(lines, start=1)
   38:         if (normalized := normalize_line(path, line, line_number)) is not None
   39:     ]
   40: 
   41: 
   42: def normalize_line(path: Path, line: str, line_number: int) -> NormalizedLine | None:
   43:     stripped = " ".join(line.strip().split())
   44:     if not stripped:
   45:         return None
   46:     if _is_service_line(path, stripped):
   47:         return None
   48:     return NormalizedLine(text=stripped, original=line, line_number=line_number)
   49: 
   50: 
   51: def is_risky_change(before: str, after: str, notes: str = "") -> bool:
   52:     haystack = f"{before}\n{after}\n{notes}"
   53:     return any(pattern.search(haystack) for pattern in RISK_PATTERNS)
   54: 
   55: 
   56: def risk_note(before: str, after: str, notes: str = "") -> str:
   57:     return "risk rule: critical config keyword" if is_risky_change(before, after, notes) else ""
   58: 
   59: 
   60: def _is_service_line(path: Path, stripped: str) -> bool:
   61:     suffix = path.suffix.lower()
   62:     if any(pattern.search(stripped) for pattern in SERVICE_LINE_PATTERNS):
   63:         return True
   64:     if suffix in {".klp", ".cfg", ".conf"} and re.match(r"^\s*!?\s*$", stripped):
   65:         return True
   66:     return False

Файл: src\file_compare_app\core\models.py
Комментарий: Общие модели, профили нормализации, маршрутизация сравнения.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    4: from typing import Literal
    5: 
    6: 
    7: ChangeType = Literal["added", "removed", "modified", "moved", "metadata", "binary"]
    8: Severity = Literal["info", "normal", "warning", "risk"]
    9: 
   10: 
   11: @dataclass(frozen=True)
   12: class ChangeLocation:
   13:     path: str
   14:     line: int | None = None
   15:     column: int | None = None
   16:     page: int | None = None
   17:     ocr_line: int | None = None
   18:     sheet: str | None = None
   19:     cell: str | None = None
   20:     byte_offset: int | None = None
   21:     byte_length: int | None = None
   22:     x: int | None = None
   23:     y: int | None = None
   24:     width: int | None = None
   25:     height: int | None = None
   26: 
   27:     def display(self) -> str:
   28:         if self.sheet and self.cell:
   29:             return f"{self.path} {self.sheet}!{self.cell}"
   30:         if self.page is not None and self.ocr_line is not None:
   31:             return f"{self.path} page {self.page} OCR line {self.ocr_line}"
   32:         if self.page is not None:
   33:             return f"{self.path} page {self.page}"
   34:         if self.line is not None and self.column is not None:
   35:             return f"{self.path}:{self.line}:{self.column}"
   36:         if self.line is not None:
   37:             return f"{self.path}:{self.line}"
   38:         if self.byte_offset is not None and self.byte_length is not None:
   39:             end = self.byte_offset + self.byte_length
   40:             return f"{self.path} bytes {self.byte_offset}-{end}"
   41:         if self.x is not None and self.y is not None and self.width is not None and self.height is not None:
   42:             return f"{self.path} region {self.x},{self.y},{self.width}x{self.height}"
   43:         return self.path
   44: 
   45: 
   46: @dataclass(frozen=True)
   47: class Change:
   48:     change_id: str
   49:     change_type: ChangeType
   50:     severity: Severity
   51:     source_location: ChangeLocation | None
   52:     target_location: ChangeLocation | None
   53:     before: str
   54:     after: str
   55:     format: str
   56:     confidence: float
   57:     notes: str = ""
   58: 
   59: 
   60: @dataclass(frozen=True)
   61: class ComparisonResult:
   62:     left_path: str
   63:     right_path: str
   64:     file_kind: str
   65:     changes: list[Change] = field(default_factory=list)
   66:     metadata: dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)
   67: 
   68:     @property
   69:     def change_count(self) -> int:
   70:         return len(self.changes)
   71: 
   72:     @property
   73:     def has_changes(self) -> bool:
   74:         return bool(self.changes)

Файл: src\file_compare_app\core\orchestrator.py
Комментарий: Общие модели, профили нормализации, маршрутизация сравнения.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import Analyzer
    4: from file_compare_app.analyzers.binary import BinaryAnalyzer
    5: from file_compare_app.analyzers.docx import DocxAnalyzer
    6: from file_compare_app.analyzers.image import ImageAnalyzer
    7: from file_compare_app.analyzers.klp import KasperskyKlpAnalyzer
    8: from file_compare_app.analyzers.pdf import PdfAnalyzer
    9: from file_compare_app.analyzers.text_config import TextConfigAnalyzer
   10: from file_compare_app.analyzers.xlsx import XlsxAnalyzer
   11: from file_compare_app.core.models import ComparisonResult
   12: from file_compare_app.core.type_detection import detect_file_kind
   13: 
   14: 
   15: def build_analyzer(file_kind: str) -> Analyzer:
   16:     if file_kind in {"text", "config"}:
   17:         return TextConfigAnalyzer()
   18:     if file_kind == "docx":
   19:         return DocxAnalyzer()
   20:     if file_kind == "pdf":
   21:         return PdfAnalyzer()
   22:     if file_kind == "xlsx":
   23:         return XlsxAnalyzer()
   24:     if file_kind == "image":
   25:         return ImageAnalyzer()
   26:     if file_kind == "klp":
   27:         return KasperskyKlpAnalyzer()
   28:     return BinaryAnalyzer()
   29: 
   30: 
   31: def compare_files(left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   32:     left_kind = detect_file_kind(left_path)
   33:     right_kind = detect_file_kind(right_path)
   34:     file_kind = left_kind if left_kind == right_kind else "binary"
   35:     analyzer = build_analyzer(file_kind)
   36:     return analyzer.compare(left_path, right_path)

Файл: src\file_compare_app\core\text_diff.py
Комментарий: Общие модели, профили нормализации, маршрутизация сравнения.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: from collections import Counter
    4: from difflib import SequenceMatcher
    5: 
    6: 
    7: LineChange = tuple[str, int | None, int | None, str, str]
    8: MIN_MODIFIED_SIMILARITY = 0.35
    9: 
   10: 
   11: def line_changes(left_lines: list[str], right_lines: list[str]) -> list[LineChange]:
   12:     return _patience_line_changes(left_lines, right_lines, 0, 0)
   13: 
   14: 
   15: def _patience_line_changes(
   16:     left_lines: list[str],
   17:     right_lines: list[str],
   18:     left_offset: int,
   19:     right_offset: int,
   20: ) -> list[LineChange]:
   21:     anchors = _unique_lcs_anchors(left_lines, right_lines)
   22:     if not anchors:
   23:         return _sequence_line_changes(left_lines, right_lines, left_offset, right_offset)
   24: 
   25:     changes: list[LineChange] = []
   26:     previous_left = 0
   27:     previous_right = 0
   28:     for left_index, right_index in anchors:
   29:         changes.extend(
   30:             _patience_line_changes(
   31:                 left_lines[previous_left:left_index],
   32:                 right_lines[previous_right:right_index],
   33:                 left_offset + previous_left,
   34:                 right_offset + previous_right,
   35:             )
   36:         )
   37:         previous_left = left_index + 1
   38:         previous_right = right_index + 1
   39:     changes.extend(
   40:         _patience_line_changes(
   41:             left_lines[previous_left:],
   42:             right_lines[previous_right:],
   43:             left_offset + previous_left,
   44:             right_offset + previous_right,
   45:         )
   46:     )
   47:     return changes
   48: 
   49: 
   50: def _sequence_line_changes(
   51:     left_lines: list[str],
   52:     right_lines: list[str],
   53:     left_offset: int,
   54:     right_offset: int,
   55: ) -> list[LineChange]:
   56:     matcher = SequenceMatcher(a=left_lines, b=right_lines, autojunk=False)
   57:     changes: list[LineChange] = []
   58:     for tag, i1, i2, j1, j2 in matcher.get_opcodes():
   59:         if tag == "equal":
   60:             continue
   61:         if tag == "replace":
   62:             max_len = max(i2 - i1, j2 - j1)
   63:             for offset in range(max_len):
   64:                 local_left_index = i1 + offset if i1 + offset < i2 else None
   65:                 local_right_index = j1 + offset if j1 + offset < j2 else None
   66:                 before = left_lines[local_left_index] if local_left_index is not None else ""
   67:                 after = right_lines[local_right_index] if local_right_index is not None else ""
   68:                 left_index = left_offset + local_left_index if local_left_index is not None else None
   69:                 right_index = right_offset + local_right_index if local_right_index is not None else None
   70:                 if before and after and _should_split_replace(before, after):
   71:                     changes.append(("removed", left_index, None, before, ""))
   72:                     changes.append(("added", None, right_index, "", after))
   73:                 else:
   74:                     kind = "modified" if before and after else "added" if after else "removed"
   75:                     changes.append((kind, left_index, right_index, before, after))
   76:         elif tag == "delete":
   77:             for local_left_index in range(i1, i2):
   78:                 changes.append(("removed", left_offset + local_left_index, None, left_lines[local_left_index], ""))
   79:         elif tag == "insert":
   80:             for local_right_index in range(j1, j2):
   81:                 changes.append(("added", None, right_offset + local_right_index, "", right_lines[local_right_index]))
   82:     return changes
   83: 
   84: 
   85: def _unique_lcs_anchors(left_lines: list[str], right_lines: list[str]) -> list[tuple[int, int]]:
   86:     left_counts = Counter(left_lines)
   87:     right_counts = Counter(right_lines)
   88:     right_positions = {line: index for index, line in enumerate(right_lines) if right_counts[line] == 1}
   89:     pairs = [
   90:         (left_index, right_positions[line])
   91:         for left_index, line in enumerate(left_lines)
   92:         if left_counts[line] == 1 and right_counts[line] == 1
   93:     ]
   94:     return _longest_increasing_pairs(pairs)
   95: 
   96: 
   97: def _longest_increasing_pairs(pairs: list[tuple[int, int]]) -> list[tuple[int, int]]:
   98:     if not pairs:
   99:         return []
  100:     best: list[tuple[int, int]] = []
  101:     for pair in pairs:
  102:         left_index, right_index = pair
  103:         candidates = [sequence + [pair] for sequence in best if sequence[-1][1] < right_index]
  104:         candidate = max(candidates, key=len, default=[pair])
  105:         best.append(candidate)
  106:     return max(best, key=len, default=[])
  107: 
  108: 
  109: def _line_similarity(left: str, right: str) -> float:
  110:     return SequenceMatcher(a=left.strip().lower(), b=right.strip().lower(), autojunk=False).ratio()
  111: 
  112: 
  113: def _should_split_replace(left: str, right: str) -> bool:
  114:     if min(len(left.strip()), len(right.strip())) < 8:
  115:         return False
  116:     return _line_similarity(left, right) < MIN_MODIFIED_SIMILARITY

Файл: src\file_compare_app\core\type_detection.py
Комментарий: Общие модели, профили нормализации, маршрутизация сравнения.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: 
    4: TEXT_EXTENSIONS = {".txt", ".md", ".log", ".csv", ".tsv", ".py", ".sql", ".css", ".js", ".html"}
    5: CONFIG_EXTENSIONS = {
    6:     ".json",
    7:     ".yaml",
    8:     ".yml",
    9:     ".toml",
   10:     ".ini",
   11:     ".cfg",
   12:     ".conf",
   13:     ".env",
   14:     ".properties",
   15:     ".xml",
   16: }
   17: IMAGE_EXTENSIONS = {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".bmp", ".tiff", ".tif", ".webp"}
   18: 
   19: 
   20: def detect_file_kind(path: Path) -> str:
   21:     name = path.name.lower()
   22:     suffix = path.suffix.lower()
   23: 
   24:     if name in {"dockerfile", ".gitignore"}:
   25:         return "config"
   26:     if suffix in TEXT_EXTENSIONS:
   27:         return "text"
   28:     if suffix in CONFIG_EXTENSIONS:
   29:         return "config"
   30:     if suffix == ".docx":
   31:         return "docx"
   32:     if suffix == ".pdf":
   33:         return "pdf"
   34:     if suffix == ".klp":
   35:         return "klp"
   36:     if suffix in {".xlsx", ".xlsm"}:
   37:         return "xlsx"
   38:     if suffix in IMAGE_EXTENSIONS:
   39:         return "image"
   40:     return "binary"

Файл: src\file_compare_app\diagnostics\dependencies.py
Комментарий: Файл проекта.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: from dataclasses import dataclass
    4: from importlib.util import find_spec
    5: from shutil import which
    6: 
    7: 
    8: @dataclass(frozen=True)
    9: class DependencyStatus:
   10:     key: str
   11:     label: str
   12:     required_for: str
   13:     available: bool
   14:     detail: str
   15: 
   16: 
   17: def collect_dependency_statuses() -> list[DependencyStatus]:
   18:     return [
   19:         _python_module("ui", "PySide6", "Интерфейс приложения", "PySide6"),
   20:         _python_module("docx", "DOCX", "Word-документы", "docx"),
   21:         _python_module("pdf", "PDF", "PDF с текстовым слоем", "fitz"),
   22:         _python_module("ocr_python", "OCR Python", "OCR-обвязка для PDF и изображений", "pytesseract"),
   23:         _external_program("ocr_engine", "OCR Tesseract", "Распознавание сканов", "tesseract"),
   24:         _python_module("excel", "Excel", "XLSX-книги и ячейки", "openpyxl"),
   25:         _python_module("image", "Images", "PNG/JPG/WebP и визуальное сравнение", "PIL"),
   26:         _python_module("yaml", "YAML", "Config-файлы .yaml/.yml", "yaml"),
   27:     ]
   28: 
   29: 
   30: def format_dependency_report(statuses: list[DependencyStatus]) -> str:
   31:     lines = ["Диагностика локальных возможностей", ""]
   32:     for status in statuses:
   33:         state = "доступно" if status.available else "не найдено"
   34:         lines.append(f"{status.label}: {state}")
   35:         lines.append(f"  Для: {status.required_for}")
   36:         lines.append(f"  Детали: {status.detail}")
   37:     return "\n".join(lines)
   38: 
   39: 
   40: def _python_module(key: str, label: str, required_for: str, module_name: str) -> DependencyStatus:
   41:     available = find_spec(module_name) is not None
   42:     detail = f"Python-модуль `{module_name}` установлен" if available else f"Python-модуль `{module_name}` не найден"
   43:     return DependencyStatus(key, label, required_for, available, detail)
   44: 
   45: 
   46: def _external_program(key: str, label: str, required_for: str, executable: str) -> DependencyStatus:
   47:     path = which(executable)
   48:     available = path is not None
   49:     detail = f"Найден: {path}" if path else f"`{executable}` не найден в PATH"
   50:     return DependencyStatus(key, label, required_for, available, detail)

Файл: src\file_compare_app\registry\database.py
Комментарий: База данных, реестр объектов, версии файлов и мониторинг.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: import os
    4: import shutil
    5: import sqlite3
    6: import sys
    7: from pathlib import Path
    8: 
    9: 
   10: REGISTRY_DB_FILENAME = "registry.sqlite3"
   11: LEGACY_REGISTRY_DIR_NAME = "FileCompareRegistry"
   12: 
   13: 
   14: def default_registry_db_path() -> Path:
   15:     if getattr(sys, "frozen", False):
   16:         return Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent / REGISTRY_DB_FILENAME
   17:     return legacy_registry_db_path()
   18: 
   19: 
   20: def legacy_registry_db_path() -> Path:
   21:     base = Path(os.environ.get("LOCALAPPDATA", Path.home() / "AppData" / "Local"))
   22:     return base / LEGACY_REGISTRY_DIR_NAME / REGISTRY_DB_FILENAME
   23: 
   24: 
   25: def connect_registry_db(path: Path | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
   26:     db_path = Path(path) if path is not None else default_registry_db_path()
   27:     if path is None:
   28:         copy_legacy_registry_db_if_needed(db_path)
   29:     db_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   30:     connection = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
   31:     connection.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
   32:     connection.execute("pragma foreign_keys = on")
   33:     return connection
   34: 
   35: 
   36: def copy_legacy_registry_db_if_needed(target_path: Path) -> None:
   37:     legacy_path = legacy_registry_db_path()
   38:     if target_path == legacy_path or target_path.exists() or not legacy_path.exists():
   39:         return
   40:     target_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   41:     shutil.copy2(legacy_path, target_path)
   42: 
   43: 
   44: def initialize_registry_db(connection: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
   45:     connection.executescript(
   46:         """
   47:         create table if not exists registry_nodes (
   48:             id integer primary key autoincrement,
   49:             parent_id integer references registry_nodes(id) on delete cascade,
   50:             name text not null,
   51:             node_type text not null default 'Объект',
   52:             code text not null default '',
   53:             responsible text not null default '',
   54:             description text not null default '',
   55:             template_key text not null default '',
   56:             monitoring_enabled integer not null default 1,
   57:             monitor_interval_minutes integer not null default 30,
   58:             created_at text not null,
   59:             updated_at text not null
   60:         );
   61: 
   62:         create table if not exists watched_files (
   63:             id integer primary key autoincrement,
   64:             node_id integer not null references registry_nodes(id) on delete cascade,
   65:             file_path text not null,
   66:             label text not null,
   67:             file_kind text not null,
   68:             baseline_hash text not null,
   69:             last_hash text not null,
   70:             last_checked_at text,
   71:             status text not null default 'ok',
   72:             last_error text not null default '',
   73:             created_at text not null,
   74:             updated_at text not null
   75:         );
   76: 
   77:         create table if not exists file_versions (
   78:             id integer primary key autoincrement,
   79:             watched_file_id integer not null references watched_files(id) on delete cascade,
   80:             version_number integer not null,
   81:             snapshot_path text not null,
   82:             sha256 text not null,
   83:             size_bytes integer not null default 0,
   84:             change_count integer not null default 0,
   85:             created_at text not null,
   86:             unique(watched_file_id, version_number)
   87:         );
   88: 
   89:         create table if not exists monitor_events (
   90:             id integer primary key autoincrement,
   91:             node_id integer not null references registry_nodes(id) on delete cascade,
   92:             watched_file_id integer not null references watched_files(id) on delete cascade,
   93:             event_type text not null,
   94:             change_count integer not null default 0,
   95:             report_path text not null default '',
   96:             message text not null default '',
   97:             risk_count integer not null default 0,
   98:             risk_summary text not null default '',
   99:             created_at text not null
  100:         );
  101: 
  102:         create table if not exists comparison_reviews (
  103:             id integer primary key autoincrement,
  104:             watched_file_id integer not null references watched_files(id) on delete cascade,
  105:             from_version integer not null,
  106:             to_version integer not null,
  107:             status text not null default 'new',
  108:             reviewer text not null default '',
  109:             comment text not null default '',
  110:             reviewed_at text not null default '',
  111:             updated_at text not null,
  112:             unique(watched_file_id, from_version, to_version)
  113:         );
  114: 
  115:         create index if not exists idx_registry_nodes_parent on registry_nodes(parent_id);
  116:         create index if not exists idx_watched_files_node on watched_files(node_id);
  117:         create index if not exists idx_file_versions_watched on file_versions(watched_file_id);
  118:         create index if not exists idx_monitor_events_node on monitor_events(node_id);
  119:         create index if not exists idx_comparison_reviews_watched on comparison_reviews(watched_file_id);
  120:         """
  121:     )
  122:     _ensure_column(connection, "registry_nodes", "template_key", "text not null default ''")
  123:     _ensure_column(connection, "monitor_events", "risk_count", "integer not null default 0")
  124:     _ensure_column(connection, "monitor_events", "risk_summary", "text not null default ''")
  125:     connection.commit()
  126: 
  127: 
  128: def _ensure_column(connection: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, column: str, definition: str) -> None:
  129:     columns = {row["name"] for row in connection.execute(f"pragma table_info({table})").fetchall()}
  130:     if column not in columns:
  131:         connection.execute(f"alter table {table} add column {column} {definition}")

Файл: src\file_compare_app\registry\monitor.py
Комментарий: База данных, реестр объектов, версии файлов и мониторинг.

    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: import hashlib
    4: import shutil
    5: from collections import Counter
    6: from pathlib import Path
    7: 
    8: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change
    9: from file_compare_app.core.orchestrator import compare_files
   10: from file_compare_app.core.type_detection import detect_file_kind
   11: from file_compare_app.registry.models import FileVersion, MonitoringFileInfo, MonitoringSummary, WatchedFile
   12: from file_compare_app.registry.repository import RegistryRepository
   13: 
   14: 
   15: def file_sha256(path: Path) -> str:
   16:     digest = hashlib.sha256()
   17:     with path.open("rb") as handle:
   18:         for chunk in iter(lambda: handle.read(1024 * 1024), b""):
   19:             digest.update(chunk)
   20:     return digest.hexdigest()
   21: 
   22: 
   23: class RegistryMonitor:
   24:     def __init__(self, repository: RegistryRepository) -> None:
   25:         self.repository = repository
   26: 
   27:     def add_file(self, node_id: int, path: Path | str, label: str | None = None) -> WatchedFile:
   28:         file_path = Path(path)
   29:         digest = file_sha256(file_path)
   30:         watched = self.repository.create_watched_file(
   31:             node_id=node_id,
   32:             file_path=str(file_path),
   33:             label=label or file_path.name,
   34:             file_kind=detect_file_kind(file_path),
   35:             baseline_hash=digest,
   36:             last_hash=digest,
   37:         )
   38:         snapshot_path = self._store_snapshot(watched, file_path, 1)
   39:         self.repository.create_file_version(
   40:             watched_file_id=watched.id,
   41:             version_number=1,
   42:             snapshot_path=str(snapshot_path),
   43:             sha256=digest,
   44:             size_bytes=file_path.stat().st_size,
   45:         )
   46:         self.repository.create_event(
   47:             node_id=node_id,
   48:             watched_file_id=watched.id,
   49:             event_type="baseline",
   50:             message=f"Базовая версия v1 сохранена: {file_path.name}",
   51:         )
   52:         return watched
   53: 
   54:     def add_file_pair(
   55:         self,
   56:         node_id: int,
   57:         before_path: Path | str,
   58:         after_path: Path | str,
   59:         label: str | None = None,
   60:     ) -> WatchedFile:
   61:         before_file = Path(before_path)
   62:         watched = self.add_file(node_id, before_file, label=label or before_file.name)
   63:         return self.add_next_version(watched.id, after_path)
   64: 
   65:     def add_next_version(self, watched_file_id: int, path: Path | str) -> WatchedFile:
   66:         watched = self.repository.get_watched_file(watched_file_id)
   67:         file_path = Path(path)
   68:         digest = file_sha256(file_path)
   69:         latest = self._ensure_latest_version(watched, file_path, digest)
   70:         status = "changed" if digest != latest.sha256 else "ok"
   71:         updated = self.repository.update_watched_file_status(
   72:             watched.id,
   73:             digest,
   74:             status,
   75:             file_path=str(file_path),
   76:         )
   77:         if status == "ok":
   78:             self.repository.create_event(
   79:                 watched.node_id,
   80:                 watched.id,
   81:                 "checked",
   82:                 message=f"Новая версия совпадает с v{latest.version_number}: {file_path.name}",
   83:             )
   84:             return updated
   85: 
   86:         self._record_changed_version(updated, file_path, digest, latest)
   87:         return updated
   88: 
   89:     def check_file(self, watched_file_id: int) -> WatchedFile:
   90:         watched = self.repository.get_watched_file(watched_file_id)
   91:         file_path = Path(watched.file_path)
   92:         if not file_path.exists():
   93:             updated = self.repository.update_watched_file_status(
   94:                 watched.id,
   95:                 watched.last_hash,
   96:                 "missing",
   97:                 "Файл не найден",
   98:             )
   99:             self.repository.create_event(
  100:                 watched.node_id,
  101:                 watched.id,
  102:                 "missing",
  103:                 message=f"Файл не найден: {file_path}",
  104:             )
  105:             return updated
  106:         try:
  107:             digest = file_sha256(file_path)
  108:         except OSError as exc:
  109:             updated = self.repository.update_watched_file_status(
  110:                 watched.id,
  111:                 watched.last_hash,
  112:                 "error",
  113:                 exc.__class__.__name__,
  114:             )
  115:             self.repository.create_event(watched.node_id, watched.id, "error", message=exc.__class__.__name__)
  116:             return updated
  117: 
  118:         latest = self._ensure_latest_version(watched, file_path, digest)
  119:         status = "changed" if digest != latest.sha256 else "ok"
  120:         updated = self.repository.update_watched_file_status(watched.id, digest, status)
  121:         if status == "ok":
  122:             self.repository.create_event(
  123:                 watched.node_id,
  124:                 watched.id,
  125:                 "checked",
  126:                 message=f"Без изменений: v{latest.version_number}, {file_path.name}",
  127:             )
  128:             return updated
  129: 
  130:         self._record_changed_version(updated, file_path, digest, latest)
  131:         return updated
  132: 
  133:     def check_node(self, node_id: int, include_children: bool = True) -> list[WatchedFile]:
  134:         node_ids = self.repository.list_descendant_ids(node_id) if include_children else [node_id]
  135:         checked: list[WatchedFile] = []
  136:         for current_node_id in node_ids:
  137:             for watched in self.repository.list_watched_files(current_node_id):
  138:                 checked.append(self.check_file(watched.id))
  139:         return checked
  140: 
  141:     def build_node_summary(self, node_id: int) -> MonitoringSummary:
  142:         files = self.repository.list_watched_files_for_tree(node_id)
  143:         items: list[MonitoringFileInfo] = []
  144:         status_counts: Counter[str] = Counter({"ok": 0, "changed": 0, "missing": 0, "error": 0})
  145:         for watched in files:
  146:             latest: FileVersion | None = None
  147:             try:
  148:                 latest = self.repository.get_latest_file_version(watched.id)
  149:             except KeyError:
  150:                 pass
  151:             status_counts[watched.status] += 1
  152:             items.append(
  153:                 MonitoringFileInfo(
  154:                     node_path=self.repository.node_path(watched.node_id),
  155:                     watched_file=watched,
  156:                     latest_version=latest,
  157:                     last_event=self.repository.get_last_event_for_watched_file(watched.id),
  158:                 )
  159:             )
  160:         return MonitoringSummary(
  161:             node_id=node_id,
  162:             total_files=len(files),
  163:             status_counts=status_counts,
  164:             files=items,
  165:         )
  166: 
  167:     def _ensure_latest_version(self, watched: WatchedFile, file_path: Path, digest: str) -> FileVersion:
  168:         try:
  169:             return self.repository.get_latest_file_version(watched.id)
  170:         except KeyError:
  171:             snapshot_path = self._store_snapshot(watched, file_path, 1)
  172:             return self.repository.create_file_version(
  173:                 watched_file_id=watched.id,
  174:                 version_number=1,
  175:                 snapshot_path=str(snapshot_path),
  176:                 sha256=digest,
  177:                 size_bytes=file_path.stat().st_size,
  178:             )
  179: 
  180:     def _store_snapshot(self, watched: WatchedFile, source_path: Path, version_number: int) -> Path:
  181:         version_dir = self.repository.snapshot_root() / f"node_{watched.node_id}" / f"file_{watched.id}"
  182:         version_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  183:         snapshot_path = version_dir / f"v{version_number:04d}_{_safe_filename(source_path.name)}"
  184:         shutil.copy2(source_path, snapshot_path)
  185:         return snapshot_path
  186: 
  187:     def _record_changed_version(
  188:         self,
  189:         watched: WatchedFile,
  190:         file_path: Path,
  191:         digest: str,
  192:         latest: FileVersion,
  193:     ) -> None:
  194:         result = compare_files(Path(latest.snapshot_path), file_path)
  195:         risk_changes = [change for change in result.changes if change.severity == "risk"]
  196:         next_version_number = latest.version_number + 1
  197:         snapshot_path = self._store_snapshot(watched, file_path, next_version_number)
  198:         self.repository.create_file_version(
  199:             watched_file_id=watched.id,
  200:             version_number=next_version_number,
  201:             snapshot_path=str(snapshot_path),
  202:             sha256=digest,
  203:             size_bytes=file_path.stat().st_size,
  204:             change_count=len(result.changes),
  205:         )
  206:         self.repository.create_event(
  207:             watched.node_id,
  208:             watched.id,
  209:             "changed",
  210:             change_count=len(result.changes),
  211:             risk_count=len(risk_changes),
  212:             risk_summary=_format_risk_summary(risk_changes),
  213:             message=(
  214:                 f"Изменен {watched.label}: v{latest.version_number} -> v{next_version_number}; "
  215:                 f"изменений: {len(result.changes)}; {_format_change_preview(result.changes)}"
  216:             ),
  217:         )
  218: 
  219: 
  220: def _safe_filename(name: str) -> str:
  221:     safe = "".join(character if character.isalnum() or character in ".-_" else "_" for character in name)
  222:     return safe or "file"
  223: 
  224: 
  225: def _format_change_preview(changes: list[Change]) -> str:
  226:     if not changes:
  227:         return "структурных изменений не найдено"
  228:     first = changes[0]
  229:     before = _shorten(first.before)
  230:     after = _shorten(first.after)
  231:     key = first.notes if first.notes not in {"line diff", "Kaspersky KLP policy profile"} else ""
  232:     if before and after:
  233:         if key:
  234:             return f"{key}: {before} -> {key}: {after}"
  235:         return f"{before} -> {after}"
  236:     if after:
  237:         return f"добавлено: {after}"
  238:     if before:
  239:         return f"удалено: {before}"
  240:     return first.notes or first.change_type
  241: 
  242: 
  243: def _format_risk_summary(changes: list[Change]) -> str:
  244:     if not changes:
  245:         return ""
  246:     previews: list[str] = []
  247:     for change in changes[:3]:
  248:         preview = change.after or change.before or change.notes or change.change_type
  249:         previews.append(_shorten(preview, 90))
  250:     if len(changes) > 3:
  251:         previews.append(f"еще {len(changes) - 3}")
  252:     return "; ".join(previews)
  253: 
  254: 
  255: def _shorten(value: str, limit: int = 120) -> str:
  256:     compact = " ".join(value.split())
  257:     if len(compact) <= limit:
  258:         return compact
  259:     return compact[: limit - 1] + "…"

    1: from __future__ import annotations
