   13: 
   14: def _now() -> str:
   15:     return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds")
   16: 
   17: 
   18: class RegistryRepository:
   19:     def __init__(self, connection: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
   20:         self.connection = connection
   21:         self.db_path = _connection_path(connection)
   22: 
   23:     @classmethod
   24:     def create(cls, path: Path | None = None) -> "RegistryRepository":
   25:         connection = connect_registry_db(path)
   26:         initialize_registry_db(connection)
   27:         return cls(connection)
   28: 
   29:     def create_node(
   30:         self,
   31:         name: str,
   32:         parent_id: int | None = None,
   33:         node_type: str = "Объект",
   34:         code: str = "",
   35:         responsible: str = "",
   36:         description: str = "",
   37:         template_key: str = "",
   38:         monitoring_enabled: bool = True,
   39:         monitor_interval_minutes: int = 30,
   40:     ) -> RegistryNode:
   41:         timestamp = _now()
   42:         cursor = self.connection.execute(
   43:             """
   44:             insert into registry_nodes
   45:             (parent_id, name, node_type, code, responsible, description, template_key, monitoring_enabled, monitor_interval_minutes, created_at, updated_at)
   46:             values (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
   47:             """,
   48:             (
   49:                 parent_id,
   50:                 name,
   51:                 node_type,
   52:                 code,
   53:                 responsible,
   54:                 description,
   55:                 template_key,
   56:                 1 if monitoring_enabled else 0,
   57:                 monitor_interval_minutes,
   58:                 timestamp,
   59:                 timestamp,
   60:             ),
   61:         )
   62:         self.connection.commit()
   63:         return self.get_node(int(cursor.lastrowid))
   64: 
   65:     def get_node(self, node_id: int) -> RegistryNode:
   66:         row = self.connection.execute(
   67:             "select * from registry_nodes where id = ?",
   68:             (node_id,),
   69:         ).fetchone()
   70:         if row is None:
   71:             raise KeyError(f"registry node {node_id} not found")
   72:         return _node_from_row(row)
   73: 
   74:     def update_node(
   75:         self,
   76:         node_id: int,
   77:         *,
   78:         name: str | None = None,
   79:         node_type: str | None = None,
   80:         code: str | None = None,
   81:         responsible: str | None = None,
   82:         description: str | None = None,
   83:         template_key: str | None = None,
   84:         monitoring_enabled: bool | None = None,
   85:         monitor_interval_minutes: int | None = None,
   86:     ) -> RegistryNode:
   87:         current = self.get_node(node_id)
   88:         timestamp = _now()
   89:         self.connection.execute(
   90:             """
   91:             update registry_nodes
   92:             set name = ?,
   93:                 node_type = ?,
   94:                 code = ?,
   95:                 responsible = ?,
   96:                 description = ?,
   97:                 template_key = ?,
   98:                 monitoring_enabled = ?,
   99:                 monitor_interval_minutes = ?,
  100:                 updated_at = ?
  101:             where id = ?
  102:             """,
  103:             (
  104:                 current.name if name is None else name,
  105:                 current.node_type if node_type is None else node_type,
  106:                 current.code if code is None else code,
  107:                 current.responsible if responsible is None else responsible,
  108:                 current.description if description is None else description,
  109:                 current.template_key if template_key is None else template_key,
  110:                 int(current.monitoring_enabled if monitoring_enabled is None else monitoring_enabled),
  111:                 current.monitor_interval_minutes if monitor_interval_minutes is None else monitor_interval_minutes,
  112:                 timestamp,
  113:                 node_id,
  114:             ),
  115:         )
  116:         self.connection.commit()
  117:         return self.get_node(node_id)
  118: 
  119:     def list_children(self, parent_id: int | None) -> list[RegistryNode]:
  120:         if parent_id is None:
  121:             rows = self.connection.execute(
  122:                 "select * from registry_nodes where parent_id is null order by name"
  123:             ).fetchall()
  124:         else:
  125:             rows = self.connection.execute(
  126:                 "select * from registry_nodes where parent_id = ? order by name",
  127:                 (parent_id,),
  128:             ).fetchall()
  129:         return [_node_from_row(row) for row in rows]
  130: 
  131:     def list_descendant_ids(self, node_id: int) -> list[int]:
  132:         rows = self.connection.execute(
  133:             """
  134:             with recursive tree(id) as (
  135:                 select id from registry_nodes where id = ?
  136:                 union all
  137:                 select registry_nodes.id
  138:                 from registry_nodes
  139:                 join tree on registry_nodes.parent_id = tree.id
  140:             )
  141:             select id from tree
  142:             """,
  143:             (node_id,),
  144:         ).fetchall()
  145:         return [int(row["id"]) for row in rows]
  146: 
  147:     def delete_node(self, node_id: int) -> list[int]:
  148:         deleted_ids = self.list_descendant_ids(node_id)
  149:         if not deleted_ids:
  150:             raise KeyError(f"registry node {node_id} not found")
  151:         self.connection.execute("delete from registry_nodes where id = ?", (node_id,))
  152:         self.connection.commit()
  153:         return deleted_ids

  155:     def create_watched_file(
  156:         self,
  157:         node_id: int,

  159:         label: str,

  161:         baseline_hash: str,

  168:             insert into watched_files
  169:             (node_id, file_path, label, file_kind, baseline_hash, last_hash, status, created_at, updated_at)
  170:             values (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
  171:             """,
  172:             (node_id, file_path, label, file_kind, baseline_hash, last_hash, status, timestamp, timestamp),
  173:         )
  174:         self.connection.commit()
  175:         return self.get_watched_file(int(cursor.lastrowid))
  176: 
  177:     def get_watched_file(self, watched_file_id: int) -> WatchedFile:
  178:         row = self.connection.execute(
  179:             "select * from watched_files where id = ?",
  180:             (watched_file_id,),
  181:         ).fetchone()
  182:         if row is None:
  183:             raise KeyError(f"watched file {watched_file_id} not found")
  184:         return _watched_file_from_row(row)
  185: 
  186:     def delete_watched_file(self, watched_file_id: int) -> WatchedFile:
  187:         watched = self.get_watched_file(watched_file_id)
  188:         self.connection.execute("delete from watched_files where id = ?", (watched_file_id,))
  189:         self.connection.commit()
  190:         return watched
  191: 
  192:     def list_watched_files(self, node_id: int) -> list[WatchedFile]:
  193:         rows = self.connection.execute(
  194:             "select * from watched_files where node_id = ? order by label",
  195:             (node_id,),
  196:         ).fetchall()
  197:         return [_watched_file_from_row(row) for row in rows]
  198: 
  199:     def list_watched_files_for_tree(self, node_id: int) -> list[WatchedFile]:
  200:         node_ids = self.list_descendant_ids(node_id)
  201:         if not node_ids:
  202:             return []
  203:         placeholders = ", ".join("?" for _ in node_ids)
  204:         rows = self.connection.execute(
  205:             f"select * from watched_files where node_id in ({placeholders}) order by node_id, label",
  206:             node_ids,
  207:         ).fetchall()
  208:         return [_watched_file_from_row(row) for row in rows]
  209: 
  210:     def update_watched_file_status(
  211:         self,
  212:         watched_file_id: int,
  213:         last_hash: str,
  214:         status: str,
  215:         last_error: str = "",
  216:         file_path: str | None = None,
  217:     ) -> WatchedFile:
  218:         timestamp = _now()
  219:         self.connection.execute(
  220:             """
  221:             update watched_files
  222:             set file_path = coalesce(?, file_path),
  223:                 last_hash = ?,
  224:                 status = ?,
  225:                 last_error = ?,
  226:                 last_checked_at = ?,
  227:                 updated_at = ?
  228:             where id = ?
  229:             """,
  230:             (file_path, last_hash, status, last_error, timestamp, timestamp, watched_file_id),
  231:         )
  232:         self.connection.commit()
  233:         return self.get_watched_file(watched_file_id)
  234: 
  235:     def create_file_version(

  238:         version_number: int,
  239:         snapshot_path: str,
  240:         sha256: str,
  241:         size_bytes: int,
  242:         change_count: int = 0,
  243:     ) -> FileVersion:

  249:             values (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)

  251:             (watched_file_id, version_number, snapshot_path, sha256, size_bytes, change_count, timestamp),
  252:         )
  253:         self.connection.commit()

  255: 
  256:     def get_file_version(self, version_id: int) -> FileVersion:

  270:         return [_file_version_from_row(row) for row in rows]
  271: 
  272:     def get_latest_file_version(self, watched_file_id: int) -> FileVersion:
  273:         row = self.connection.execute(
  274:             """
  275:             select * from file_versions
  276:             where watched_file_id = ?
  277:             order by version_number desc
  278:             limit 1
  279:             """,
  280:             (watched_file_id,),
  281:         ).fetchone()
  282:         if row is None:
  283:             raise KeyError(f"file version for watched file {watched_file_id} not found")
  284:         return _file_version_from_row(row)
  285: 
  286:     def create_event(
  287:         self,
  288:         node_id: int,
  289:         watched_file_id: int,
  290:         event_type: str,
  291:         change_count: int = 0,
  292:         report_path: str = "",
  293:         message: str = "",
  294:         risk_count: int = 0,
  295:         risk_summary: str = "",
  296:     ) -> MonitorEvent:
  297:         timestamp = _now()
  298:         cursor = self.connection.execute(
  299:             """
  300:             insert into monitor_events
  301:             (node_id, watched_file_id, event_type, change_count, report_path, message, risk_count, risk_summary, created_at)
  302:             values (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
  303:             """,
  304:             (node_id, watched_file_id, event_type, change_count, report_path, message, risk_count, risk_summary, timestamp),
  305:         )
  306:         self.connection.commit()
  307:         return self.get_event(int(cursor.lastrowid))
  308: 
  309:     def get_event(self, event_id: int) -> MonitorEvent:
  310:         row = self.connection.execute(
  311:             "select * from monitor_events where id = ?",
  312:             (event_id,),
  313:         ).fetchone()
  314:         if row is None:
  315:             raise KeyError(f"monitor event {event_id} not found")
  316:         return _event_from_row(row)
  317: 
  318:     def list_events(self, node_id: int) -> list[MonitorEvent]:
  319:         rows = self.connection.execute(
  320:             "select * from monitor_events where node_id = ? order by id desc",
  321:             (node_id,),
  322:         ).fetchall()
  323:         return [_event_from_row(row) for row in rows]
  324: 
  325:     def list_events_for_tree(self, node_id: int) -> list[MonitorEvent]:
  326:         node_ids = self.list_descendant_ids(node_id)
  327:         if not node_ids:
  328:             return []
  329:         placeholders = ", ".join("?" for _ in node_ids)
  330:         rows = self.connection.execute(
  331:             f"select * from monitor_events where node_id in ({placeholders}) order by id desc",
  332:             node_ids,
  333:         ).fetchall()
  334:         return [_event_from_row(row) for row in rows]
  335: 
  336:     def get_last_event_for_watched_file(self, watched_file_id: int) -> MonitorEvent | None:
  337:         row = self.connection.execute(
  338:             """
  339:             select * from monitor_events
  340:             where watched_file_id = ?
  341:             order by id desc
  342:             limit 1
  343:             """,
  344:             (watched_file_id,),
  345:         ).fetchone()
  346:         return None if row is None else _event_from_row(row)
  347: 
  348:     def get_comparison_review(self, watched_file_id: int, from_version: int, to_version: int) -> ComparisonReview:
  349:         row = self.connection.execute(
  350:             """
  351:             select * from comparison_reviews
  352:             where watched_file_id = ? and from_version = ? and to_version = ?
  353:             """,
  354:             (watched_file_id, from_version, to_version),
  355:         ).fetchone()
  356:         if row is None:
  357:             timestamp = _now()
  358:             return ComparisonReview(
  359:                 id=0,
  360:                 watched_file_id=watched_file_id,
  361:                 from_version=from_version,
  362:                 to_version=to_version,
  363:                 status="new",
  364:                 reviewer="",
  365:                 comment="",
  366:                 reviewed_at="",
  367:                 updated_at=timestamp,
  368:             )
  369:         return _comparison_review_from_row(row)
  370: 
  371:     def upsert_comparison_review(
  372:         self,
  373:         watched_file_id: int,
  374:         from_version: int,
  375:         to_version: int,
  376:         status: str,
  377:         reviewer: str = "",
  378:         comment: str = "",
  379:     ) -> ComparisonReview:
  380:         timestamp = _now()
  381:         reviewed_at = timestamp if status != "new" else ""
  382:         self.connection.execute(
  383:             """
  384:             insert into comparison_reviews
  385:             (watched_file_id, from_version, to_version, status, reviewer, comment, reviewed_at, updated_at)
  386:             values (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
  387:             on conflict(watched_file_id, from_version, to_version) do update set
  388:                 status = excluded.status,
  389:                 reviewer = excluded.reviewer,
  390:                 comment = excluded.comment,
  391:                 reviewed_at = excluded.reviewed_at,
  392:                 updated_at = excluded.updated_at
  393:             """,
  394:             (watched_file_id, from_version, to_version, status, reviewer, comment, reviewed_at, timestamp),
  395:         )
  396:         self.connection.commit()
  397:         return self.get_comparison_review(watched_file_id, from_version, to_version)
  398: 
  399:     def node_path(self, node_id: int) -> str:
  400:         names: list[str] = []
  401:         current: int | None = node_id
  402:         while current is not None:
  403:             node = self.get_node(current)
  404:             names.append(node.name)
  405:             current = node.parent_id
  406:         return " / ".join(reversed(names))
  407: 
  408:     def snapshot_root(self) -> Path:
  409:         if self.db_path is None:
  410:             return Path.cwd() / "registry_snapshots"
  411:         return self.db_path.parent / "registry_snapshots"
  412: 
  413:     def backup_database(self, target_dir: Path | str | None = None) -> Path:
  414:         if self.db_path is None:
  415:             raise RuntimeError("database backup requires a file-backed SQLite database")
  416:         self.connection.commit()
  417:         backup_dir = Path(target_dir) if target_dir is not None else self.db_path.parent / "backups"
  418:         backup_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  419:         timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d-%H%M%S-%f")
  420:         backup_path = backup_dir / f"registry-backup-{timestamp}.sqlite3"
  421:         with sqlite3.connect(backup_path) as target:
  422:             self.connection.backup(target)
  423:         return backup_path
  424: 
  425:     def export_registry_excel(self, output_path: Path | str) -> Path:
  426:         export_path = Path(output_path)
  427:         export_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  428: 
  429:         workbook = Workbook()
  430:         objects_sheet = workbook.active
  431:         objects_sheet.title = "Объекты"
  432:         files_sheet = workbook.create_sheet("Файлы")
  433:         compare_sheet = workbook.create_sheet("Сверки")
  434:         history_sheet = workbook.create_sheet("История")
  435: 
  436:         _write_rows(
  437:             objects_sheet,
  438:             [
  439:                 ["ID", "Родитель", "Путь объекта", "Название", "Код", "Ответственный", "Тип", "Описание", "Создан", "Обновлен"],
  440:                 *self._object_export_rows(),
  441:             ],
  442:         )
  443:         _write_rows(
  444:             files_sheet,
  445:             [
  446:                 ["ID", "Путь объекта", "Объект", "Файл", "Тип", "Статус", "Текущий путь", "Версий", "Последняя проверка", "Обновлен"],
  447:                 *self._file_export_rows(),
  448:             ],
  449:         )
  450:         _write_rows(
  451:             compare_sheet,
  452:             [
  453:                 [
  454:                     "ID",
  455:                     "Файл ID",
  456:                     "Путь объекта",
  457:                     "Файл",
  458:                     "Версии",
  459:                     "Файл до",
  460:                     "Файл после",
  461:                     "Изменений",
  462:                     "Загружено",
  463:                     "Согласование",
  464:                     "Проверил",
  465:                     "Комментарий",
  466:                 ],
  467:                 *self._comparison_export_rows(),
  468:             ],
  469:         )
  470:         _write_rows(
  471:             history_sheet,
  472:             [
  473:                 ["ID", "Путь объекта", "Файл", "Тип события", "Статус", "Изменений", "Сообщение", "Создано"],
  474:                 *self._history_export_rows(),
  475:             ],
  476:         )
  477:         for sheet in workbook.worksheets:
  478:             _style_export_sheet(sheet)
  479:         workbook.save(export_path)
  480:         return export_path
  481: 
  482:     def _object_export_rows(self) -> list[list[object]]:
  483:         rows = self.connection.execute("select * from registry_nodes order by id").fetchall()
  484:         result: list[list[object]] = []
  485:         for row in rows:
  486:             node = _node_from_row(row)
  487:             parent_name = self.get_node(node.parent_id).name if node.parent_id is not None else ""
  488:             result.append(
  489:                 [
  490:                     node.id,
  491:                     parent_name,
  492:                     self.node_path(node.id),
  493:                     node.name,
  494:                     node.code,
  495:                     node.responsible,
  496:                     node.node_type,
  497:                     node.description,
  498:                     node.created_at,
  499:                     node.updated_at,
  500:                 ]
  501:             )
  502:         return result
  503: 
  504:     def _file_export_rows(self) -> list[list[object]]:
  505:         rows = self.connection.execute("select * from watched_files order by id").fetchall()
  506:         result: list[list[object]] = []
  507:         for row in rows:
  508:             watched = _watched_file_from_row(row)
  509:             node = self.get_node(watched.node_id)
  510:             result.append(
  511:                 [
  512:                     watched.id,
  513:                     self.node_path(watched.node_id),
  514:                     node.name,
  515:                     watched.label,
  516:                     watched.file_kind,
  517:                     _registry_status_text(watched.status),
  518:                     watched.file_path,
  519:                     len(self.list_file_versions(watched.id)),
  520:                     watched.last_checked_at or "",
  521:                     watched.updated_at,
  522:                 ]
  523:             )
  524:         return result
  525: 
  526:     def _comparison_export_rows(self) -> list[list[object]]:
  527:         watched_rows = self.connection.execute("select * from watched_files order by id").fetchall()
  528:         result: list[list[object]] = []
  529:         row_number = 1
  530:         for watched_row in watched_rows:
  531:             watched = _watched_file_from_row(watched_row)
  532:             versions = self.list_file_versions(watched.id)
  533:             for previous, current in zip(versions, versions[1:]):
  534:                 review = self.get_comparison_review(watched.id, previous.version_number, current.version_number)
  535:                 result.append(
  536:                     [
  537:                         row_number,
  538:                         watched.id,
  539:                         self.node_path(watched.node_id),
  540:                         watched.label,
  541:                         f"v{previous.version_number} -> v{current.version_number}",
  542:                         _snapshot_display_name(previous.snapshot_path),
  543:                         _snapshot_display_name(current.snapshot_path),
  544:                         current.change_count,
  545:                         current.created_at,
  546:                         _review_status_text(review.status),
  547:                         review.reviewer,
  548:                         review.comment,
  549:                     ]
  550:                 )
  551:                 row_number += 1
  552:         return result
  553: 
  554:     def _history_export_rows(self) -> list[list[object]]:
  555:         rows = self.connection.execute(
  556:             """
  557:             select monitor_events.*, watched_files.label as file_label
  558:             from monitor_events
  559:             left join watched_files on watched_files.id = monitor_events.watched_file_id
  560:             order by monitor_events.id desc
  561:             """
  562:         ).fetchall()
  563:         result: list[list[object]] = []
  564:         for row in rows:
  565:             event = _event_from_row(row)
  566:             result.append(
  567:                 [
  568:                     event.id,
  569:                     self.node_path(event.node_id),
  570:                     row["file_label"] or "",
  571:                     event.event_type,
  572:                     _registry_status_text(event.event_type),
  573:                     event.change_count,
  574:                     event.message,
  575:                     event.created_at,
  576:                 ]
  577:             )
  578:         return result
  579: 
  580: 
  581: def _node_from_row(row: sqlite3.Row) -> RegistryNode:
  582:     return RegistryNode(
  583:         id=int(row["id"]),
  584:         parent_id=row["parent_id"],
  585:         name=row["name"],
  586:         node_type=row["node_type"],
  587:         code=row["code"],
  588:         responsible=row["responsible"],
  589:         description=row["description"],
  590:         monitoring_enabled=bool(row["monitoring_enabled"]),
  591:         monitor_interval_minutes=int(row["monitor_interval_minutes"]),
  592:         created_at=row["created_at"],
  593:         updated_at=row["updated_at"],
  594:         template_key=row["template_key"],
  595:     )
  596: 
  597: 
  598: def _file_version_from_row(row: sqlite3.Row) -> FileVersion:
  599:     return FileVersion(
  600:         id=int(row["id"]),
  601:         watched_file_id=int(row["watched_file_id"]),
  602:         version_number=int(row["version_number"]),
  603:         snapshot_path=row["snapshot_path"],
  604:         sha256=row["sha256"],
  605:         size_bytes=int(row["size_bytes"]),
  606:         change_count=int(row["change_count"]),
  607:         created_at=row["created_at"],
  608:     )
  609: 
  610: 
  611: def _watched_file_from_row(row: sqlite3.Row) -> WatchedFile:
  612:     return WatchedFile(
  613:         id=int(row["id"]),
  614:         node_id=int(row["node_id"]),
  615:         file_path=row["file_path"],
  616:         label=row["label"],
  617:         file_kind=row["file_kind"],
  618:         baseline_hash=row["baseline_hash"],
  619:         last_hash=row["last_hash"],
  620:         last_checked_at=row["last_checked_at"],
  621:         status=row["status"],
  622:         last_error=row["last_error"],
  623:         created_at=row["created_at"],
  624:         updated_at=row["updated_at"],
  625:     )
  626: 
  627: 
  628: def _event_from_row(row: sqlite3.Row) -> MonitorEvent:
  629:     return MonitorEvent(
  630:         id=int(row["id"]),
  631:         node_id=int(row["node_id"]),
  632:         watched_file_id=int(row["watched_file_id"]),
  633:         event_type=row["event_type"],
  634:         change_count=int(row["change_count"]),
  635:         report_path=row["report_path"],
  636:         message=row["message"],
  637:         created_at=row["created_at"],
  638:         risk_count=int(row["risk_count"]),
  639:         risk_summary=row["risk_summary"],
  640:     )
  641: 
  642: 
  643: def _comparison_review_from_row(row: sqlite3.Row) -> ComparisonReview:
  644:     return ComparisonReview(
  645:         id=int(row["id"]),
  646:         watched_file_id=int(row["watched_file_id"]),
  647:         from_version=int(row["from_version"]),
  648:         to_version=int(row["to_version"]),
  649:         status=row["status"],
  650:         reviewer=row["reviewer"],
  651:         comment=row["comment"],
  652:         reviewed_at=row["reviewed_at"],
  653:         updated_at=row["updated_at"],
  654:     )
  655: 
  656: 
  657: def _connection_path(connection: sqlite3.Connection) -> Path | None:
  658:     row = connection.execute("pragma database_list").fetchone()
  659:     if row is None:
  660:         return None
  661:     file_path = row["file"] if isinstance(row, sqlite3.Row) else row[2]
  662:     return Path(file_path) if file_path else None
  663: 
  664: 
  665: def _registry_status_text(status: str) -> str:
  666:     return {
  667:         "ok": "OK",
  668:         "baseline": "Базовая версия",
  669:         "changed": "Изменен",
  670:         "missing": "Нет файла",
  671:         "error": "Ошибка",
  672:     }.get(status, status)
  673: 
  674: 
  675: def _review_status_text(status: str) -> str:
  676:     return {
  677:         "new": "Новое",
  678:         "checked": "Проверено",
  679:         "approved": "Согласовано",
  680:         "rejected": "Отклонено",
  681:     }.get(status, status)
  682: 
  683: 
  684: def _snapshot_display_name(snapshot_path: str) -> str:
  685:     name = Path(snapshot_path).name
  686:     return name[6:] if len(name) > 6 and name.startswith("v") and name[1:5].isdigit() and name[5] == "_" else name
  687: 
  688: 
  689: def _write_rows(sheet, rows: list[list[object]]) -> None:
  690:     for row in rows:
  691:         sheet.append(row)
  692: 
  693: 
  694: def _style_export_sheet(sheet) -> None:
  695:     header_fill = PatternFill("solid", fgColor="EFF6FF")
  696:     header_font = Font(bold=True, color="1F3A5F")
  697:     for cell in sheet[1]:
  698:         cell.fill = header_fill
  699:         cell.font = header_font
  700:         cell.alignment = Alignment(horizontal="center", vertical="center")
  701:     sheet.freeze_panes = "A2"
  702:     for column_cells in sheet.columns:
  703:         width = 12
  704:         for cell in column_cells:
  705:             value = "" if cell.value is None else str(cell.value)
  706:             width = max(width, min(len(value) + 2, 70))
  707:             cell.alignment = Alignment(vertical="top", wrap_text=True)
  708:         sheet.column_dimensions[column_cells[0].column_letter].width = width

    9: def render_html_report(result: ComparisonResult) -> str:
   10:     counts = Counter(change.change_type for change in result.changes)
   11:     summary_cards = "".join(
   12:         _summary_card(label, value)
   13:         for label, value in (
   14:             ("Всего", result.change_count),
   15:             ("Добавлено", counts.get("added", 0)),
   16:             ("Удалено", counts.get("removed", 0)),
   17:             ("Изменено", counts.get("modified", 0)),
   18:         )
   19:     )
   20:     rows = []
   21:     for change in result.changes:
   22:         source = compact_location(change.source_location)
   23:         target = compact_location(change.target_location)
   24:         rows.append(
   25:             "<tr>"
   26:             f"<td><span class='type'>{escape(change_type_label(change.change_type))}</span></td>"
   27:             f"<td>{escape(source)}</td>"
   28:             f"<td>{escape(target)}</td>"
   29:             f"<td class='old'>{escape(change.before)}</td>"
   30:             f"<td class='new'>{escape(change.after)}</td>"
   31:             f"<td>{escape(change.notes)}</td>"
   32:             "</tr>"
   33:         )
   34:     body = "\n".join(rows) or "<tr><td colspan='6' class='empty'>Изменений не найдено</td></tr>"
   35:     left_name = Path(result.left_path).name
   36:     right_name = Path(result.right_path).name
   37:     return f"""<!doctype html>
   38: <html lang="ru">

  114:     tr:last-child td {{ border-bottom: 0; }}
  115:     td {{ font-size: 13px; }}
  116:     .type {{ color: var(--blue); font-weight: 700; }}
  117:     .old {{ background: #fff1f0; color: var(--red); font-family: Consolas, Courier New, monospace; }}
  118:     .new {{ background: #ecfdf3; color: var(--green); font-family: Consolas, Courier New, monospace; }}
  119:     .empty {{ color: var(--muted); text-align: center; }}
  120:     .credit {{ margin-top: 18px; color: #8b95a7; font-size: 11px; text-align: right; }}
  121:   </style>
  122: </head>
  123: <body>
  124:   <main>
  125:     <header>
  126:       <div>
  127:         <h1>Сравнение файлов</h1>
  128:         <p class="subtitle">Найдено изменений: {result.change_count}</p>
  129:       </div>
  130:       <div class="mode">Строгий локальный режим</div>
  131:     </header>
  132:     <section class="summary-grid">{summary_cards}</section>
  133:     <section class="files">
  134:       <div><strong>Было:</strong> {escape(left_name)} <span>({escape(result.left_path)})</span></div>
  135:       <div><strong>Стало:</strong> {escape(right_name)} <span>({escape(result.right_path)})</span></div>
  136:     </section>
  137:     <table>
  138:       <thead>
  139:         <tr><th>Тип</th><th>Было где</th><th>Стало где</th><th>Было</th><th>Стало</th><th>Примечание</th></tr>
  140:       </thead>
  141:       <tbody>{body}</tbody>
  142:     </table>
  143:     <div class="credit">Разработал: Абдрахманов Амаль Даулетович</div>
  144:   </main>
  145: </body>
  146: </html>"""
  147: 
  148: 
  149: def _summary_card(label: str, value: int) -> str:
  150:     return f"<div class='summary-card'><strong>{value}</strong><span>{escape(label)}</span></div>"

Файл: src\file_compare_app\security\strict_mode.py
Комментарий: Файл проекта.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: import shutil
    4: import tempfile
    5: from dataclasses import dataclass
    6: from pathlib import Path
    7: 
    8: 
    9: @dataclass
   10: class StrictModeWorkspace:
   11:     root: Path | None = None
   12: 
   13:     def __post_init__(self) -> None:
   14:         base = self.root if self.root is not None else Path(tempfile.gettempdir())
   15:         self.path = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="file-compare-", dir=base))
   16: 
   17:     def __enter__(self) -> "StrictModeWorkspace":
   18:         return self
   19: 
   20:     def __exit__(self, exc_type: object, exc: object, tb: object) -> None:
   21:         shutil.rmtree(self.path, ignore_errors=True)
   22: 
   23: 
   24: def safe_log_message(analyzer: str, status: str) -> str:
   25:     clean_status = "failed" if "fail" in status.lower() or "error" in status.lower() else "ok"
   26:     return f"analyzer={analyzer} status={clean_status}"

   13:

====================================================================================================
Файл: src\file_compare_app\ui\compare_worker.py
Комментарий: Графический интерфейс PySide6 и пользовательские сценарии.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: from collections.abc import Callable
    4: from pathlib import Path
    5: 
    6: from PySide6.QtCore import QObject, Signal
    7: 
    8: from file_compare_app.analyzers.base import AnalyzerDependencyError
    9: from file_compare_app.core.models import ComparisonResult
   10: from file_compare_app.core.orchestrator import compare_files
   11: 
   12: 
   13: CompareFunc = Callable[[Path, Path], ComparisonResult]
   14: 
   15: 
   16: class CompareWorker(QObject):
   17:     progress = Signal(int, str)
   18:     finished = Signal(object)
   19:     failed = Signal(str, str)
   20:     canceled = Signal()
   21: 
   22:     def __init__(self, left_path: Path | str, right_path: Path | str, compare_func: CompareFunc = compare_files) -> None:
   23:         super().__init__()
   24:         self.left_path = Path(left_path)
   25:         self.right_path = Path(right_path)
   26:         self._compare_func = compare_func
   27:         self._cancel_requested = False
   28: 
   29:     def cancel(self) -> None:
   30:         self._cancel_requested = True
   31: 
   32:     def run(self) -> None:
   33:         if self._cancel_requested:
   34:             self.canceled.emit()
   35:             return
   36: 
   37:         self.progress.emit(10, "Подготовка файлов")
   38:         if self._cancel_requested:
   39:             self.canceled.emit()
   40:             return
   41: 
   42:         self.progress.emit(70, "Сравнение содержимого")
   43:         try:
   44:             result = self._compare_func(self.left_path, self.right_path)
   45:         except AnalyzerDependencyError as exc:
   46:             self.failed.emit("Не хватает зависимости", str(exc))
   47:             return
   48:         except Exception as exc:
   49:             self.failed.emit("Ошибка сравнения", f"Не удалось сравнить файлы: {exc.__class__.__name__}")
   50:             return
   51: 
   52:         if self._cancel_requested:
   53:             self.canceled.emit()
   54:             return
   55: 
   56:         self.progress.emit(100, "Готово")
   57:         self.finished.emit(result)

====================================================================================================
Файл: src\file_compare_app\ui\diff_view.py
Комментарий: Графический интерфейс PySide6 и пользовательские сценарии.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from __future__ import annotations
    2: 
    3: from html import escape
    4: from pathlib import Path
    5: 
    6: from file_compare_app.core.models import Change, ChangeLocation, ComparisonResult
    7: 
    8: 
    9: TEXTUAL_KINDS = {"text", "config"}
   10: CHANGE_LABELS = {
   11:     "added": "Добавлено",
   12:     "removed": "Удалено",
   13:     "modified": "Изменено",
   14: }
   15: 
   16: 
   17: def change_type_label(change_type: str) -> str:
   18:     return CHANGE_LABELS.get(change_type, change_type)
   19: 
   20: 
   21: def compact_location(location: ChangeLocation | None) -> str:
   22:     if location is None:
   23:         return ""
   24:     if location.sheet and location.cell:
   25:         return f"{location.sheet}!{location.cell}"
   26:     if location.page is not None and location.ocr_line is not None:
   27:         return f"стр. {location.page}, OCR {location.ocr_line}"
   28:     if location.page is not None:
   29:         return f"стр. {location.page}"
   30:     if location.line is not None and location.column is not None:
   31:         return f"строка {location.line}, колонка {location.column}"
   32:     if location.line is not None:
   33:         return f"строка {location.line}"
   34:     if location.byte_offset is not None and location.byte_length is not None:
   35:         return f"bytes {location.byte_offset}-{location.byte_offset + location.byte_length}"
   36:     if location.x is not None and location.y is not None and location.width is not None and location.height is not None:
   37:         return f"{location.x},{location.y} {location.width}x{location.height}"
   38:     return Path(location.path).name
   39: 
   40: 
   41: def render_result_html(result: ComparisonResult) -> tuple[str, str]:
   42:     if result.file_kind in TEXTUAL_KINDS:
   43:         left_lines = _read_display_lines(Path(result.left_path))
   44:         right_lines = _read_display_lines(Path(result.right_path))
   45:         return (
   46:             _render_lines(left_lines, _line_classes(result.changes, "left")),
   47:             _render_lines(right_lines, _line_classes(result.changes, "right")),
   48:         )
   49:     return _render_change_table(result, "left"), _render_change_table(result, "right")
   50: 
   51: 
   52: def _read_display_lines(path: Path) -> list[str]:
   53:     for encoding in ("utf-8-sig", "utf-8", "cp1251", "latin-1"):
   54:         try:
   55:             return path.read_text(encoding=encoding).splitlines()
   56:         except UnicodeDecodeError:
   57:             continue
   58:     return path.read_text(errors="replace").splitlines()
   59: 
   60: 
   61: def _line_classes(changes: list[Change], side: str) -> dict[int, tuple[str, str]]:
   62:     classes: dict[int, tuple[str, str]] = {}
   63:     for change in changes:
   64:         if side == "left":
   65:             location = change.source_location
   66:             if location is None or location.line is None:
   67:                 continue
   68:             if change.change_type == "removed":
   69:                 classes[location.line] = ("old", change_type_label(change.change_type))
   70:             elif change.change_type == "modified":
   71:                 classes[location.line] = ("old", change_type_label(change.change_type))
   72:         else:
   73:             location = change.target_location
   74:             if location is None or location.line is None:
   75:                 continue
   76:             if change.change_type == "added":
   77:                 classes[location.line] = ("added", change_type_label(change.change_type))
   78:             elif change.change_type == "modified":
   79:                 classes[location.line] = ("new", change_type_label(change.change_type))
   80:     return classes
   81: 
   82: 
   83: def _render_lines(lines: list[str], line_classes: dict[int, tuple[str, str]]) -> str:
   84:     rows = []
   85:     for index, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
   86:         css_class, label = line_classes.get(index, ("", ""))
   87:         badge = f"<span class='badge'>{escape(label)}</span>" if label else ""
   88:         rows.append(
   89:             f"<p class='line {css_class}'><span class='ln'>{index}</span>"
   90:             f"{badge}<span class='txt'>{escape(line)}</span></p>"
   91:         )
   92:     return _wrap_lines("".join(rows))
   93: 
   94: 
   95: def _render_change_table(result: ComparisonResult, side: str) -> str:
   96:     rows = []
   97:     for index, change in enumerate(result.changes, start=1):
   98:         value = change.before if side == "left" else change.after
   99:         css_class = "old" if side == "left" else "new"
  100:         if change.change_type == "added" and side == "left":
  101:             value = ""
  102:             css_class = ""
  103:         if change.change_type == "removed" and side == "right":
  104:             value = ""
  105:             css_class = ""
  106:         badge = f"<span class='badge'>{escape(change_type_label(change.change_type))}</span>" if value else ""
  107:         rows.append(
  108:             f"<p class='line {css_class}'><span class='ln'>{index}</span>"
  109:             f"{badge}<span class='txt'>{escape(value)}</span></p>"
  110:         )
  111:     if not rows:
  112:         rows.append("<p class='line'><span class='ln'>1</span><span class='txt'>Изменений не найдено</span></p>")
  113:     return _wrap_lines("".join(rows))
  114: 
  115: 
  116: def _wrap_lines(rows: str) -> str:
  117:     return f"""
  118:     <style>
  119:       body {{ margin: 0; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New'; font-size: 12px; color: #111827; }}
  120:       p.line {{
  121:         margin: 0;
  122:         padding: 4px 8px;
  123:         white-space: pre-wrap;
  124:         word-wrap: break-word;
  125:       }}
  126:       span {{
  127:         padding: 2px 6px;
  128:       }}
  129:       span.ln {{
  130:         display: inline-block;
  131:         min-width: 38px;
  132:         color: #8a95a8;
  133:         background: #f8fafc;
  134:         text-align: right;
  135:         border-right: 1px solid #eef2f7;
  136:       }}
  137:       span.badge {{
  138:         display: inline-block;
  139:         min-width: 72px;
  140:         margin: 0 6px;
  141:         border-radius: 6px;
  142:         text-align: center;
  143:         font-family: Segoe UI, Arial;
  144:         font-size: 11px;
  145:         font-weight: 700;
  146:         color: #344054;
  147:         background: #f2f4f7;
  148:       }}
  149:       span.txt {{
  150:         white-space: pre-wrap;
  151:         word-wrap: break-word;
  152:       }}
  153:       p.old {{ background: #fff1f0; color: #b42318; }}
  154:       p.new {{ background: #ecfdf3; color: #087443; }}
  155:       p.added {{ background: #ecfdf3; color: #087443; }}
  156:       p.warn {{ background: #fffaeb; color: #b54708; }}
  157:       p.focus {{ background: #eff6ff; color: #1d4ed8; }}
  158:     </style>
  159:     {rows}
  160:     """

  115:     def handle_file_path(self, path: Path | str) -> None:
  116:         file_path = Path(path)
  117:         if file_path.is_file():
  118:             self._on_file(file_path)
  119: 
  120:     def dragEnterEvent(self, event: QDragEnterEvent) -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
  121:         if self._first_local_path(event) is not None:
  122:             event.acceptProposedAction()
  123:         else:
  124:             event.ignore()
  125: 
  126:     def dropEvent(self, event: QDropEvent) -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
  127:         path = self._first_local_path(event)
  128:         if path is None:
  129:             event.ignore()
  130:             return
  131:         self.handle_file_path(path)
  132:         event.acceptProposedAction()
  133: 
  134:     @staticmethod
  135:     def _first_local_path(event: QDragEnterEvent | QDropEvent) -> Path | None:
  136:         mime_data = event.mimeData()
  137:         if not mime_data.hasUrls():
  138:             return None
  139:         for url in mime_data.urls():
  140:             if url.isLocalFile():
  141:                 return Path(url.toLocalFile())
  142:         return None
  143:

  201:     def _toggle_max_restore(self) -> None:
  202:         if self.window.isMaximized():
  203:             self.window.showNormal()
  204:         else:
  205:             self.window.showMaximized()
  206: 
  207:     def mousePressEvent(self, event) -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
  208:         if event.button() == Qt.LeftButton:
  209:             self.drag_position = event.globalPosition().toPoint() - self.window.frameGeometry().topLeft()
  210:             event.accept()
  211: 
  212:     def mouseMoveEvent(self, event) -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
  213:         if self.drag_position is not None and event.buttons() & Qt.LeftButton and not self.window.isMaximized():
  214:             self.window.move(event.globalPosition().toPoint() - self.drag_position)
  215:             event.accept()
  216: 
  217:     def mouseReleaseEvent(self, event) -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
  218:         self.drag_position = None
  219:         event.accept()
  220:

  222: class MainWindow(QMainWindow):

  224:         super().__init__()
  225:         self.left_path: Path | None = None
  226:         self.right_path: Path | None = None
  227:         self.result: ComparisonResult | None = None
  228:         self.compare_view_mode = "text"
  229:         self.change_filter = "all"
  230:         self.visible_changes: list[Change] = []
  231:         self.preview_left_html = ""
  232:         self.preview_right_html = ""
  233:         self.sync_scroll_enabled = True
  234:         self._syncing_scrollbars = False
  235:         self.compare_thread: QThread | None = None
  236:         self.compare_worker: CompareWorker | None = None
  237:         self.registry_repository = registry_repository or RegistryRepository.create()
  238:         self.registry_monitor = RegistryMonitor(self.registry_repository)
  239:         self.selected_registry_node_id: int | None = None
  240:         self.registry_search_query = ""
  241:         self.registry_status_filter_key = "all"
  242:         self.current_mode = "compare"
  243:         self.setWindowTitle("Сравнение файлов")
  244:         self.setWindowIcon(app_icon())
  245:         self.setWindowFlags(Qt.Window | Qt.FramelessWindowHint)
  246:         self.resize(1320, 820)
  247:         self.setMinimumSize(940, 620)
  248:         self._build_ui()

  306:     def resizeEvent(self, event) -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
  307:         super().resizeEvent(event)
  308:         if all(hasattr(self, name) for name in ("privacy_pill", "status_temp", "tech_label", "registry_search_box")):
  309:             self._apply_responsive_toolbar(event.size().width())
  310: 
  311:     def _apply_responsive_toolbar(self, width: int) -> None:
  312:         compact = width < 1320
  313:         very_compact = width < 960
  314:         mode = getattr(self, "current_mode", "compare")
  315: 
  316:         file_min = 180 if compact else 250
  317:         file_max = 240 if compact else 340
  318:         for button in (self.left_file_button, self.right_file_button):
  319:             button.setMinimumWidth(file_min)
  320:             button.setMaximumWidth(file_max)
  321: 
  322:         self.progress_bar.setFixedWidth(90 if compact else 120)
  323:         self.privacy_pill.setVisible(not compact)
  324:         self.status_temp.setVisible(not compact)
  325:         self.tech_label.setVisible(not very_compact)
  326:         self.registry_search_box.setVisible(mode == "registry" and not very_compact)
  327:         self.registry_search_box.setMinimumWidth(210 if compact else 280)
  328:         self.registry_search_box.setMaximumWidth(260 if compact else 16777215)
  329:         self.registry_status_filter.setVisible(mode == "registry" and not very_compact)
  330:         self.registry_status_filter.setMinimumWidth(120 if compact else 150)
  331:         self.registry_status_filter.setMaximumWidth(150 if compact else 180)
  332: 
  333:         self.mode_compare_button.setText("↔ Сравнение" if not very_compact else "↔")
  334:         self.mode_compare_button.setToolTip("Сравнение файлов")
  335:         self.mode_registry_button.setText("▦ Реестр объектов" if not very_compact else "▦ Реестр")
  336:         self.mode_registry_button.setToolTip("Реестр объектов")
  337: 
  338:         self.add_root_toolbar_button.setText("+ Объект")
  339:         self.add_child_button.setText("+ Подобъект" if not very_compact else "+ Под")
  340:         self.add_file_button.setText("+ Файл")
  341:         self.compare_registry_button.setText("Сравнить")
  342:         self.check_registry_button.setText("Проверить" if compact else "⟳ Проверить")
  343:         self.backup_registry_button.setText("Бэкап" if compact else "Бэкап БД")
  344:         self.export_registry_excel_button.setText("Excel")
  345:         self.delete_node_button.setText("Удалить")
  346:         self._refresh_file_chip_labels(compact, very_compact)
  347: 
  348:     def _refresh_file_chip_labels(self, compact: bool, very_compact: bool) -> None:
  349:         if self.left_path is None:
  350:             self.left_file_name.setText("До" if very_compact else "Исходный файл" if compact else "Выберите исходный файл")
  351:         if self.right_path is None:
  352:             self.right_file_name.setText("После" if very_compact else "Новая версия" if compact else "Выберите новую версию")
  353: 
  354:     def _create_message_box(
  355:         self,
  356:         icon: QMessageBox.Icon,
  357:         title: str,
  358:         message: str,
  359:         buttons: QMessageBox.StandardButton = QMessageBox.StandardButton.Ok,
  360:         default_button: QMessageBox.StandardButton = QMessageBox.StandardButton.NoButton,
  361:     ) -> QMessageBox:
  362:         box = QMessageBox(self)
  363:         box.setWindowIcon(app_icon())
  364:         box.setIcon(icon)
  365:         box.setWindowTitle(title)
  366:         box.setText(message)
  367:         box.setStandardButtons(buttons)
  368:         if default_button != QMessageBox.StandardButton.NoButton:
  369:             box.setDefaultButton(default_button)
  370:         return box
  371: 
  372:     def _show_message(self, icon: QMessageBox.Icon, title: str, message: str) -> QMessageBox.StandardButton:
  373:         return QMessageBox.StandardButton(self._create_message_box(icon, title, message).exec())
  374: 
  375:     def _ask_question(
  376:         self,
  377:         title: str,
  378:         message: str,
  379:         buttons: QMessageBox.StandardButton,
  380:         default_button: QMessageBox.StandardButton,
  381:     ) -> QMessageBox.StandardButton:
  382:         return QMessageBox.StandardButton(
  383:             self._create_message_box(QMessageBox.Icon.Question, title, message, buttons, default_button).exec()
  384:         )

  558:     def _file_chip(self, object_name: str, icon: str, name: str, note: str) -> tuple[DropFileButton, QLabel, QLabel]:
  559:         callback = self.assign_right_file if icon == "NEW" else self.assign_left_file
  560:         button = DropFileButton(object_name, icon, name, note, callback)
  561:         return button, button.name_label, button.note_label

  563:     def _build_workspace(self) -> QFrame:
  564:         workspace = QFrame()
  565:         workspace.setObjectName("workspace")
  566:         layout = QHBoxLayout(workspace)
  567:         layout.setContentsMargins(18, 16, 18, 16)
  568:         layout.setSpacing(14)
  569:         layout.addWidget(self._build_compare_area(), 1)
  570:         layout.addWidget(self._build_sidebar())
  571:         return workspace
  572: 
  573:     def _build_registry_workspace(self) -> QFrame:
  574:         workspace = QFrame()
  575:         workspace.setObjectName("registryWorkspace")
  576:         layout = QHBoxLayout(workspace)
  577:         layout.setContentsMargins(18, 16, 18, 16)
  578:         layout.setSpacing(14)
  579:         layout.addWidget(self._build_registry_tree_panel())
  580:         layout.addWidget(self._build_registry_detail_panel(), 1)
  581:         return workspace

  583:     def _build_registry_tree_panel(self) -> QFrame:
  584:         panel = QFrame()
  585:         panel.setObjectName("registryPanel")
  586:         panel.setFixedWidth(330)
  587:         layout = QVBoxLayout(panel)
  588:         layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0)
  589:         layout.setSpacing(0)
  590: 
  591:         header = QFrame()
  592:         header.setObjectName("summaryPanel")
  593:         header_layout = QHBoxLayout(header)
  594:         header_layout.setContentsMargins(14, 10, 14, 10)
  595:         title = QLabel("Реестр")
  596:         title.setObjectName("summaryTitle")
  597:         self.add_root_button = QToolButton()
  598:         self.add_root_button.setText("+")
  599:         self.add_root_button.setObjectName("iconButtonSmall")
  600:         header_layout.addWidget(title)
  601:         header_layout.addStretch(1)
  602:         header_layout.addWidget(self.add_root_button)
  603: 
  604:         self.registry_tree = QTreeWidget()

  606:         self.registry_tree.setHeaderHidden(True)
  607: 
  608:         layout.addWidget(header)
  609:         layout.addWidget(self.registry_tree, 1)
  610:         return panel

  835:     def _build_viewer(self, title: str, place: str) -> dict[str, QWidget]:
  836:         panel = QFrame()
  837:         panel.setObjectName("viewer")
  838:         panel_layout = QVBoxLayout(panel)
  839:         panel_layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0)
  840:         panel_layout.setSpacing(0)
  841: 
  842:         head = QFrame()
  843:         head.setObjectName("viewerHead")
  844:         head.setFixedHeight(34)
  845:         head_layout = QHBoxLayout(head)
  846:         head_layout.setContentsMargins(12, 0, 12, 0)
  847:         title_label = QLabel(title)
  848:         title_label.setObjectName("viewerTitle")
  849:         place_label = QLabel(place)
  850:         place_label.setObjectName("viewerPlace")
  851:         head_layout.addWidget(title_label)
  852:         head_layout.addStretch(1)
  853:         head_layout.addWidget(place_label)
  854: 
  855:         text = QTextEdit()
  856:         text.setObjectName("viewerBody")
  857:         text.setReadOnly(True)
  858:         text.setLineWrapMode(QTextEdit.WidgetWidth)
  859:         text.setWordWrapMode(QTextOption.WrapAtWordBoundaryOrAnywhere)
  860:         text.setFont(QFont("Consolas", 10))
  861: 
  862:         panel_layout.addWidget(head)
  863:         panel_layout.addWidget(text, 1)
  864:         return {"panel": panel, "text": text, "place": place_label}

  975:     def _set_mode(self, mode: str) -> None:
  976:         self.current_mode = mode
  977:         self.mode_stack.setCurrentIndex(1 if mode == "registry" else 0)
  978:         self.mode_compare_button.setProperty("active", mode == "compare")
  979:         self.mode_registry_button.setProperty("active", mode == "registry")
  980:         for widget in self.compare_toolbar_widgets:
  981:             widget.setVisible(mode == "compare")
  982:         for widget in self.registry_toolbar_widgets:
  983:             widget.setVisible(mode == "registry")
  984:         self.mode_compare_button.style().unpolish(self.mode_compare_button)
  985:         self.mode_compare_button.style().polish(self.mode_compare_button)
  986:         self.mode_registry_button.style().unpolish(self.mode_registry_button)
  987:         self.mode_registry_button.style().polish(self.mode_registry_button)
  988:         if hasattr(self, "privacy_pill"):
  989:             self._apply_responsive_toolbar(self.width())

  991:     def _on_registry_tree_selection(self, current: QTreeWidgetItem | None, previous: QTreeWidgetItem | None) -> None:
  992:         if current is None:
  993:             return
  994:         node_id = current.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
  995:         if isinstance(node_id, int) and hasattr(self, "select_registry_node"):
  996:             self.select_registry_node(node_id)
  997: 
  998:     def _create_root_node_dialog(self) -> None:
  999:         name, accepted = QInputDialog.getText(self, "Новый объект", "Название объекта:")
 1000:         if accepted and name.strip() and hasattr(self, "create_registry_node"):
 1001:             self.create_registry_node(name.strip())
 1002: 
 1003:     def _create_child_node_dialog(self) -> None:
 1004:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is None:
 1005:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Information, "Не выбран объект", "Выберите объект или подобъект в реестре.")
 1006:             return
 1007:         name, accepted = QInputDialog.getText(self, "Новый подобъект", "Название подобъекта:")
 1008:         if accepted and name.strip():
 1009:             child = self.create_registry_node(name.strip(), parent_id=self.selected_registry_node_id)
 1010:             self.select_registry_node(child.id)
 1011: 
 1012:     def _add_watched_file_dialog(self) -> None:
 1013:         self._add_registry_file_dialog()
 1014: 
 1015:     def _add_registry_file_dialog(self) -> None:
 1016:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is None:
 1017:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Information, "Не выбран объект", "Выберите объект или подобъект в реестре.")
 1018:             return
 1019:         title = "Выберите файл"
 1020:         if self._selected_watched_file_id() is not None:
 1021:             title = "Выберите новую версию файла"
 1022:         path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(self, title)
 1023:         if path:
 1024:             self.add_registry_file_to_selected_context(Path(path))
 1025: 
 1026:     def _add_before_file_dialog(self) -> None:
 1027:         self._add_registry_file_dialog()
 1028: 
 1029:     def _add_after_version_dialog(self) -> None:
 1030:         self._add_registry_file_dialog()
 1031: 
 1032:     def _confirm_delete_selected_registry_node(self) -> None:
 1033:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is None:
 1034:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Information, "Не выбран объект", "Выберите объект или подобъект в реестре.")
 1035:             return
 1036:         node = self.registry_repository.get_node(self.selected_registry_node_id)
 1037:         descendants = self.registry_repository.list_descendant_ids(node.id)
 1038:         answer = self._ask_question(
 1039:             "Удалить объект",
 1040:             f"Удалить «{node.name}» и все подобъекты ниже?\nБудет удалено записей: {len(descendants)}.",
 1041:             QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes | QMessageBox.StandardButton.No,
 1042:             QMessageBox.StandardButton.No,
 1043:         )
 1044:         if answer == QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes:
 1045:             self.delete_selected_registry_node()
 1046: 
 1047:     def create_registry_node(self, name: str, parent_id: int | None = None):
 1048:         node_type = "Подобъект" if parent_id is not None else "Объект"
 1049:         node = self.registry_repository.create_node(name=name, parent_id=parent_id, node_type=node_type)
 1050:         self.refresh_registry_tree()
 1051:         return node
 1052: 
 1053:     def refresh_registry_tree(self) -> None:
 1054:         self.registry_tree.clear()
 1055:         for node in self.registry_repository.list_children(None):
 1056:             if not self._node_matches_registry_search(node):
 1057:                 continue
 1058:             item = self._registry_tree_item(node)
 1059:             self.registry_tree.addTopLevelItem(item)
 1060:             self._append_registry_children(item, node.id)
 1061:         self.registry_tree.expandAll()
 1062: 
 1063:     def _append_registry_children(self, parent_item: QTreeWidgetItem, parent_id: int) -> None:
 1064:         for child in self.registry_repository.list_children(parent_id):
 1065:             if not self._node_matches_registry_search(child):
 1066:                 continue
 1067:             child_item = self._registry_tree_item(child)
 1068:             parent_item.addChild(child_item)
 1069:             self._append_registry_children(child_item, child.id)
 1070: 
 1071:     def _registry_tree_item(self, node) -> QTreeWidgetItem:
 1072:         item = QTreeWidgetItem([node.name])
 1073:         item.setData(0, Qt.UserRole, node.id)
 1074:         return item
 1075: 
 1076:     def set_registry_search_query(self, text: str) -> None:
 1077:         self.registry_search_query = text.strip().casefold()
 1078:         self.refresh_registry_tree()
 1079:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is not None:
 1080:             self._render_registry_files(self.selected_registry_node_id)
 1081:             self._render_registry_versions_for_current_file()
 1082: 
 1083:     def set_registry_status_filter(self, status: str) -> None:
 1084:         allowed = {"all", "ok", "changed", "missing", "error"}
 1085:         self.registry_status_filter_key = status if status in allowed else "all"
 1086:         if hasattr(self, "registry_status_filter"):
 1087:             index = self.registry_status_filter_combo_index(self.registry_status_filter_key)
 1088:             if index >= 0 and self.registry_status_filter.currentIndex() != index:
 1089:                 self.registry_status_filter.blockSignals(True)
 1090:                 self.registry_status_filter.setCurrentIndex(index)
 1091:                 self.registry_status_filter.blockSignals(False)
 1092:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is not None:
 1093:             self._render_registry_files(self.selected_registry_node_id)
 1094:             self._render_registry_versions_for_current_file()
 1095: 
 1096:     def registry_status_filter_combo_index(self, status: str) -> int:
 1097:         for index in range(self.registry_status_filter.count()):
 1098:             if self.registry_status_filter.itemData(index) == status:
 1099:                 return index
 1100:         return -1
 1101: 
 1102:     def _on_registry_status_filter_changed(self) -> None:
 1103:         status = self.registry_status_filter.currentData()
 1104:         self.set_registry_status_filter(status if isinstance(status, str) else "all")
 1105: 
 1106:     def _node_matches_registry_search(self, node) -> bool:
 1107:         query = self.registry_search_query
 1108:         if not query:
 1109:             return True
 1110:         node_text = " ".join(
 1111:             [
 1112:                 node.name,
 1113:                 node.node_type,
 1114:                 node.code,
 1115:                 node.responsible,
 1116:                 node.description,
 1117:             ]
 1118:         ).casefold()
 1119:         if query in node_text:
 1120:             return True
 1121:         for watched in self.registry_repository.list_watched_files(node.id):
 1122:             if query in f"{watched.label} {watched.file_path} {watched.file_kind} {watched.status}".casefold():
 1123:                 return True
 1124:         return any(self._node_matches_registry_search(child) for child in self.registry_repository.list_children(node.id))
 1125:

 1127:         self.selected_registry_node_id = node_id

 1129:         self.registry_object_title.setText(node.name)
 1130:         self._render_registry_node_card(node_id)
 1131:         self._render_registry_files(node_id)
 1132:         self._render_registry_events(node_id)
 1133:         self._render_registry_monitoring(node_id)
 1134:         self._render_registry_risks(node_id)
 1135:         self._render_registry_versions_for_current_file()

 1137:     def save_selected_registry_node_card(self) -> bool:
 1138:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is None:
 1139:             return False
 1140:         name = self.registry_node_name_input.text().strip()
 1141:         if not name:
 1142:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Warning, "Название не заполнено", "Укажите название объекта.")
 1143:             return False
 1144:         updated = self.registry_repository.update_node(
 1145:             self.selected_registry_node_id,
 1146:             name=name,
 1147:             code=self.registry_node_code_input.text().strip(),
 1148:             responsible=self.registry_node_responsible_input.text().strip(),
 1149:             description=self.registry_node_description_input.toPlainText().strip(),
 1150:             template_key=str(self.registry_node_template_input.currentData() or ""),
 1151:             monitor_interval_minutes=self.registry_monitor_interval_input.value(),
 1152:         )
 1153:         self.registry_object_title.setText(updated.name)
 1154:         self.refresh_registry_tree()
 1155:         self._render_registry_node_card(updated.id)
 1156:         self._render_registry_files(updated.id)
 1157:         self._render_registry_events(updated.id)
 1158:         self._render_registry_monitoring(updated.id)
 1159:         self._render_registry_risks(updated.id)
 1160:         self._render_registry_versions_for_current_file()
 1161:         self.status_text.setText(f"Карточка объекта сохранена: {updated.name}")
 1162:         return True

 1164:     def _render_registry_node_card(self, node_id: int | None) -> None:
 1165:         if node_id is None:
 1166:             self.registry_node_name_input.clear()
 1167:             self.registry_node_code_input.clear()
 1168:             self.registry_node_responsible_input.clear()
 1169:             self.registry_node_description_input.clear()
 1170:             self.registry_node_template_input.setCurrentIndex(0)
 1171:             self.registry_monitor_interval_input.setValue(30)
 1172:             self.registry_node_card_summary.setHtml(
 1173:                 _html_page("<div class='empty-state'><h2>Выберите объект</h2><p>Карточка появится после выбора объекта в реестре.</p></div>")
 1174:             )
 1175:             return
 1176: 
 1177:         node = self.registry_repository.get_node(node_id)
 1178:         self.registry_node_name_input.setText(node.name)
 1179:         self.registry_node_code_input.setText(node.code)
 1180:         self.registry_node_responsible_input.setText(node.responsible)
 1181:         self.registry_node_description_input.setPlainText(node.description)
 1182:         template_index = self.registry_node_template_input.findData(node.template_key)
 1183:         self.registry_node_template_input.setCurrentIndex(template_index if template_index >= 0 else 0)
 1184:         self.registry_monitor_interval_input.setValue(node.monitor_interval_minutes)
 1185: 
 1186:         descendants = self.registry_repository.list_descendant_ids(node_id)
 1187:         watched_files = self.registry_repository.list_watched_files_for_tree(node_id)
 1188:         events = self.registry_repository.list_events_for_tree(node_id)
 1189:         status_counts = {"ok": 0, "changed": 0, "missing": 0, "error": 0}
 1190:         version_count = 0
 1191:         for watched in watched_files:
 1192:             status_counts[watched.status] = status_counts.get(watched.status, 0) + 1
 1193:             version_count += len(self.registry_repository.list_file_versions(watched.id))
 1194: 
 1195:         self.registry_node_card_summary.setHtml(
 1196:             _html_page(
 1197:                 f"""
 1198:                 <h2>Карточка объекта</h2>
 1199:                 <div class='summary-grid'>
 1200:                     <div><b>Код</b><br>{escape(node.code or '-')}</div>
 1201:                     <div><b>Ответственный</b><br>{escape(node.responsible or '-')}</div>
 1202:                     <div><b>Подобъектов</b><br>{max(len(descendants) - 1, 0)}</div>
 1203:                     <div><b>Файлов</b><br>{len(watched_files)}</div>
 1204:                     <div><b>Версий</b><br>{version_count}</div>
 1205:                     <div><b>Событий</b><br>{len(events)}</div>
 1206:                 </div>
 1207:                 <div class='monitor-card'>
 1208:                     <div class='card-title'>{escape(node.name)}</div>
 1209:                     <div><b>Тип:</b> {escape(node.node_type)}</div>
 1210:                     <div><b>Шаблон:</b> {escape(_template_label(node.template_key))} | <b>Интервал:</b> {node.monitor_interval_minutes} мин</div>
 1211:                     <div><b>Описание:</b> {escape(node.description or 'не заполнено')}</div>
 1212:                     <div><b>Создан:</b> {escape(_format_registry_datetime(node.created_at))} | <b>Обновлен:</b> {escape(_format_registry_datetime(node.updated_at))}</div>
 1213:                 </div>
 1214:                 <div class='summary-grid'>
 1215:                     <div><b>OK</b><br>{status_counts.get('ok', 0)}</div>
 1216:                     <div><b>Изменено</b><br>{status_counts.get('changed', 0)}</div>
 1217:                     <div><b>Нет файла</b><br>{status_counts.get('missing', 0)}</div>

 1224:     def delete_selected_registry_node(self) -> bool:
 1225:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is None:
 1226:             return False
 1227:         node = self.registry_repository.get_node(self.selected_registry_node_id)
 1228:         parent_id = node.parent_id
 1229:         deleted_ids = self.registry_repository.delete_node(node.id)
 1230:         self.refresh_registry_tree()
 1231:         if parent_id is not None:
 1232:             try:
 1233:                 self.select_registry_node(parent_id)
 1234:             except KeyError:
 1235:                 self._clear_registry_selection()
 1236:         else:
 1237:             self._clear_registry_selection()
 1238:         self.status_text.setText(f"Удалено объектов: {len(deleted_ids)}")
 1239:         return True

 1241:     def _confirm_delete_selected_registry_file(self) -> None:
 1242:         watched_file_id = self._selected_watched_file_id()
 1243:         if watched_file_id is None:
 1244:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Information, "Не выбран файл", "Выберите файл в списке.")
 1245:             return
 1246:         watched = self.registry_repository.get_watched_file(watched_file_id)
 1247:         answer = self._ask_question(
 1248:             "Удалить файл",
 1249:             f"Удалить «{watched.label}» из реестра вместе с историей версий?",
 1250:             QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes | QMessageBox.StandardButton.No,
 1251:             QMessageBox.StandardButton.No,
 1252:         )
 1253:         if answer == QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes:
 1254:             self.delete_selected_registry_file()

 1256:     def delete_selected_registry_file(self) -> bool:

 1259:             return False

 1264:             self._render_registry_monitoring(self.selected_registry_node_id)
 1265:             self._render_registry_versions_for_current_file()
 1266:         self.status_text.setText(f"Файл удален из реестра: {deleted.label}")

 1295:     def add_registry_file_to_selected_context(self, path: Path | str):
 1296:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is None:
 1297:             raise RuntimeError("registry node is not selected")
 1298:         watched_file_id = self._selected_watched_file_id()

 1300:             watched = self.add_watched_file_to_selected_node(path)
 1301:             self._select_watched_file(watched.id)
 1302:             return watched
 1303:         return self.add_after_version_to_selected_registry_file(path)

 1315:         self._render_registry_versions_for_current_file()
 1316:         self.status_text.setText("Добавлена пара версий: файл до и файл после")
 1317:         return watched

 1329:             self._render_registry_versions_for_current_file()

 1358:     def _show_registry_file_context_menu(self, position: QPoint) -> None:
 1359:         row = self.registry_files_table.rowAt(position.y())
 1360:         if row >= 0:
 1361:             self.registry_files_table.setCurrentCell(row, 0)
 1362:             self.registry_files_table.selectRow(row)
 1363:         menu = self._build_registry_file_context_menu()
 1364:         menu.exec(self.registry_files_table.viewport().mapToGlobal(position))
 1365: 
 1366:     def _build_registry_file_context_menu(self) -> QMenu:
 1367:         menu = QMenu(self)
 1368:         compare_action = menu.addAction("Сравнить")
 1369:         compare_action.setEnabled(self._selected_registry_compare_pair() is not None)
 1370:         compare_action.triggered.connect(self.compare_selected_registry_file)
 1371: 
 1372:         export_action = menu.addAction("Экспорт отчета")
 1373:         export_action.setEnabled(self._selected_registry_compare_pair() is not None)
 1374:         export_action.triggered.connect(lambda checked=False: self.export_selected_registry_report())
 1375: 
 1376:         add_version_action = menu.addAction("Добавить новую версию")
 1377:         add_version_action.setEnabled(self.selected_registry_node_id is not None)
 1378:         add_version_action.triggered.connect(self._add_registry_file_dialog)
 1379: 
 1380:         check_action = menu.addAction("Проверить файл")
 1381:         check_action.setEnabled(self._selected_watched_file_id() is not None)
 1382:         check_action.triggered.connect(self.check_selected_registry_file)
 1383: 
 1384:         delete_action = menu.addAction("Удалить файл")
 1385:         delete_action.setEnabled(self._selected_watched_file_id() is not None)
 1386:         delete_action.triggered.connect(self._confirm_delete_selected_registry_file)
 1387:         return menu

 1389:     def compare_selected_registry_file(self) -> bool:
 1390:         pair = self._selected_registry_compare_pair()
 1391:         if pair is None:
 1392:             self._show_message(
 1393:                 QMessageBox.Icon.Information,
 1394:                 "Недостаточно версий",
 1395:                 "Выберите файл реестра, у которого есть минимум две версии: файл ДО и файл ПОСЛЕ.",
 1396:             )
 1397:             return False
 1398:         left_path, right_path = pair
 1399:         missing = [str(path) for path in (left_path, right_path) if not path.is_file()]
 1400:         if missing:
 1401:             self._show_message(
 1402:                 QMessageBox.Icon.Warning,
 1403:                 "Снимок версии не найден",
 1404:                 "Не найден сохраненный файл версии:\n" + "\n".join(missing),
 1405:             )
 1406:             return False
 1407:         self.assign_left_file(left_path)
 1408:         self.assign_right_file(right_path)
 1409:         self._set_mode("compare")
 1410:         self.status_text.setText("Сравнение запущено из реестра")
 1411:         self._compare()
 1412:         return True
 1413: 
 1414:     def export_selected_registry_report(self, path: Path | str | None = None) -> Path | None:
 1415:         pair = self._selected_registry_compare_pair()
 1416:         if pair is None:
 1417:             self._show_message(
 1418:                 QMessageBox.Icon.Information,
 1419:                 "Недостаточно версий",
 1420:                 "Выберите файл реестра, у которого есть минимум две версии.",
 1421:             )
 1422:             return None
 1423:         left_path, right_path = pair
 1424:         missing = [str(file_path) for file_path in (left_path, right_path) if not file_path.is_file()]
 1425:         if missing:
 1426:             self._show_message(
 1427:                 QMessageBox.Icon.Warning,
 1428:                 "Снимок версии не найден",
 1429:                 "Не найден сохраненный файл версии:\n" + "\n".join(missing),
 1430:             )
 1431:             return None
 1432:         if path is None:
 1433:             selected_path, _ = QFileDialog.getSaveFileName(
 1434:                 self,
 1435:                 "Сохранить отчет реестра",
 1436:                 "registry-comparison-report.html",
 1437:                 "HTML (*.html)",
 1438:             )
 1439:             if not selected_path:
 1440:                 return None
 1441:             path = selected_path
 1442:         output_path = Path(path)
 1443:         result = compare_files(left_path, right_path)
 1444:         output_path.write_text(render_html_report(result), encoding="utf-8")
 1445:         self.status_text.setText(f"Отчет реестра сохранен: {output_path}")
 1446:         return output_path

 1448:     def _backup_registry_database_dialog(self) -> None:

 1451:         if selected_dir:
 1452:             self.backup_registry_database(Path(selected_dir))

 1454:     def backup_registry_database(self, target_dir: Path | str | None = None) -> Path | None:
 1455:         try:
 1456:             backup_path = self.registry_repository.backup_database(target_dir)
 1457:         except Exception as exc:
 1458:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Warning, "Ошибка резервной копии", f"Не удалось создать резервную копию: {exc}")
 1459:             return None
 1460:         self.status_text.setText(f"Резервная копия БД создана: {backup_path}")
 1461:         return backup_path

 1474:     def export_registry_excel(self, path: Path | str | None = None) -> Path | None:
 1475:         if path is None:
 1476:             self._export_registry_excel_dialog()
 1477:             return None
 1478:         try:
 1479:             export_path = self.registry_repository.export_registry_excel(path)
 1480:         except Exception as exc:
 1481:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Warning, "Ошибка выгрузки", f"Не удалось выгрузить реестр: {exc}")
 1482:             return None
 1483:         self.status_text.setText(f"Реестр выгружен в Excel: {export_path}")
