 1486:     def _selected_registry_compare_pair(self) -> tuple[Path, Path] | None:
 1487:         row_meta = self._selected_registry_row_meta()
 1488:         if row_meta is not None:
 1489:             left_path = row_meta.get("left_path")
 1490:             right_path = row_meta.get("right_path")
 1491:             if isinstance(left_path, str) and isinstance(right_path, str):
 1492:                 return Path(left_path), Path(right_path)
 1493:         watched_file_id = self._selected_watched_file_id()
 1494:         if watched_file_id is None:
 1495:             return None
 1496:         versions = self.registry_repository.list_file_versions(watched_file_id)
 1497:         if len(versions) < 2:
 1498:             return None
 1499:         previous, latest = versions[-2], versions[-1]
 1500:         return Path(previous.snapshot_path), Path(latest.snapshot_path)
 1501: 
 1502:     def _refresh_registry_compare_action(self) -> None:
 1503:         self.compare_registry_button.setEnabled(self._selected_registry_compare_pair() is not None)
 1504: 
 1505:     def _render_registry_files(self, node_id: int) -> None:
 1506:         selected_meta = self._selected_registry_row_meta()
 1507:         selected_id = selected_meta.get("watched_id") if selected_meta is not None else None
 1508:         selected_to_version = selected_meta.get("to_version") if selected_meta is not None else None
 1509:         self.registry_files_table.setRowCount(0)
 1510:         row_to_select = 0
 1511:         for watched in self.registry_repository.list_watched_files(node_id):
 1512:             versions = self.registry_repository.list_file_versions(watched.id)
 1513:             if len(versions) >= 2:
 1514:                 version_pairs = list(zip(versions, versions[1:]))
 1515:             elif versions:
 1516:                 version_pairs = [(versions[0], None)]
 1517:             else:
 1518:                 version_pairs = [(None, None)]
 1519: 
 1520:             for before_version, after_version in version_pairs:
 1521:                 if before_version is not None:
 1522:                     before_text = _snapshot_display_name(before_version.snapshot_path)
 1523:                 else:
 1524:                     before_text = "Добавьте файл до"
 1525:                 if after_version is not None:
 1526:                     after_text = _snapshot_display_name(after_version.snapshot_path)
 1527:                     route_text = f"v{before_version.version_number} -> v{after_version.version_number}" if before_version else "-"
 1528:                     loaded_text = _format_registry_datetime(after_version.created_at)
 1529:                 elif before_version is not None:
 1530:                     after_text = "Добавьте файл после"
 1531:                     route_text = f"v{before_version.version_number}"
 1532:                     loaded_text = _format_registry_datetime(before_version.created_at)
 1533:                 else:
 1534:                     after_text = "Добавьте файл после"
 1535:                     route_text = "-"
 1536:                     loaded_text = "-"
 1537: 
 1538:                 if not self._watched_file_matches_registry_filters(watched, before_text, after_text, route_text, loaded_text):
 1539:                     continue
 1540: 
 1541:                 row = self.registry_files_table.rowCount()
 1542:                 row_meta = {
 1543:                     "watched_id": watched.id,
 1544:                     "from_version": before_version.version_number if before_version is not None else None,
 1545:                     "to_version": after_version.version_number if after_version is not None else None,
 1546:                     "left_path": before_version.snapshot_path if before_version is not None and after_version is not None else None,
 1547:                     "right_path": after_version.snapshot_path if after_version is not None else None,
 1548:                 }
 1549:                 self.registry_files_table.insertRow(row)
 1550:                 values = [
 1551:                     str(row + 1),
 1552:                     before_text,
 1553:                     after_text,
 1554:                     route_text,
 1555:                     _registry_status_text(watched.status),
 1556:                     loaded_text,
 1557:                 ]
 1558:                 for column, value in enumerate(values):
 1559:                     cell = QTableWidgetItem(value)
 1560:                     cell.setToolTip(
 1561:                         "\n".join(
 1562:                             [
 1563:                                 f"ID: {row + 1}",
 1564:                                 f"Файл: {watched.label}",
 1565:                                 f"Текущий путь: {watched.file_path}",
 1566:                                 f"Строка сверки: {route_text}",
 1567:                                 f"Версий: {len(versions)}",
 1568:                             ]
 1569:                         )
 1570:                     )
 1571:                     if column == 0:
 1572:                         cell.setData(Qt.UserRole, row_meta)
 1573:                     if column in {0, 3, 4}:
 1574:                         cell.setTextAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter)
 1575:                     elif column == 5:
 1576:                         cell.setTextAlignment(Qt.AlignRight | Qt.AlignVCenter)
 1577:                     if column == 4:
 1578:                         _apply_registry_status_style(cell, watched.status)
 1579:                     self.registry_files_table.setItem(row, column, cell)
 1580:                 self.registry_files_table.setRowHeight(row, 38)
 1581:                 if watched.id == selected_id and (
 1582:                     selected_to_version is None or selected_to_version == row_meta["to_version"]
 1583:                 ):
 1584:                     row_to_select = row
 1585:         if self.registry_files_table.rowCount():
 1586:             self.registry_files_stack.setCurrentWidget(self.registry_files_table)
 1587:             self.registry_files_table.setCurrentCell(row_to_select, 0)
 1588:             self.registry_files_table.selectRow(row_to_select)
 1589:         else:
 1590:             self.registry_files_stack.setCurrentWidget(self.registry_files_empty_state)
 1591:             if self.registry_repository.list_watched_files(node_id):
 1592:                 self._render_registry_files_empty_state(
 1593:                     "Ничего не найдено",
 1594:                     "Измените поиск или фильтр статуса, чтобы снова увидеть строки сверок.",
 1595:                 )
 1596:             else:
 1597:                 self._render_registry_files_empty_state(
 1598:                     "Загрузите первый файл",
 1599:                     "Нажмите '+ Файл'. Первая загрузка станет базовая версия v1. Следующая загрузка создаст строку сверки v1 -> v2.",
 1600:                 )
 1601:             self.registry_versions_panel.setPlainText("Добавьте файл до и файл после, чтобы начать историю версий.")
 1602:         self._render_selected_registry_pair_panel()
 1603:         self._refresh_registry_compare_action()
 1604: 
 1605:     def _render_registry_files_empty_state(self, title: str, message: str) -> None:
 1606:         self.registry_files_empty_state.setHtml(
 1607:             _html_page(
 1608:                 f"""
 1609:                 <div class='empty-state'>
 1610:                     <h2>{escape(title)}</h2>
 1611:                     <p>{escape(message)}</p>
 1612:                     <p class='hint'>Реестр хранит цепочку сверок: v1 -> v2, v2 -> v3 и дальше по порядку.</p>
 1613:                 </div>
 1614:                 """
 1615:             )
 1616:         )
 1617: 
 1618:     def _watched_file_matches_registry_filters(
 1619:         self,
 1620:         watched,
 1621:         before_text: str,
 1622:         after_text: str,
 1623:         route_text: str,
 1624:         loaded_text: str,
 1625:     ) -> bool:
 1626:         if self.registry_status_filter_key != "all" and watched.status != self.registry_status_filter_key:
 1627:             return False
 1628:         query = self.registry_search_query
 1629:         if not query:
 1630:             return True
 1631:         haystack = " ".join(
 1632:             [
 1633:                 watched.label,
 1634:                 watched.file_path,
 1635:                 watched.file_kind,
 1636:                 _registry_status_text(watched.status),
 1637:                 before_text,
 1638:                 after_text,
 1639:                 route_text,
 1640:                 loaded_text,
 1641:             ]
 1642:         ).casefold()
 1643:         return query in haystack
 1644: 
 1645:     def _selected_watched_file_id(self) -> int | None:
 1646:         row_meta = self._selected_registry_row_meta()
 1647:         if row_meta is not None:
 1648:             watched_file_id = row_meta.get("watched_id")
 1649:             return watched_file_id if isinstance(watched_file_id, int) else None
 1650: 
 1651:         return None
 1652: 
 1653:     def _selected_registry_row_meta(self) -> dict[str, object] | None:
 1654:         row = self.registry_files_table.currentRow()
 1655:         if row < 0:
 1656:             return None
 1657:         item = self.registry_files_table.item(row, 0)
 1658:         if item is None:
 1659:             return None
 1660:         row_data = item.data(Qt.UserRole)
 1661:         if isinstance(row_data, dict):
 1662:             return row_data
 1663:         if isinstance(row_data, int):
 1664:             return {"watched_id": row_data}
 1665:         return None
 1666: 
 1667:     def _select_watched_file(self, watched_file_id: int) -> None:
 1668:         row_to_select = -1
 1669:         for row in range(self.registry_files_table.rowCount()):
 1670:             item = self.registry_files_table.item(row, 0)
 1671:             if item is None:
 1672:                 continue
 1673:             row_data = item.data(Qt.UserRole)
 1674:             if isinstance(row_data, dict) and row_data.get("watched_id") == watched_file_id:
 1675:                 row_to_select = row
 1676:             elif row_data == watched_file_id:
 1677:                 row_to_select = row
 1678:         if row_to_select >= 0:
 1679:             self.registry_files_table.setCurrentCell(row_to_select, 0)
 1680:             self.registry_files_table.selectRow(row_to_select)
 1681: 
 1682:     def _render_registry_events(self, node_id: int) -> None:
 1683:         self.registry_events_list.clear()
 1684:         for event in self.registry_repository.list_events(node_id):
 1685:             self.registry_events_list.addItem(f"{event.created_at} | {event.event_type}\n{event.message}")
 1686:

 1689:         self._render_selected_registry_pair_panel()

 1691:     def _render_selected_registry_pair_panel(self) -> None:
 1692:         row = self.registry_files_table.currentRow()
 1693:         if row < 0 or self.registry_files_table.rowCount() == 0:
 1694:             self.registry_selected_pair_panel.setHtml(
 1695:                 _html_page(
 1696:                     """
 1697:                     <div class='selected-pair'>
 1698:                         <h2>Выбранная сверка</h2>
 1699:                         <p class='hint'>Выберите строку в таблице, чтобы увидеть файл до, файл после, версию, статус и действия.</p>
 1700:                     </div>
 1701:                     """
 1702:                 )
 1703:             )
 1704:             self._render_registry_review_controls()
 1705:             return
 1706: 
 1707:         def cell_text(column: int) -> str:
 1708:             item = self.registry_files_table.item(row, column)
 1709:             return item.text() if item is not None else "-"
 1710: 
 1711:         row_id = cell_text(0)
 1712:         before_text = cell_text(1)
 1713:         after_text = cell_text(2)
 1714:         route_text = cell_text(3)
 1715:         status_text = cell_text(4)
 1716:         loaded_text = cell_text(5)
 1717:         row_meta = self._selected_registry_row_meta()
 1718:         review_text = "Новое"
 1719:         if row_meta is not None and isinstance(row_meta.get("watched_id"), int) and isinstance(row_meta.get("from_version"), int) and isinstance(row_meta.get("to_version"), int):
 1720:             review = self.registry_repository.get_comparison_review(
 1721:                 row_meta["watched_id"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 1722:                 row_meta["from_version"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 1723:                 row_meta["to_version"],  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 1724:             )
 1725:             review_text = _review_status_text(review.status)
 1726:         self.registry_selected_pair_panel.setHtml(
 1727:             _html_page(
 1728:                 f"""
 1729:                 <div class='selected-pair'>
 1730:                     <h2>Выбранная сверка</h2>
 1731:                     <div class='summary-grid'>
 1732:                         <div><b>ID {escape(row_id)}</b><br>{escape(route_text)}</div>
 1733:                         <div><b>Статус</b><br>{escape(status_text)}</div>
 1734:                         <div><b>Согласование</b><br>{escape(review_text)}</div>
 1735:                         <div><b>Загружено</b><br>{escape(loaded_text)}</div>
 1736:                     </div>
 1737:                     <div class='monitor-card'>
 1738:                         <div><b>Файл до:</b> {escape(before_text)}</div>
 1739:                         <div><b>Файл после:</b> {escape(after_text)}</div>
 1740:                         <div class='hint'>Действия: Сравнить | Экспорт отчета | Добавить новую версию</div>
 1741:                     </div>
 1742:                 </div>
 1743:                 """
 1744:             )
 1745:         )
 1746:         self._render_registry_review_controls()

 1748:     def _render_registry_review_controls(self) -> None:
 1749:         row_meta = self._selected_registry_row_meta()
 1750:         watched_id = row_meta.get("watched_id") if row_meta else None
 1751:         from_version = row_meta.get("from_version") if row_meta else None
 1752:         to_version = row_meta.get("to_version") if row_meta else None
 1753:         enabled = isinstance(watched_id, int) and isinstance(from_version, int) and isinstance(to_version, int)
 1754:         for widget in (
 1755:             self.registry_review_status_input,
 1756:             self.registry_review_reviewer_input,
 1757:             self.registry_review_comment_input,
 1758:             self.save_registry_review_button,
 1759:         ):
 1760:             widget.setEnabled(enabled)
 1761:         if not enabled:
 1762:             self.registry_review_status_input.setCurrentIndex(0)
 1763:             self.registry_review_reviewer_input.clear()
 1764:             self.registry_review_comment_input.clear()
 1765:             return
 1766:         review = self.registry_repository.get_comparison_review(watched_id, from_version, to_version)
 1767:         status_index = self.registry_review_status_input.findData(review.status)
 1768:         self.registry_review_status_input.setCurrentIndex(status_index if status_index >= 0 else 0)
 1769:         self.registry_review_reviewer_input.setText(review.reviewer)
 1770:         self.registry_review_comment_input.setPlainText(review.comment)
 1771: 
 1772:     def save_selected_registry_review(self) -> bool:
 1773:         row_meta = self._selected_registry_row_meta()
 1774:         if row_meta is None:
 1775:             return False
 1776:         watched_id = row_meta.get("watched_id")
 1777:         from_version = row_meta.get("from_version")
 1778:         to_version = row_meta.get("to_version")
 1779:         if not isinstance(watched_id, int) or not isinstance(from_version, int) or not isinstance(to_version, int):
 1780:             return False
 1781:         self.registry_repository.upsert_comparison_review(
 1782:             watched_id,
 1783:             from_version,
 1784:             to_version,
 1785:             status=str(self.registry_review_status_input.currentData() or "new"),
 1786:             reviewer=self.registry_review_reviewer_input.text().strip(),
 1787:             comment=self.registry_review_comment_input.toPlainText().strip(),
 1788:         )
 1789:         self._render_selected_registry_pair_panel()
 1790:         if self.selected_registry_node_id is not None:
 1791:             self._render_registry_files(self.selected_registry_node_id)
 1792:         self.status_text.setText("Статус сверки сохранен")
 1793:         return True
 1794: 
 1795:     def _render_registry_versions_for_current_file(self) -> None:
 1796:         self._refresh_registry_compare_action()
 1797:         watched_file_id = self._selected_watched_file_id()
 1798:         if watched_file_id is None:
 1799:             self.registry_versions_panel.setPlainText("Выберите файл в списке, чтобы увидеть его версии.")
 1800:             return
 1801:         watched = self.registry_repository.get_watched_file(watched_file_id)
 1802:         versions = self.registry_repository.list_file_versions(watched_file_id)
 1803:         version_cards: list[str] = []
 1804:         transition_cards: list[str] = []
 1805:         if not versions:
 1806:             version_cards.append("<div class='version-card'>Версии пока не сохранены.</div>")
 1807:         if len(versions) < 2:
 1808:             transition_cards.append("<div class='version-card'>Загрузите файл после, чтобы появилась первая сверка.</div>")
 1809:         for previous, current in zip(versions, versions[1:]):
 1810:             transition_cards.append(
 1811:                 "<div class='version-card'>"
 1812:                 f"<div class='card-title'>Сверка v{previous.version_number} -> v{current.version_number}</div>"
 1813:                 f"<div><b>Файл до:</b> {escape(_snapshot_display_name(previous.snapshot_path))}</div>"
 1814:                 f"<div><b>Файл после:</b> {escape(_snapshot_display_name(current.snapshot_path))}</div>"
 1815:                 f"<div><b>Изменений:</b> {current.change_count}</div>"
 1816:                 f"<div><b>Загружено:</b> {escape(_format_registry_datetime(current.created_at))}</div>"
 1817:                 "</div>"
 1818:             )
 1819:         for version in versions:
 1820:             version_cards.append(
 1821:                 "<div class='version-card'>"
 1822:                 f"<div class='card-title'>v{version.version_number}</div>"
 1823:                 f"<div>Размер: {version.size_bytes} байт</div>"
 1824:                 f"<div>Изменений: {version.change_count}</div>"
 1825:                 f"<div>Сохранено: {escape(version.created_at)}</div>"
 1826:                 f"<div class='path'>Снимок: {escape(version.snapshot_path)}</div>"
 1827:                 "</div>"
 1828:             )
 1829:         self.registry_versions_panel.setHtml(
 1830:             _html_page(
 1831:                 f"""
 1832:                 <h2>Файл: {escape(watched.label)}</h2>
 1833:                 <div class='summary-grid'>
 1834:                     <div><b>Статус</b><br>{escape(_registry_status_text(watched.status))}</div>
 1835:                     <div><b>Версий: {len(versions)}</b><br>цепочка v1 -> vN</div>
 1836:                 </div>
 1837:                 <p><b>Текущий путь:</b><br><span class='path'>{escape(watched.file_path)}</span></p>
 1838:                 <p class='hint'>v1 остается базовым файлом ДО. Каждая следующая версия хранит новый файл ПОСЛЕ и сравнивается с предыдущей версией.</p>
 1839:                 <h2>Цепочка сверок</h2>
 1840:                 {''.join(transition_cards)}
 1841:                 <h2>Снимки версий</h2>
 1842:                 {''.join(version_cards)}
 1843:                 """
 1844:             )
 1845:         )

 1847:     def _render_registry_monitoring(self, node_id: int) -> None:
 1848:         summary = self.registry_monitor.build_node_summary(node_id)
 1849:         cards: list[str] = []
 1850:         problem_cards: list[str] = []
 1851:         if not summary.files:
 1852:             cards.append(
 1853:                 "<div class='monitor-card'>Файлы для мониторинга пока не добавлены.<br>"
 1854:                 "Начните с кнопки '+ Файл': первая загрузка станет базовой версией v1.</div>"
 1855:             )
 1856:         for item in summary.files:
 1857:             watched = item.watched_file
 1858:             version = item.latest_version
 1859:             event = item.last_event
 1860:             version_text = f"v{version.version_number}" if version is not None else "версий нет"
 1861:             hash_text = version.sha256[:12] if version is not None else "-"
 1862:             changes_text = str(version.change_count) if version is not None else "0"
 1863:             checked_at = watched.last_checked_at or "еще не проверялся"
 1864:             last_event = f"{event.event_type}; {event.message}" if event is not None else "событий пока нет"
 1865:             card = (
 1866:                 "<div class='monitor-card'>"
 1867:                 f"<div class='card-title'>{escape(watched.label)}</div>"
 1868:                 f"<div><span class='badge'>{escape(_registry_status_text(watched.status))}</span>"
 1869:                 f" <b>Объект:</b> {escape(item.node_path)}</div>"
 1870:                 f"<div><b>Текущая версия:</b> {escape(version_text)} | "
 1871:                 f"<b>Изменений:</b> {escape(changes_text)} | <b>hash:</b> {escape(hash_text)}</div>"
 1872:                 f"<div><b>Последняя проверка:</b> {escape(checked_at)}</div>"
 1873:                 f"<div class='path'><b>Текущий файл после:</b> {escape(watched.file_path)}</div>"
 1874:                 f"<div><b>Последнее событие:</b> {escape(last_event)}</div>"
 1875:                 "</div>"
 1876:             )
 1877:             cards.append(card)
 1878:             if watched.status != "ok":
 1879:                 problem_cards.append(card)
 1880:         if not problem_cards:
 1881:             problem_cards.append("<div class='monitor-card'>Проблемных файлов нет.</div>")
 1882:         self.registry_monitoring_panel.setHtml(
 1883:             _html_page(
 1884:                 f"""
 1885:                 <h2>Панель мониторинга</h2>
 1886:                 <p class='hint'>Проверяется выбранный объект и все его подобъекты. Файлов под контролем: {summary.total_files}</p>
 1887:                 <div class='summary-grid'>
 1888:                     <div><b>Всего файлов</b><br>{summary.total_files}</div>
 1889:                     <div><b>OK</b><br>{summary.status_counts['ok']}</div>
 1890:                     <div><b>Изменено</b><br>{summary.status_counts['changed']}</div>
 1891:                     <div><b>Нет файла</b><br>{summary.status_counts['missing']}</div>
 1892:                     <div><b>Ошибка</b><br>{summary.status_counts['error']}</div>
 1893:                 </div>
 1894:                 <h2>Проблемные файлы</h2>
 1895:                 {''.join(problem_cards)}
 1896:                 <h2>Все файлы</h2>
 1897:                 {''.join(cards)}
 1898:                 """
 1899:             )
 1900:         )
 1901: 
 1902:     def _render_registry_risks(self, node_id: int) -> None:
 1903:         risk_events = [event for event in self.registry_repository.list_events_for_tree(node_id) if event.risk_count > 0]
 1904:         total_risks = sum(event.risk_count for event in risk_events)
 1905:         if not risk_events:
 1906:             self.registry_risks_panel.setHtml(
 1907:                 _html_page(
 1908:                     """
 1909:                     <h2>Риски</h2>
 1910:                     <div class='monitor-card'>Критичных изменений по выбранному объекту пока нет.</div>
 1911:                     """
 1912:                 )
 1913:             )
 1914:             return
 1915:         cards = []
 1916:         for event in risk_events[:30]:
 1917:             cards.append(
 1918:                 "<div class='monitor-card'>"
 1919:                 f"<div class='card-title'>{escape(event.event_type)} | рисков: {event.risk_count}</div>"
 1920:                 f"<div><b>Событие:</b> {escape(event.message)}</div>"
 1921:                 f"<div><b>Риск:</b> {escape(event.risk_summary)}</div>"
 1922:                 f"<div><b>Дата:</b> {escape(_format_registry_datetime(event.created_at))}</div>"
 1923:                 "</div>"
 1924:             )
 1925:         self.registry_risks_panel.setHtml(
 1926:             _html_page(
 1927:                 f"""
 1928:                 <h2>Риски</h2>
 1929:                 <div class='summary-grid'>
 1930:                     <div><b>Всего рисков</b><br>{total_risks}</div>
 1931:                     <div><b>Событий с риском</b><br>{len(risk_events)}</div>
 1932:                 </div>
 1933:                 {''.join(cards)}
 1934:                 """
 1935:             )
 1936:         )

 1938:     def _apply_style(self) -> None:
 1939:         self.setStyleSheet(
 1940:             """
 1941:             QWidget#appShell { background: #eef2f6; color: #111827; font-family: Segoe UI, Arial; }
 1942:             QFrame#titleBar { background: #111827; color: #f9fafb; }
 1943:             QLabel#brandMark {

 2431:     def _render_empty_preview(self) -> None:
 2432:         left_html = self._lines_html(
 2433:             [
 2434:                 ("38", "4.1. Исполнитель обязуется выполнить работы в срок.", ""),
 2435:                 ("39", "4.2. Заказчик предоставляет исходные данные.", ""),
 2436:                 ("40", "4.3. Срок оплаты составляет 10 банковских дней.", "old"),
 2437:                 ("41", "4.4. Штраф за просрочку составляет 0,05% за каждый день.", "focus"),
 2438:                 ("42", "4.5. Все приложения являются частью договора.", ""),
 2439:                 ("43", "OCR confidence: 91%", "warn"),
 2440:             ]
 2441:         )
 2442:         right_html = self._lines_html(
 2443:             [
 2444:                 ("38", "4.1. Исполнитель обязуется выполнить работы в срок.", ""),
 2445:                 ("39", "4.2. Заказчик предоставляет исходные данные.", ""),
 2446:                 ("40", "4.3. Срок оплаты составляет 7 банковских дней.", "new"),
 2447:                 ("41", "4.4. Штраф за просрочку составляет 0,1% за каждый день.", "focus"),
 2448:                 ("42", "4.5. Все приложения являются частью договора.", ""),
 2449:                 ("43", "OCR confidence: 88%", "warn"),
 2450:             ]
 2451:         )
 2452:         self.preview_left_html = left_html
 2453:         self.preview_right_html = right_html
 2454:         self.left_view["text"].setHtml(left_html)
 2455:         self.right_view["text"].setHtml(right_html)
 2456:         self._populate_demo_changes()
 2457: 
 2458:     def _refresh_button_group(self, buttons: dict[str, QPushButton], active_key: str) -> None:
 2459:         for key, button in buttons.items():
 2460:             button.setProperty("active", key == active_key)
 2461:             button.style().unpolish(button)
 2462:             button.style().polish(button)
 2463: 
 2464:     def _set_sync_scroll_enabled(self, enabled: bool) -> None:
 2465:         self.sync_scroll_enabled = enabled
 2466: 
 2467:     def _connect_sync_scrollbars(self) -> None:
 2468:         self.left_view["text"].verticalScrollBar().valueChanged.connect(
 2469:             lambda value: self._sync_scrollbar("left", "vertical", value)
 2470:         )
 2471:         self.right_view["text"].verticalScrollBar().valueChanged.connect(
 2472:             lambda value: self._sync_scrollbar("right", "vertical", value)
 2473:         )
 2474:         self.left_view["text"].horizontalScrollBar().valueChanged.connect(
 2475:             lambda value: self._sync_scrollbar("left", "horizontal", value)
 2476:         )
 2477:         self.right_view["text"].horizontalScrollBar().valueChanged.connect(
 2478:             lambda value: self._sync_scrollbar("right", "horizontal", value)
 2479:         )
 2480: 
 2481:     def _sync_scrollbar(self, source: str, orientation: str, value: int) -> None:
 2482:         if not self.sync_scroll_enabled or self._syncing_scrollbars:
 2483:             return
 2484:         source_text = self.left_view["text"] if source == "left" else self.right_view["text"]
 2485:         target_text = self.right_view["text"] if source == "left" else self.left_view["text"]
 2486:         source_bar = source_text.verticalScrollBar() if orientation == "vertical" else source_text.horizontalScrollBar()
 2487:         target_bar = target_text.verticalScrollBar() if orientation == "vertical" else target_text.horizontalScrollBar()
 2488:         if source_bar.maximum() <= 0:
 2489:             target_value = 0
 2490:         else:
 2491:             target_value = round((value / source_bar.maximum()) * target_bar.maximum())
 2492:         self._syncing_scrollbars = True
 2493:         try:
 2494:             target_bar.setValue(max(0, min(target_bar.maximum(), target_value)))
 2495:         finally:
 2496:             self._syncing_scrollbars = False
 2497: 
 2498:     def set_compare_view_mode(self, mode: str) -> None:
 2499:         if mode not in self.compare_tab_buttons:
 2500:             return
 2501:         self.compare_view_mode = mode
 2502:         self._refresh_button_group(self.compare_tab_buttons, mode)
 2503:         self._render_compare_view_mode()
 2504: 
 2505:     def set_change_filter(self, filter_key: str) -> None:
 2506:         if filter_key not in self.change_filter_buttons:
 2507:             return
 2508:         self.change_filter = filter_key
 2509:         self._refresh_button_group(self.change_filter_buttons, filter_key)
 2510:         self._render_change_list()
 2511: 
 2512:     def _render_compare_view_mode(self) -> None:
 2513:         if self.result is None:
 2514:             if self.compare_view_mode == "text":
 2515:                 self.left_view["text"].setHtml(self.preview_left_html)
 2516:                 self.right_view["text"].setHtml(self.preview_right_html)
 2517:             else:
 2518:                 message = {
 2519:                     "pages": "Нет постраничных данных",
 2520:                     "ocr": "Нет OCR-данных",
 2521:                     "hex": "Нет hex-данных",
 2522:                 }.get(self.compare_view_mode, "Нет данных")
 2523:                 self.left_view["text"].setPlainText(message)
 2524:                 self.right_view["text"].setPlainText(message)
 2525:             return
 2526: 
 2527:         if self.compare_view_mode == "text":
 2528:             left_html, right_html = render_result_html(self.result)
 2529:         else:
 2530:             left_html, right_html = self._render_mode_changes(self._changes_for_compare_mode(self.compare_view_mode))
 2531:         self.left_view["text"].setHtml(left_html)
 2532:         self.right_view["text"].setHtml(right_html)
 2533: 
 2534:     def _changes_for_compare_mode(self, mode: str) -> list[Change]:
 2535:         if self.result is None:
 2536:             return []
 2537:         if mode == "text":
 2538:             return self.result.changes
 2539:         if mode == "pages":
 2540:             return [change for change in self.result.changes if self._change_has_page_location(change)]
 2541:         if mode == "ocr":
 2542:             return [
 2543:                 change
 2544:                 for change in self.result.changes
 2545:                 if change.format.lower() == "ocr"
 2546:                 or "ocr" in change.notes.lower()
 2547:                 or any(location and location.ocr_line is not None for location in (change.source_location, change.target_location))
 2548:             ]
 2549:         if mode == "hex":
 2550:             return [
 2551:                 change
 2552:                 for change in self.result.changes
 2553:                 if change.format.lower() in {"hex", "binary"}
 2554:                 or any(location and location.byte_offset is not None for location in (change.source_location, change.target_location))
 2555:             ]
 2556:         return self.result.changes
 2557: 
 2558:     @staticmethod
 2559:     def _change_has_page_location(change: Change) -> bool:
 2560:         return any(location and location.page is not None for location in (change.source_location, change.target_location))
 2561: 
 2562:     def _render_mode_changes(self, changes: list[Change]) -> tuple[str, str]:
 2563:         if not changes:
 2564:             empty = self._lines_html([("1", "Данных для этого вида не найдено", "warn")])
 2565:             return empty, empty
 2566:         left_rows: list[tuple[str, str, str]] = []
 2567:         right_rows: list[tuple[str, str, str]] = []
 2568:         for index, change in enumerate(changes, start=1):
 2569:             left_place = compact_location(change.source_location)
 2570:             right_place = compact_location(change.target_location)
 2571:             left_text = f"{left_place} {change.before}".strip()
 2572:             right_text = f"{right_place} {change.after}".strip()
 2573:             left_rows.append((str(index), left_text, "old" if change.before else ""))
 2574:             right_rows.append((str(index), right_text, "new" if change.after else ""))
 2575:         return self._lines_html(left_rows), self._lines_html(right_rows)
 2576: 
 2577:     def _render_change_list(self) -> None:
 2578:         if self.result is None:
 2579:             return
 2580:         self.changes_list.clear()
 2581:         self.visible_changes = [change for change in self.result.changes if self._change_matches_filter(change)]
 2582:         for change in self.visible_changes:
 2583:             place = compact_location(change.target_location or change.source_location)
 2584:             self.changes_list.addItem(
 2585:                 QListWidgetItem(f"{change_type_label(change.change_type)}\n{place}\n- {change.before}\n+ {change.after}")
 2586:             )
 2587:         if self.visible_changes:
 2588:             self.changes_list.setCurrentRow(0)
 2589: 
 2590:     def _change_matches_filter(self, change: Change) -> bool:
 2591:         if self.change_filter == "all":
 2592:             return True
 2593:         if self.change_filter == "text":
 2594:             return (
 2595:                 change.format.lower() in {"text", "config", "docx", "pdf", "xlsx"}
 2596:                 or any(location and location.line is not None for location in (change.source_location, change.target_location))
 2597:             )
 2598:         if self.change_filter == "ocr":
 2599:             return change in self._changes_for_compare_mode("ocr")
 2600:         if self.change_filter == "risk":
 2601:             return change.severity == "risk" or "risk" in change.notes.lower() or "риск" in change.notes.lower()
 2602:         return True
 2603: 
 2604:     def _lines_html(self, rows: list[tuple[str, str, str]]) -> str:
 2605:         style = """
 2606:         <style>
 2607:           body { margin: 0; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New'; font-size: 12px; color: #111827; }
 2608:           table { border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; }
 2609:           td { padding: 4px 8px; white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; }
 2610:           td.ln { width: 38px; color: #8a95a8; background: #f8fafc; text-align: right; border-right: 1px solid #eef2f7; }
 2611:           tr.old td.txt { background: #fff1f0; color: #b42318; }
 2612:           tr.new td.txt { background: #ecfdf3; color: #087443; }
 2613:           tr.warn td.txt { background: #fffaeb; color: #b54708; }
 2614:           tr.focus td.txt { background: #eff6ff; color: #1d4ed8; outline: 2px solid rgba(37,99,235,.45); }
 2615:         </style>
 2616:         """
 2617:         body = "".join(f"<tr class='{cls}'><td class='ln'>{line}</td><td class='txt'>{text}</td></tr>" for line, text, cls in rows)
 2618:         return f"{style}<table>{body}</table>"
 2619: 
 2620:     def _populate_demo_changes(self) -> None:

 2622:         for text in (
 2623:             "Срок оплаты\nстр. 4, строка 40\n- 10 банковских дней\n+ 7 банковских дней",
 2624:             "Штраф\nстр. 4, строка 41\n- 0,05% за каждый день\n+ 0,1% за каждый день",
 2625:             "Новый пункт\nстр. 7, строка 82\n+ электронный документооборот",
 2626:             "Config key\napp.yaml:18\n- timeout: 30\n+ timeout: 45",
 2627:         ):
 2628:             self.changes_list.addItem(QListWidgetItem(text))
 2629:         self.changes_list.setCurrentRow(0)

 2652: 
 2653:     @staticmethod
 2654:     def _file_note(path: Path) -> str:
 2655:         suffix = path.suffix.upper().lstrip(".") or "FILE"
 2656:         try:
 2657:             size = path.stat().st_size
 2658:         except OSError:
 2659:             size = 0
 2660:         return f"{suffix} | {MainWindow._format_size(size)}"
 2661: 
 2662:     @staticmethod
 2663:     def _format_size(size: int) -> str:
 2664:         units = ("B", "KB", "MB", "GB")
 2665:         value = float(size)
 2666:         for unit in units:
 2667:             if value < 1024 or unit == units[-1]:
 2668:                 return f"{int(value)} {unit}" if unit == "B" else f"{value:.1f} {unit}"
 2669:             value /= 1024
 2670:         return f"{size} B"
 2671: 
 2672:     def _compare(self) -> None:
 2673:         if self.left_path is None or self.right_path is None:
 2674:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Warning, "Не выбраны файлы", "Выберите два файла для сравнения.")
 2675:             return
 2676:         if self.compare_thread is not None:
 2677:             return
 2678: 
 2679:         self._set_compare_busy(True)
 2680:         self.compare_thread = QThread(self)
 2681:         self.compare_worker = CompareWorker(self.left_path, self.right_path)
 2682:         self.compare_worker.moveToThread(self.compare_thread)
 2683: 
 2684:         self.compare_thread.started.connect(self.compare_worker.run)
 2685:         self.compare_worker.progress.connect(self._on_compare_progress)
 2686:         self.compare_worker.finished.connect(self._on_compare_finished)
 2687:         self.compare_worker.failed.connect(self._on_compare_failed)
 2688:         self.compare_worker.canceled.connect(self._on_compare_canceled)
 2689:         self.compare_worker.finished.connect(self.compare_thread.quit)
 2690:         self.compare_worker.failed.connect(self.compare_thread.quit)
 2691:         self.compare_worker.canceled.connect(self.compare_thread.quit)
 2692:         self.compare_thread.finished.connect(self.compare_worker.deleteLater)
 2693:         self.compare_thread.finished.connect(self._clear_compare_worker)
 2694:         self.compare_thread.start()
 2695: 
 2696:     def _set_compare_busy(self, busy: bool) -> None:
 2697:         self.compare_button.setEnabled(not busy)

 2705:             self.status_text.setText("Сравнение запущено")

 2718:     def _on_compare_finished(self, result: object) -> None:

 2730:         if title == "Не хватает зависимости":
 2731:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Warning, title, message)
 2732:         else:
 2733:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Critical, title, message)

 2750:     def _render_result(self, result: ComparisonResult) -> None:
 2751:         self.result = result
 2752:         self.summary.setText(f"Найдено {result.change_count} изменений")
 2753:         removed = sum(_removed_metric_count(change) for change in result.changes)
 2754:         added = sum(_added_metric_count(change) for change in result.changes)
 2755:         ocr = sum(1 for change in result.changes if change.format == "ocr" or "OCR" in change.notes)
 2756:         self.removed_stat.number_label.setText(str(removed))  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
 2757:         self.added_stat.number_label.setText(str(added))  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
 2758:         self.ocr_stat.number_label.setText(str(ocr))  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
 2759:         self._render_change_list()
 2760:         self._render_compare_view_mode()
 2761:         if result.changes:
 2762:             self.changes_list.setCurrentRow(0)
 2763:         else:
 2764:             self.left_view["text"].setPlainText("Изменений не найдено")
 2765:             self.right_view["text"].setPlainText("Изменений не найдено")
 2766:         self.status_ready.setText("Готово")
 2767:         self.status_text.setText("Сравнение выполнено локально")
 2768: 
 2769:     def _show_change(self, row: int) -> None:
 2770:         if self.result is None or row < 0 or row >= len(self.visible_changes):
 2771:             return
 2772:         change = self.visible_changes[row]
 2773:         if change.source_location:
 2774:             self.left_view["place"].setText(compact_location(change.source_location))
 2775:         if change.target_location:
 2776:             self.right_view["place"].setText(compact_location(change.target_location))
 2777:         self._scroll_to_change(change)
 2778: 
 2779:     def _scroll_to_change(self, change: Change) -> None:
 2780:         if self.result is None:
 2781:             return
 2782:         if change.source_location and change.source_location.line is not None:
 2783:             self._scroll_view_to_line(
 2784:                 self.left_view["text"],
 2785:                 change.source_location.line,
 2786:                 self._line_count(Path(self.result.left_path)),
 2787:             )
 2788:         if change.target_location and change.target_location.line is not None:
 2789:             self._scroll_view_to_line(
 2790:                 self.right_view["text"],
 2791:                 change.target_location.line,
 2792:                 self._line_count(Path(self.result.right_path)),
 2793:             )
 2794: 
 2795:     @staticmethod
 2796:     def _scroll_view_to_line(view: QTextEdit, line: int, total_lines: int) -> None:
 2797:         bar = view.verticalScrollBar()
 2798:         if bar.maximum() <= 0:
 2799:             return
 2800:         ratio = max(0, min(total_lines - 1, line - 1)) / max(total_lines - 1, 1)
 2801:         bar.setValue(round(bar.maximum() * ratio))
 2802: 
 2803:     @staticmethod
 2804:     def _line_count(path: Path) -> int:
 2805:         for encoding in ("utf-8-sig", "utf-8", "cp1251", "latin-1"):
 2806:             try:
 2807:                 return max(1, len(path.read_text(encoding=encoding).splitlines()))
 2808:             except UnicodeDecodeError:
 2809:                 continue
 2810:             except OSError:
 2811:                 return 1
 2812:         try:
 2813:             return max(1, len(path.read_text(errors="replace").splitlines()))
 2814:         except OSError:
 2815:             return 1
 2816: 
 2817:     def _move_selection(self, delta: int) -> None:
 2818:         count = self.changes_list.count()
 2819:         if count == 0:
 2820:             return
 2821:         row = self.changes_list.currentRow()
 2822:         self.changes_list.setCurrentRow(max(0, min(count - 1, row + delta)))
 2823: 
 2824:     def _export_report(self) -> None:
 2825:         if self.result is None:
 2826:             self._show_message(QMessageBox.Icon.Information, "Нет отчета", "Сначала выполните сравнение.")
 2827:             return
 2828:         path, _ = QFileDialog.getSaveFileName(self, "Сохранить отчет", "comparison-report.html", "HTML (*.html)")
 2829:         if not path:
 2830:             return
 2831:         Path(path).write_text(render_html_report(self.result), encoding="utf-8")
 2832:         self.status_text.setText(f"Отчет сохранен: {path}")
 2833:

 2846:         if value == template_key:

 2848:     return "Без шаблона"

 2851: def _review_status_text(status: str) -> str:
 2852:     for value, label in REVIEW_STATUSES:

 2858: def _apply_registry_status_style(item: QTableWidgetItem, status: str) -> None:
 2859:     colors = {
 2860:         "ok": ("#087443", "#ecfdf3"),
 2861:         "changed": ("#b54708", "#fffaeb"),
 2862:         "missing": ("#b42318", "#fff1f0"),
 2863:         "error": ("#b42318", "#fff1f0"),
 2864:     }
 2865:     foreground, background = colors.get(status, ("#667085", "#f7f9fc"))
 2866:     item.setForeground(QBrush(QColor(foreground)))
 2867:     item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(background)))
 2868: 
 2869: 
 2870: def _snapshot_display_name(snapshot_path: str) -> str:
 2871:     name = Path(snapshot_path).name
 2872:     match = re.match(r"^v\d{4}_(.+)$", name)
 2873:     return match.group(1) if match else name
 2874: 
 2875: 
 2876: def _format_registry_datetime(value: str) -> str:
 2877:     if not value:
 2878:         return "-"
 2879:     try:
 2880:         parsed = datetime.fromisoformat(value)
 2881:     except ValueError:
 2882:         return value
 2883:     if parsed.tzinfo is not None:
 2884:         parsed = parsed.astimezone()
 2885:     return parsed.strftime("%d.%m.%Y %H:%M")
 2886: 
 2887: 
 2888: _GROUPED_REMOVED_RE = re.compile(r"\bудал\w*\s*\((\d+)\)", re.IGNORECASE)
 2889: _GROUPED_ADDED_RE = re.compile(r"\bдобав\w*\s*\((\d+)\)", re.IGNORECASE)
 2890: 
 2891: 
 2892: def _removed_metric_count(change: Change) -> int:
 2893:     grouped_count = _grouped_metric_count(_GROUPED_REMOVED_RE, change.before)
 2894:     if grouped_count:
 2895:         return grouped_count
 2896:     return 1 if change.change_type == "removed" else 0
 2897: 
 2898: 
 2899: def _added_metric_count(change: Change) -> int:
 2900:     grouped_count = _grouped_metric_count(_GROUPED_ADDED_RE, change.after)
 2901:     if grouped_count:
 2902:         return grouped_count
 2903:     return 1 if change.change_type == "added" else 0
 2904: 
 2905: 
 2906: def _grouped_metric_count(pattern: re.Pattern[str], value: str) -> int:
 2907:     match = pattern.search(value)
 2908:     return int(match.group(1)) if match else 0
 2909: 
 2910: 
 2911: def _html_page(body: str) -> str:
 2912:     return f"""
 2913:     <html>
 2914:     <head>
 2915:     <style>
 2916:         body {{
 2917:             font-family: Segoe UI, Arial;
 2918:             color: #111827;
 2919:             background: #ffffff;
 2920:             font-size: 12px;
 2921:         }}
 2922:         h2 {{
 2923:             margin: 0 0 10px 0;
 2924:             font-size: 18px;
 2925:             font-weight: 800;
 2926:             color: #111827;
 2927:         }}
 2928:         .hint {{
 2929:             color: #667085;
 2930:             margin: 4px 0 12px 0;
 2931:         }}
 2932:         .summary-grid {{
 2933:             margin: 8px 0 12px 0;
 2934:         }}
 2935:         .summary-grid div {{
 2936:             display: inline-block;
 2937:             min-width: 118px;
 2938:             margin: 0 8px 8px 0;

   11: 
   12: 
   13: class TkMainWindow:
   14:     def __init__(self, root: tk.Tk) -> None:
   15:         self.root = root
   16:         self.left_path: Path | None = None
   17:         self.right_path: Path | None = None
   18:         self.result: ComparisonResult | None = None
   19:         self.root.title("Сравнение файлов")
   20:         self.root.geometry("1320x820")
   21:         self._configure_style()
   22:         self._build()
   23: 
   24:     def _configure_style(self) -> None:
   25:         style = ttk.Style()
   26:         style.theme_use("clam")
   27:         style.configure("Root.TFrame", background="#eef2f6")
   28:         style.configure("Panel.TFrame", background="#ffffff", relief="flat")
   29:         style.configure("Title.TLabel", background="#eef2f6", foreground="#111827", font=("Segoe UI", 18, "bold"))
   30:         style.configure("Credit.TLabel", background="#ffffff", foreground="#8b95a7", font=("Segoe UI", 8, "bold"))
   31:         style.configure("Mode.TLabel", background="#ecfdf8", foreground="#0f766e", font=("Segoe UI", 10, "bold"))
   32:         style.configure("Primary.TButton", background="#2563eb", foreground="#ffffff", font=("Segoe UI", 10, "bold"))
   33:         style.configure("TButton", font=("Segoe UI", 10, "bold"))
   34: 
   35:     def _build(self) -> None:
   36:         outer = ttk.Frame(self.root, style="Root.TFrame", padding=14)
   37:         outer.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
   38: 
   39:         header = ttk.Frame(outer, style="Root.TFrame")
   40:         header.pack(fill=tk.X)
   41:         ttk.Label(header, text="СФ  Сравнение файлов  2026", style="Title.TLabel").pack(side=tk.LEFT)
   42:         ttk.Label(header, text="  Строгий локальный режим  ", style="Mode.TLabel").pack(side=tk.RIGHT)
   43: 
   44:         actions = ttk.Frame(outer, style="Root.TFrame")
   45:         actions.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(12, 10))
   46:         self.left_button = ttk.Button(actions, text="Файл 1", command=self._choose_left)
   47:         self.right_button = ttk.Button(actions, text="Файл 2", command=self._choose_right)
   48:         self.compare_button = ttk.Button(actions, text="Сравнить", style="Primary.TButton", command=self._compare)
   49:         self.export_button = ttk.Button(actions, text="Экспорт отчета", command=self._export_report)
   50:         for button in (self.left_button, self.right_button, self.compare_button, self.export_button):
   51:             button.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=(0, 8))
   52: 
   53:         body = ttk.PanedWindow(outer, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL)
   54:         body.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
   55: 
   56:         viewers = ttk.PanedWindow(body, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL)
   57:         left_panel = self._text_panel(viewers, "Было")
   58:         right_panel = self._text_panel(viewers, "Стало")
   59:         viewers.add(left_panel[0], weight=1)
   60:         viewers.add(right_panel[0], weight=1)
   61:         self.left_view = left_panel[1]
   62:         self.right_view = right_panel[1]
   63: 
   64:         side = ttk.Frame(body, style="Panel.TFrame", padding=(10, 0, 0, 0))
   65:         self.summary = ttk.Label(side, text="Найдено 0 изменений", background="#ffffff", foreground="#111827", font=("Segoe UI", 14, "bold"))
   66:         self.summary.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(0, 8))
   67:         self.changes_list = tk.Listbox(side, borderwidth=1, relief=tk.SOLID, activestyle="dotbox", font=("Segoe UI", 10))
   68:         self.changes_list.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
   69:         self.changes_list.bind("<<ListboxSelect>>", self._show_selected_change)
   70: 
   71:         body.add(viewers, weight=4)
   72:         body.add(side, weight=1)
   73: 
   74:         footer = ttk.Frame(outer, style="Panel.TFrame", padding=(10, 7))
   75:         footer.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(10, 0))
   76:         self.status = ttk.Label(footer, text="Готово", background="#ffffff", foreground="#0f766e", font=("Segoe UI", 9, "bold"))
   77:         self.status.pack(side=tk.LEFT)
   78:         ttk.Label(footer, text="Разработал: Абдрахманов Амаль Даулетович", style="Credit.TLabel").pack(side=tk.RIGHT)
   79: 
   80:     def _text_panel(self, parent: ttk.PanedWindow, title: str) -> tuple[ttk.Frame, tk.Text]:
   81:         frame = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Panel.TFrame", padding=8)
   82:         ttk.Label(frame, text=title, background="#ffffff", foreground="#667085", font=("Segoe UI", 10, "bold")).pack(anchor=tk.W)
   83:         text = tk.Text(frame, wrap=tk.NONE, borderwidth=1, relief=tk.SOLID, font=("Consolas", 10), background="#ffffff")
   84:         text.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=(6, 0))
   85:         text.configure(state=tk.DISABLED)
   86:         return frame, text
   87: 
   88:     def _choose_left(self) -> None:
   89:         path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title="Выберите исходный файл")
   90:         if path:
   91:             self.left_path = Path(path)
   92:             self.left_button.configure(text=self.left_path.name)
   93: 
   94:     def _choose_right(self) -> None:
   95:         path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title="Выберите измененный файл")
   96:         if path:
   97:             self.right_path = Path(path)
   98:             self.right_button.configure(text=self.right_path.name)
   99: 
  100:     def _compare(self) -> None:
  101:         if self.left_path is None or self.right_path is None:
  102:             messagebox.showwarning("Не выбраны файлы", "Выберите два файла для сравнения.")
  103:             return
  104:         try:
  105:             self.result = compare_files(self.left_path, self.right_path)
  106:         except AnalyzerDependencyError as exc:
  107:             messagebox.showwarning("Не хватает зависимости", str(exc))
  108:             return
  109:         except Exception as exc:
  110:             messagebox.showerror("Ошибка сравнения", f"Не удалось сравнить файлы: {exc.__class__.__name__}")
  111:             return
  112:         self._render_result(self.result)
  113: 
  114:     def _render_result(self, result: ComparisonResult) -> None:
  115:         self.summary.configure(text=f"Найдено {result.change_count} изменений")
  116:         self.changes_list.delete(0, tk.END)
  117:         for change in result.changes:
  118:             place = change.target_location.display() if change.target_location else ""
  119:             self.changes_list.insert(tk.END, f"{change.change_type}: {place}")
  120:         if result.changes:
  121:             self.changes_list.selection_set(0)
  122:             self._show_change(0)
  123:         else:
  124:             self._set_text(self.left_view, "Изменений не найдено")
  125:             self._set_text(self.right_view, "Изменений не найдено")
  126:         self.status.configure(text="Сравнение выполнено локально")
  127: 
  128:     def _show_selected_change(self, _event: tk.Event[tk.Listbox]) -> None:
  129:         selection = self.changes_list.curselection()
  130:         if selection:
  131:             self._show_change(selection[0])
  132: 
  133:     def _show_change(self, row: int) -> None:
  134:         if self.result is None or row < 0 or row >= len(self.result.changes):
  135:             return
  136:         change = self.result.changes[row]
  137:         self._set_text(self.left_view, change.before)
  138:         self._set_text(self.right_view, change.after)
  139: 
  140:     def _set_text(self, widget: tk.Text, value: str) -> None:
  141:         widget.configure(state=tk.NORMAL)
  142:         widget.delete("1.0", tk.END)
  143:         widget.insert("1.0", value)
  144:         widget.configure(state=tk.DISABLED)
  145: 
  146:     def _export_report(self) -> None:
  147:         if self.result is None:
  148:             messagebox.showinfo("Нет отчета", "Сначала выполните сравнение.")
  149:             return
  150:         path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(title="Сохранить отчет", defaultextension=".html", filetypes=[("HTML", "*.html")])
  151:         if not path:
  152:             return
  153:         Path(path).write_text(render_html_report(self.result), encoding="utf-8")
  154:         self.status.configure(text=f"Отчет сохранен: {path}")
  155: 
  156: 
  157: def run_tk_app() -> int:
  158:     root = tk.Tk()
  159:     TkMainWindow(root)
  160:     root.mainloop()
  161:     return 0

Файл: tests\test_compare_worker.py
Комментарий: Автоматический тест, фиксирующий ожидаемое поведение.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: import sys
    2: from pathlib import Path
    3: 
    4: from PySide6.QtWidgets import QApplication
    5: 
    6: from file_compare_app.core.models import ComparisonResult
    7: from file_compare_app.ui.compare_worker import CompareWorker
    8: 
    9: 
   10: def _app() -> QApplication:
   11:     return QApplication.instance() or QApplication(sys.argv)
   12: 
   13: 
   14: def test_compare_worker_emits_progress_and_result(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   15:     _app()
   16:     left = tmp_path / "old.txt"
   17:     right = tmp_path / "new.txt"
   18:     left.write_text("old", encoding="utf-8")
   19:     right.write_text("new", encoding="utf-8")
   20:     result = ComparisonResult(str(left), str(right), "text")
   21: 
   22:     def fake_compare(left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   23:         assert left_path == left
   24:         assert right_path == right
   25:         return result
   26: 
   27:     worker = CompareWorker(left, right, compare_func=fake_compare)
   28:     progress: list[tuple[int, str]] = []
   29:     finished: list[ComparisonResult] = []
   30:     worker.progress.connect(lambda value, message: progress.append((value, message)))
   31:     worker.finished.connect(finished.append)
   32: 
   33:     worker.run()
   34: 
   35:     assert [value for value, _message in progress] == [10, 70, 100]
   36:     assert finished == [result]
   37: 
   38: 
   39: def test_compare_worker_can_be_canceled_before_compare(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   40:     _app()
   41:     left = tmp_path / "old.txt"
   42:     right = tmp_path / "new.txt"
   43:     left.write_text("old", encoding="utf-8")
   44:     right.write_text("new", encoding="utf-8")
   45:     calls: list[str] = []
   46: 
   47:     def fake_compare(left_path: Path, right_path: Path) -> ComparisonResult:
   48:         calls.append("called")
   49:         return ComparisonResult(str(left_path), str(right_path), "text")
   50: 
   51:     worker = CompareWorker(left, right, compare_func=fake_compare)
   52:     canceled: list[bool] = []
   53:     worker.canceled.connect(lambda: canceled.append(True))
   54: 
   55:     worker.cancel()
   56:     worker.run()
   57: 
   58:     assert calls == []
   59:     assert canceled == [True]

   31: 
   32: 
   33: def test_html_report_uses_modern_summary_and_compact_locations() -> None:

Файл: tests\test_klp_analyzer.py
Комментарий: Автоматический тест, фиксирующий ожидаемое поведение.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: import zlib
    3: 
    4: from file_compare_app.analyzers.klp import KasperskyKlpAnalyzer, extract_klp_profile_lines
    5: from file_compare_app.core.orchestrator import compare_files
    6: 
    7: 
    8: def _raw_deflate(payload: bytes) -> bytes:
    9:     compressor = zlib.compressobj(level=9, wbits=-zlib.MAX_WBITS)
   10:     return compressor.compress(payload) + compressor.flush()
   11: 
   12: 
   13: def _write_klp(path: Path, section_hash: str) -> None:
   14:     visible = (
   15:         ".core\0"
   16:         "AntiCryptor\0"
   17:         "hash\0"
   18:         f"{section_hash}\0"
   19:         "2.5.0.0\0"
   20:     ).encode("utf-16le")
   21:     compressed = "KLPOL_ACCEPT_PARENT\0KLPRSS_Mnd\0".encode("utf-16le")
   22:     path.write_bytes(
   23:         b"\x08\x00\x00\x00kscpolfmn\x01\x00\x00"
   24:         + b"ZLIB"
   25:         + _raw_deflate(b"<!--KLPARBIN -->" + compressed)
   26:         + b"<!--KLPARBIN -->"
   27:         + visible
   28:     )
   29: 
   30: 
   31: def test_kaspersky_klp_profile_lines_extract_policy_metadata(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   32:     policy = tmp_path / "policy.klp"
   33:     _write_klp(policy, "hash-old")
   34: 
   35:     lines = extract_klp_profile_lines(policy)
   36: 
   37:     assert "format: Kaspersky KLP policy" in lines
   38:     assert "magic: kscpolfmn" in lines
   39:     assert "klparbin_marker: yes" in lines
   40:     assert "zlib_blocks: 1" in lines
   41:     assert "section: AntiCryptor" in lines
   42:     assert "value: hash-old" in lines
   43:     assert "value: KLPOL_ACCEPT_PARENT" in lines
   44: 
   45: 
   46: def test_klp_analyzer_reports_changed_kaspersky_section_hash(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   47:     old = tmp_path / "old.klp"
   48:     new = tmp_path / "new.klp"
   49:     _write_klp(old, "hash-old")
   50:     _write_klp(new, "hash-new")
   51: 
   52:     result = KasperskyKlpAnalyzer().compare(old, new)
   53: 
   54:     assert result.file_kind == "klp"
   55:     assert any("hash-old" in change.before and "hash-new" in change.after for change in result.changes)
   56:     assert any(change.notes == "KLP values" for change in result.changes)
   57: 
   58: 
   59: def test_klp_analyzer_groups_large_profile_differences(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   60:     old = tmp_path / "old.klp"
   61:     new = tmp_path / "new.klp"
   62:     old.write_text("\n".join(f"section: OldSection{i}" for i in range(80)), encoding="utf-8")
   63:     new.write_text("\n".join(f"section: NewSection{i}" for i in range(25)), encoding="utf-8")
   64: 
   65:     result = KasperskyKlpAnalyzer().compare(old, new)
   66: 
   67:     assert result.file_kind == "klp"
   68:     assert len(result.changes) <= 3
   69:     assert any(change.notes == "KLP values" for change in result.changes)
   70:     assert "еще" in result.changes[0].before
   71: 
   72: 
   73: def test_klp_analyzer_keeps_group_summary_short(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   74:     old = tmp_path / "old.klp"
   75:     new = tmp_path / "new.klp"
   76:     old.write_text(
   77:         "\n".join(f"section: OldVeryLongSectionNameWithManyPartsAndSuffix{i}" for i in range(40)),
   78:         encoding="utf-8",
   79:     )
   80:     new.write_text(
   81:         "\n".join(f"section: NewVeryLongSectionNameWithManyPartsAndSuffix{i}" for i in range(40)),
   82:         encoding="utf-8",
   83:     )
   84: 
   85:     result = KasperskyKlpAnalyzer().compare(old, new)
   86: 
   87:     assert result.changes
   88:     assert all(len(change.before) <= 180 for change in result.changes if change.before)
   89:     assert all(len(change.after) <= 180 for change in result.changes if change.after)
   90: 
   91: 
   92: def test_orchestrator_uses_klp_analyzer_for_kaspersky_policy(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   93:     old = tmp_path / "old.klp"
   94:     new = tmp_path / "new.klp"
   95:     _write_klp(old, "hash-old")
   96:     _write_klp(new, "hash-new")
   97: 
   98:     result = compare_files(old, new)
   99: 
  100:     assert result.file_kind == "klp"
  101:     assert result.changes

    6: def test_xlsx_analyzer_reports_changed_cell(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
    7:     pytest.importorskip("openpyxl")

    9: 
   10:     from file_compare_app.analyzers.xlsx import XlsxAnalyzer
   11: 
   12:     old = tmp_path / "old.xlsx"

   30: def test_image_analyzer_reports_changed_region(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   31:     pytest.importorskip("PIL")
   32:     from PIL import Image
   33: 
   34:     from file_compare_app.analyzers.image import ImageAnalyzer
   35: 
   36:     old = tmp_path / "old.png"
   37:     new = tmp_path / "new.png"
   38:     Image.new("RGB", (4, 4), "white").save(old)
   39:     image = Image.new("RGB", (4, 4), "white")
   40:     image.putpixel((2, 1), (0, 0, 0))
   41:     image.save(new)
   42: 
   43:     result = ImageAnalyzer().compare(old, new)
   44: 
   45:     assert result.file_kind == "image"
   46:     assert result.change_count == 1
   47:     assert result.changes[0].target_location.x == 2
   48:     assert result.changes[0].target_location.y == 1

    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.core.orchestrator import compare_files
    4: 
    5: 
    6: def test_orchestrator_uses_text_analyzer(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
    7:     old = tmp_path / "old.txt"
    8:     new = tmp_path / "new.txt"
    9:     old.write_text("a\nb\n", encoding="utf-8")
   10:     new.write_text("a\nc\n", encoding="utf-8")
   11: 
   12:     result = compare_files(old, new)
   13: 
   14:     assert result.file_kind == "text"
   15:     assert result.change_count == 1
   16:     assert result.changes[0].before == "b"
   17:     assert result.changes[0].after == "c"
   18: 
   19: 
   20: def test_orchestrator_uses_binary_fallback(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   21:     old = tmp_path / "old.unknown"
   22:     new = tmp_path / "new.unknown"
   23:     old.write_bytes(b"a")
   24:     new.write_bytes(b"b")
   25: 
   26:     result = compare_files(old, new)
   27: 
   28:     assert result.file_kind == "binary"

    7: def test_file_sha256_changes_when_file_changes(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
    8:     file_path = tmp_path / "controller.yaml"
    9:     file_path.write_text("timeout: 30", encoding="utf-8")
   10:     first = file_sha256(file_path)
   11:

   13:     second = file_sha256(file_path)
   14: 
   15:     assert first != second

   18: def test_monitor_adds_baseline_version_and_detects_unchanged_file(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   19:     repository = RegistryRepository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
   20:     node = repository.create_node("Линия упаковки")
   21:     file_path = tmp_path / "controller.yaml"
   22:     file_path.write_text("timeout: 30", encoding="utf-8")
   23:     monitor = RegistryMonitor(repository)
   24: 
   25:     watched = monitor.add_file(node.id, file_path)
   26:     checked = monitor.check_file(watched.id)
   27: 
   28:     assert checked.status == "ok"

   30:     assert [event.event_type for event in repository.list_events(node.id)] == ["checked", "baseline"]

   33: def test_monitor_detects_changed_file_by_comparing_previous_version(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   34:     repository = RegistryRepository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
   35:     node = repository.create_node("Линия упаковки")
   36:     file_path = tmp_path / "controller.yaml"
   37:     file_path.write_text("timeout: 30", encoding="utf-8")
   38:     monitor = RegistryMonitor(repository)
   39:     watched = monitor.add_file(node.id, file_path)
   40: 
   41:     file_path.write_text("timeout: 45", encoding="utf-8")
   42:     changed = monitor.check_file(watched.id)
   43:     versions = repository.list_file_versions(watched.id)
   44:     event = repository.list_events(node.id)[0]
   45: 
   46:     assert changed.status == "changed"
   47:     assert [version.version_number for version in versions] == [1, 2]
   48:     assert versions[0].sha256 != versions[1].sha256
   49:     assert event.event_type == "changed"
   50:     assert event.change_count > 0
   51:     assert "v1 -> v2" in event.message
   52:     assert "timeout: 30" in event.message
   53:     assert "timeout: 45" in event.message

   56: def test_monitor_adds_before_after_pair_as_single_logical_file(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   57:     repository = RegistryRepository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
   58:     node = repository.create_node("Object")
   59:     before = tmp_path / "UPN1 ARM DeltaV.klp"
   60:     after = tmp_path / "UPN1 ARM DeltaV - after.klp"
   61:     before.write_text("hash=old", encoding="utf-8")
   62:     after.write_text("hash=new", encoding="utf-8")
   63:     monitor = RegistryMonitor(repository)
   64: 
   65:     watched = monitor.add_file_pair(node.id, before, after, label="UPN1 ARM DeltaV.klp")
   66: 
   67:     watched_files = repository.list_watched_files(node.id)
   68:     versions = repository.list_file_versions(watched.id)
   69:     event = repository.list_events(node.id)[0]
   70:     assert len(watched_files) == 1
   71:     assert watched_files[0].id == watched.id
   72:     assert watched_files[0].file_path == str(after)
   73:     assert watched_files[0].status == "changed"
   74:     assert [version.version_number for version in versions] == [1, 2]
   75:     assert "v1 -> v2" in event.message
   76:     assert "hash=old" in event.message
   77:     assert "hash=new" in event.message

   80: def test_monitor_adds_next_after_version_from_previous_after(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   81:     repository = RegistryRepository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
   82:     node = repository.create_node("Object")
   83:     before = tmp_path / "policy.klp"
   84:     after = tmp_path / "policy-after.klp"
   85:     next_after = tmp_path / "policy-after-2.klp"
   86:     before.write_text("hash=old", encoding="utf-8")
   87:     after.write_text("hash=new", encoding="utf-8")
   88:     next_after.write_text("hash=latest", encoding="utf-8")
   89:     monitor = RegistryMonitor(repository)
   90:     watched = monitor.add_file_pair(node.id, before, after)
   91: 
   92:     updated = monitor.add_next_version(watched.id, next_after)
   93: 
   94:     versions = repository.list_file_versions(watched.id)
   95:     event = repository.list_events(node.id)[0]
   96:     assert updated.file_path == str(next_after)
   97:     assert [version.version_number for version in versions] == [1, 2, 3]
   98:     assert "v2 -> v3" in event.message
   99:     assert "hash=new" in event.message
  100:     assert "hash=latest" in event.message
  101:

  103: def test_monitor_detects_missing_file_without_losing_previous_version(tmp_path: Path) -> None:

  140: def test_registry_monitor_records_risk_count_for_dangerous_config_change(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
  141:     repository = RegistryRepository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
  142:     monitor = RegistryMonitor(repository)
  143:     node = repository.create_node("Firewall")

  151:     event = repository.get_last_event_for_watched_file(watched.id)
  152:     assert event is not None
  153:     assert event.risk_count == 1
  154:     assert "access-list" in event.risk_summary

  260:     repository = RegistryRepository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
  261: 
  262:     node = repository.create_node(
  263:         name="Kaspersky ARM",
  264:         template_key="kaspersky",
  265:         monitor_interval_minutes=120,
  266:     )
  267:     updated = repository.update_node(
  268:         node.id,
  269:         template_key="cisco_asa",
  270:         monitoring_enabled=False,
  271:         monitor_interval_minutes=240,
  272:     )
  273: 
  274:     assert node.template_key == "kaspersky"
  275:     assert node.monitor_interval_minutes == 120
  276:     assert updated.template_key == "cisco_asa"
  277:     assert updated.monitoring_enabled is False
  278:     assert updated.monitor_interval_minutes == 240
  279: 
  280: 
  281: def test_repository_upserts_comparison_review_for_version_pair(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
  282:     repository = RegistryRepository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
  283:     node = repository.create_node(name="Object")
  284:     watched = repository.create_watched_file(
  285:         node_id=node.id,
  286:         file_path=str(tmp_path / "running.cfg"),
  287:         label="running.cfg",
  288:         file_kind="cfg",
  289:         baseline_hash="old",
  290:         last_hash="new",
  291:         status="changed",
  292:     )
  293: 
  294:     review = repository.upsert_comparison_review(
  295:         watched_file_id=watched.id,
  296:         from_version=1,
  297:         to_version=2,
  298:         status="approved",
  299:         reviewer="Amal",
  300:         comment="Согласовано после проверки",
  301:     )
  302:     updated = repository.upsert_comparison_review(
  303:         watched_file_id=watched.id,
  304:         from_version=1,
  305:         to_version=2,
  306:         status="rejected",
  307:         reviewer="Engineer",
  308:         comment="Нужно уточнение",
  309:     )
  310: 
  311:     assert review.status == "approved"
  312:     assert updated.id == review.id
  313:     assert updated.status == "rejected"
  314:     assert updated.reviewer == "Engineer"
  315:     assert repository.get_comparison_review(watched.id, 1, 2).comment == "Нужно уточнение"

  277:     app = QApplication.instance() or QApplication(sys.argv)
  278:     window = MainWindow()

  311: def test_main_window_single_file_button_adds_baseline_then_after_versions(tmp_path) -> None:
  312:     app = QApplication.instance() or QApplication(sys.argv)
  313:     window = MainWindow()
  314:     window.registry_repository = window.registry_repository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
  315:     window.registry_monitor = window.registry_monitor.__class__(window.registry_repository)
  316:     node = window.create_registry_node("Object")

  318:     after = tmp_path / "policy-new.klp"
  319:     next_after = tmp_path / "policy-new-2.klp"
  320:     before.write_text("hash=old", encoding="utf-8")
  321:     after.write_text("hash=new", encoding="utf-8")

  337:     assert window.registry_files_table.item(0, 2).text() == "policy-new.klp"
  338:     assert window.registry_files_table.item(0, 3).text() == "v1 -> v2"
  339:     assert window.registry_files_table.item(1, 0).text() == "2"
  340:     assert window.registry_files_table.item(1, 1).text() == "policy-new.klp"
  341:     assert window.registry_files_table.item(1, 2).text() == "policy-new-2.klp"
  342:     assert window.registry_files_table.item(1, 3).text() == "v2 -> v3"
  343:     assert re.fullmatch(r"\d{2}\.\d{2}\.\d{4} \d{2}:\d{2}", window.registry_files_table.item(1, 5).text())
  344:     assert "v2 -> v3" in window.registry_events_list.item(0).text()
  345:     assert "Версий: 3" in window.registry_versions_panel.toPlainText()
  346:     assert "Сверка v1 -> v2" in window.registry_versions_panel.toPlainText()
  347:     assert "Сверка v2 -> v3" in window.registry_versions_panel.toPlainText()

  579: def test_main_window_deletes_selected_registry_file_from_context(tmp_path) -> None:
  580:     app = QApplication.instance() or QApplication(sys.argv)
  581:     window = MainWindow()

  599: def test_main_window_deletes_selected_registry_node_with_children(tmp_path) -> None:
  600:     app = QApplication.instance() or QApplication(sys.argv)
  601:     window = MainWindow()
  602:     window.registry_repository = window.registry_repository.create(tmp_path / "registry.sqlite3")
  603:     window.registry_monitor = window.registry_monitor.__class__(window.registry_repository)
  604:     root = window.create_registry_node("Root")
  605:     child = window.create_registry_node("Child", parent_id=root.id)
  606:     grandchild = window.create_registry_node("Grandchild", parent_id=child.id)
  607: 
  608:     window.select_registry_node(child.id)
  609:     deleted = window.delete_selected_registry_node()
  610: 
  611:     assert deleted is True
  612:     assert window.selected_registry_node_id == root.id
  613:     assert window.registry_tree.topLevelItemCount() == 1
  614:     assert window.registry_tree.topLevelItem(0).childCount() == 0
  615:     with pytest.raises(KeyError):
  616:         window.registry_repository.get_node(child.id)
  617:     with pytest.raises(KeyError):
  618:         window.registry_repository.get_node(grandchild.id)

    6: def test_strict_workspace_cleans_temp_files(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
    7:     with StrictModeWorkspace(root=tmp_path) as workspace:
    8:         temp_file = workspace.path / "ocr.txt"
    9:         temp_file.write_text("secret document text", encoding="utf-8")
   10:         assert temp_file.exists()
   11:     assert not temp_file.exists()
   12:     assert not workspace.path.exists()
   13:

   16:     message = safe_log_message("pdf", "failed to parse contract text")

    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.analyzers.text_config import TextConfigAnalyzer
    4: 
    5: 
    6: def test_text_diff_reports_modified_and_added_lines(fixtures_dir: Path) -> None:
    7:     result = TextConfigAnalyzer().compare(
    8:         fixtures_dir / "sample_old.txt",
    9:         fixtures_dir / "sample_new.txt",
   10:     )
   11:     assert result.file_kind == "text"
   12:     assert result.change_count == 2
   13:     assert result.changes[0].before == "timeout=30"
   14:     assert result.changes[0].after == "timeout=45"
   15:     assert result.changes[0].source_location.display().endswith(":2")
   16:     assert result.changes[1].change_type == "added"
   17:     assert result.changes[1].after == "mode=strict"
   18: 
   19: 
   20: def test_json_structural_diff_reports_key_path(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   21:     old = tmp_path / "old.json"
   22:     new = tmp_path / "new.json"
   23:     old.write_text('{"database": {"host": "old"}, "timeout": 30}', encoding="utf-8")
   24:     new.write_text('{"database": {"host": "new"}, "timeout": 30}', encoding="utf-8")
   25: 
   26:     result = TextConfigAnalyzer().compare(old, new)
   27: 
   28:     assert result.file_kind == "config"
   29:     assert result.change_count == 1
   30:     assert result.changes[0].before == "old"
   31:     assert result.changes[0].after == "new"
   32:     assert result.changes[0].notes == "database.host"
   33: 
   34: 
   35: def test_cfg_without_ini_sections_falls_back_to_line_diff(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   36:     old = tmp_path / "running-config_before.cfg"
   37:     new = tmp_path / "running-config_after.cfg"
   38:     old.write_text(
   39:         "Cryptochecksum: old\n"
   40:         "interface GigabitEthernet0/1\n"
   41:         " description old uplink\n"
   42:         "!\n",
   43:         encoding="utf-8",
   44:     )
   45:     new.write_text(
   46:         "Cryptochecksum: new\n"
   47:         "interface GigabitEthernet0/1\n"
   48:         " description new uplink\n"
   49:         "!\n",
   50:         encoding="utf-8",
   51:     )
   52: 
   53:     result = TextConfigAnalyzer().compare(old, new)
   54: 
   55:     assert result.file_kind == "config"
   56:     assert result.changes
   57:     assert result.changes[0].format == "text"
   58:     assert result.changes[0].source_location.display().endswith(":3")
   59:     assert "description old uplink" in result.changes[0].before
   60: 
   61: 
   62: def test_cfg_inserted_lines_do_not_turn_shared_config_lines_into_removals(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   63:     old = tmp_path / "old.cfg"
   64:     new = tmp_path / "new.cfg"
   65:     old.write_text(
   66:         "object-group service OPC_PORTS_PERMIT\n"
   67:         " service-object tcp-udp gt 1024 \n"
   68:         " service-object tcp-udp range 135 139 \n"
   69:         " service-object tcp-udp eq 445 \n"
   70:         " service-object tcp-udp eq 12345 \n"
   71:         "access-list acl_outside_in extended permit object-group OPC_PORTS_PERMIT object-group Server\n"
   72:         "pager lines 24\n",
   73:         encoding="utf-8",
   74:     )
   75:     new.write_text(
   76:         "object-group service OPC_PORTS_PERMIT\n"
   77:         " description added letters\n"
   78:         " service-object tcp-udp range 135 139 \n"
   79:         " service-object tcp-udp eq 445 \n"
   80:         " service-object tcp range 1024 4999 \n"
   81:         "access-list acl_outside_in extended permit object-group OPC_PORTS_PERMIT object-group Server log\n"
   82:         "pager lines 24\n",
   83:         encoding="utf-8",
   84:     )
   85: 
   86:     result = TextConfigAnalyzer().compare(old, new)
   87:     changed_text = "\n".join(f"{change.change_type}: {change.before} -> {change.after}" for change in result.changes)
   88: 
   89:     assert "service-object tcp-udp eq 445" not in changed_text
   90:     assert any(change.change_type == "added" and "description added letters" in change.after for change in result.changes)
   91:     assert any(change.change_type == "modified" and " log" in change.after for change in result.changes)

    1: from pathlib import Path
    2: 
    3: from file_compare_app.core.type_detection import detect_file_kind
    4: 
    5: 
    6: def test_detects_known_extensions(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
    7:     cases = {
    8:         "a.txt": "text",
    9:         "a.json": "config",
   10:         "a.yaml": "config",
   11:         "a.yml": "config",
   12:         "a.toml": "config",
   13:         "a.ini": "config",
   14:         "a.env": "config",
   15:         "a.xml": "config",
   16:         "a.docx": "docx",
   17:         "a.pdf": "pdf",
   18:         "a.xlsx": "xlsx",
   19:         "a.png": "image",
   20:         "policy.klp": "klp",
   21:         "Dockerfile": "config",
   22:         ".gitignore": "config",
   23:     }
   24:     for name, expected in cases.items():
   25:         path = tmp_path / name
   26:         path.write_text("sample", encoding="utf-8")
   27:         assert detect_file_kind(path) == expected
   28: 
   29: 
   30: def test_unknown_extension_falls_back_to_binary(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
   31:     path = tmp_path / "archive.binpack"
   32:     path.write_bytes(b"\x00\x01\x02")
   33:     assert detect_file_kind(path) == "binary"
